32b4(phal chen): skye ste/ sems bskyed pa de skyes ma thag nas/ de dang der 'das pa'i grangs su gtogs pa dang / sngon gyi mur gyur pa ji snyed pa de bzhin gshegs pa de dag gi/ mngon par thugs su chud pa/ de dag
32b5(phal chen): tu sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das gang ji snyed mya ngan las 'das pa de dag gi dge ba'i rtsa ba ji lta ba bzhin du byang chub sems dpa' yid ches so/ /de bzhin gshegs pa ma byon pa de dang de'i dus su gtogs
32b6(phal chen): pa'i phyi ma'i mtha'i mur bstan pa dpag tu med pa'i mtha' dang / dbus med par shin tu bstan pa dpag tu med pa dag tu sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das gang ji snyed 'byung bar 'gyur ba de dag gi dge ba'i rtsa
32b7(phal chen): ba la yang byang chub sems dpa' de yid ches so/ /da ltar byung ba'i de bzhin gshegs pa'i sangs rgyas kyi ye shes mtha' dang dbus med par bstan pa/ ma lus par mngon par sangs rgyas pa'i sangs
32b8(phal chen): rgyas bcom ldan 'das de dag gi dge ba'i rtsa ba la yang byang chub sems dpa' de yid ches shing yongs su 'dzin par byed yongs su rgyas par byed/ rab tu 'thob par byed/ khong du chud par byed/ rab tu
33a1(phal chen): rig par byed/ shin tu bsgrub par byed/ rgyud gcig tu gyur par byed/ sangs rgyas thams cad kyang mnyam pa nyid du khong du chud par byed do/ /de ci'i phyir zhe na/ 'di ltar sems bskyed pa de ni de bzhin
33a2(phal chen): gshegs pa thams cad kyi gdung rgyun mi 'chad pa'i phyir skye'o/ /'jig rten gyi khams ma lus pa thams cad rgyas par dgang pa'i phyir skye'o/ /'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du gtogs pa'i sems can
33a3(phal chen): yongs su bsgral ba'i phyir skye'o/ /'jig rten gyi khams thams cad 'du ba dang / 'jig pa yongs su shes par bya ba'i phyir skye'o/ /'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du gtogs pa'i sems can rnams
33a4(phal chen): kyi kun nas nyon mongs pa dang / rnam par byang ba yongs su shes par bya ba'i phyir skye'o/ /'jig rten gyi khams thams cad kyi srid gsum yongs su dag pa yongs su shes par bya ba'i phyir skye'o/ /sems can
33a5(phal chen): thams cad kyi bsam pa dang / bag la nyal ba dang / bag chags thams cad yongs su shes par bya ba'i phyir skye'o/ /sems can thams cad kyi shi 'pho dang / skye ba yongasu shes par bya ba'i phyir skye'o/ /sems
33a6(phal chen): can thams cad kyi dbang po dang / sbyor ba yongs su shes pa bya ba'i phyir skye'o/ /sems can thams cad kyi sems dang spyod pa yongs su shes par bya ba'i phyir skye'o/ /sems can thams cad kyi dus gsum gyi
33a7(phal chen): shes pa yongs su shes par bya ba'i phyir skye ste/ sems bskyed pa des sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das 'das pa dag dang nye bar 'gyur ro/ /sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das ma byon pa dang / da ltar byung ba rnams dang nye bar 'gyur ro/ /
33a8(phal chen): 'das pa'i sangs rgyas kyi byang chub tu nye bar 'gro'o/ /ma byon pa dang / da ltar byung ba'i sangs rgyas kyi byang chub tu nye bar 'gro'o/ /sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das 'das pa rnams kyi chos kyang 'thob par
33b1(phal chen): 'gyur ro/ /sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das ma byon pa rnams kyi chos kyang thob par 'gyur ro/ /sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das da ltar byung ba rnams kyi chos kyang 'thob par 'gyur ro/ /sangs rgyas bcom ldan
33b2(phal chen): 'das 'das pa rnams dang mnyam pa nyid du nye bar 'gro'o/ /sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das ma byon pa dang / da ltar byung ba rnams dang mnyam pa nyid du nye bar 'gro'o/ /sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das 'das pa rnams
33b3(phal chen): kyi ye shes kyi tshogs rnam par dag par 'gyur ro/ /sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das ma byon pa dang / da ltar byung ba rnams kyi ye shes kyi tshogs kyang rnam par dag par 'gyur ro/ /sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das 'das
33b4(phal chen): pa dang / ma byon pa dang / da ltar byung ba'i stobs la thub pa med par yang shin tu bstan par 'gyur ro/ /'das pa dang ma byon pa dang / da ltar byung ba'i sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das dag gi mi brnyengs
33b5(phal chen): pa yongs su dag pa yongs su rdzogs par byed do/ /sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das 'das pa rnams kyi bstan par bya ba'i sangs rgyas kyi chos kyi brgyan mnyam pa nyid kyang rjes su thob bo/ /sangs
33b6(phal chen): rgyas bcom ldan 'das 'das pa dang ma byon pa dang da ltar byung ba rnams kyi bstan par bya ba'i sangs rgyas kyi chos kyi brgyan mnyam pa nyid kyang yongs su rdzogs par byed do/ /nam mkha'i dbyings kyi mthar
33b7(phal chen): thug pa/ chos kyi dbyings mtha' dang dbus med par shin tu bstan pa'i dus gsum mnyam pa nyid thugs su chud pa'i sangs rgyas kyi ye shes kyang rjes su 'thob bo/ /de ci'i phyir zhe na/ de ltar de ni
33b8(phal chen): sangs rgyas su shog shig ces bya ba'i sems bskyed pa des/ 'das pa'i sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams dang nye ba yin/ ma byon pa dang da ltar byung ba'i sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams
34a1(phal chen): dang nye ba yin/ 'das pa dang ma byon pa dang / da ltar byung ba'i sangs rgyas kyi yul rnams dang mnyam pa yin/ 'das pa'i sangs rgyas kyi chos rnams dang mnyam pa yin no/ /ma 'ongs pa dang da ltar
34a2(phal chen): byung ba'i sangs rgyas kyi chos rnams dang mnyam pa yin/ sangs rgyas kyi chos kyi yul thams cad dang mnyam pa yin/ gcig tu nges pa'i lus gcig tu gyur pas kyang dus gsum du mnyam pa'i sangs rgyas
34a3(phal chen): thams cad kyi ye shes dang / 'grogs pa yang thob pa ste/ ye shes de dang 'grogs par 'gyur ba'i sems bskyed pa'i 'byung ba de skyes ma thag tu phyogs bcu na/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyang ched du
34a4(phal chen): brjod pa mdzad do/ /sems bskyed pa de nyid rten du mdzad de/ 'dul ba ji bzhin du chos kyang yang dag par ston/ 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du yang 'dul ba tshad med pa rnams 'byung bar 'gyur/ 'jig
34a5(phal chen): rten gyi khams thams cad du yang rab tu g.yo bar 'gyur/ 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad kyang snang bas rgyas par 'gyur/ 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad kyi ngan song yang rgyun chad par 'gyur/ 'jig rten
34a6(phal chen): gyi khams thams cad kyang yongs su dag par 'gyur/ 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du sangs rgyas 'byung ba yang dag par ston par 'gyur/ sems can thams cad kyang rab tu dga' bar 'gyur/ chos kyis
34a7(phal chen): dbyings thams cad la yang rab tu 'jug par 'gyur/ sangs rgyas kyi rigs thams cad kyang yongs su 'dzin par 'gyur/ sangs rgyas kyi rigs kyi snang ba thams cad kyang rab tu thob par 'gyur te/ dus gsum
34a8(phal chen): du gtogs pa las sems bskyed pa der sangs rgyas sam/ sangs rgyas kyi chos sam/ byang chub sems dpa' 'am/ byang chub sems dpa'i chos sam/ rang sangs rgyas sam/ rang sangs rgyas
34b1(phal chen): kyi chos sam/ nyan thos sam nyan thos kyi chos sam/ 'jig rten pa 'am 'jig rten pa'i chos sam/ 'jig rten las 'das pa 'am/ 'jig rten las 'das pa'i chos sam/ sems can nam
34b2(phal chen): sems can gyi chos kyang rung ste/ ma 'dus pa gang yang med de/ thams cad mkhyen pa nyid ni ma gtogs so/ /de ltar na sems bskyed pa der ni chos kyi dbyings thams cad 'dus so/ /de nas sangs rgyas
34b3(phal chen): kyi mthus/ de'i tshe phyogs bcur 'jig rten gyi khams sangs rgyas kyi zhing gi rdul shin tu phra ba snyed rnam pa drug du g.yos par gyur te/ g.yos so rab tu g.yos so/ /kun tu g.yos so/ /'gul to/
34b4(phal chen): rab tu 'gul to/ /kun tu 'gul to/ /ldeg go rab tu ldeg go/ kun tu ldeg go/ chem chem rab tu chem chem/ kun tu chem chem mo/ /'ur 'ur rab tu 'ur/ kun tu 'ur 'ur ro/ /shig shig kun tu
34b5(phal chen): shig shig go/ /de nas sangs rgyas kyis mthu dang / sems bskyed pa de'i yon tan yang dag par brjod pa'i chos nyid rab tu thob pa'i phyir/ lha rdzas kyi me tog gi char yang mngon par bab bo/ /
34b6(phal chen): lha rdzas kyi spos kyi char yang mngon par bab bo/ /lha rdzas kyi phye ma'i char yang mngon par bab bo/ /lha rdzas kyi phreng ba'i char yang mngon par bab bo/ /lha rdzas kyi gos kyi char yang mngon par bab bo/ /
34b7(phal chen): lha rdzas kyi rin po che'i char yang mngon par bab bo/ /lha rdzas kyi rgyan gyi char yang mngon par bab bo/ /lha rdzas kyi rol mo rnams kyang mngon par sgra 'byin par gyur to/ /lha rdzas kyi snang ba yang rab tu
34b8(phal chen): 'byung ngo / /lha rdzas kyi 'od kyang rab tu byung ngo / /phyogs bcur 'jig rten gyi khams sangs rgyas kyi zhing gi rdul shin tu phra ba snyed 'das pa'i pha rol nas/ de bzhin gshegs pa chos kyi blo gros
35a1(phal chen): su mtshan btags pa/ sangs rgyas kyi zhing gi rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyi zhal mngon par bstan te/ gsung brjod pa chos kyi blo gros legs so/ /legs so/ /phyogs bcu na de bzhin gshegs
35a2(phal chen): pa sangs rgyas kyi zhing gi brdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyi chos bstan pa de la ched du brjod pa mdzad do/ /nged kyis kyang chos bstan pa 'di nyid shin tu rnam par phye ste/ nged kyis ji ltar shin tu rnam par phye ba de bzhin
35a3(phal chen): du sangs rgyas thams cad kyi kyang shin tu rnam par phye'o/ /'di nyid du yang khyod kyis chos bstan pa des byang chub sems dpa' sangs rgyas kyi zhing gi rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyis byang chub tu sems bskyed do/ /de dag
35a4(phal chen): kyang nged kyis lung bstan te/ de dag ni ma 'ongs pa'i dus bskal pa stong phrag brjod du med pa'i mthar thams cad kyang dus gcig tu 'jig rten gyi khams ming tha dad pa dag tu de bzhin gshegs pa mtshan
35a5(phal chen): gcig pa sha stag 'byung bar 'gyur te/ 'di ltar sems rnam par dag pa zhes bya ba sha stag tu 'gyur ro/ /nged kyis chos bstan pa 'di yang ji ltar ma 'ongs pa'i dus na/ ma 'ongs pa'i byang chub sems
35a6(phal chen): dpa' ma thos pa rnams kyis thos par bya ba dang / ji ltar 'jig rten gyi khams mi mjed 'dir sems can rnams kyis shes shing gling bzhi pa 'di'i ri rab kyi rtse mo la ji ltar sems can rnams 'dul bar gyur
35a7(phal chen): pa de bzhin du phyogs bcu'i 'jig rten gyi khams bye ba khrag khrig brgya stong tshad med pa grangs med pa/ bsam gyi mi khyab pa mtshungs pa med pa/ kun tu mtha' yas pa/ dpag tu med pa/ sa mtshams med
35a8(phal chen): pa/ brjod du med pa/ chos kyi dbyings kyis klas pa/ nam mkha'i mthas gtugs pa dag tu yang / sems can rnams 'dul bar bya ba'i phyir byin gyis brlab bo/ /thams cad du yang chos
35b1(phal chen): bstan pa 'di nyid byang chub sems dpa' chos kyi blo gros shes bya ba sha stag / sangs rgyas kyi mthu dang / bcom ldan 'das kyi sngon gyi smon lam gyis sangs rgyas kyi chos thams cad yang dag par bstan
35b2(phal chen): pa dang / ye shes kyi snang ba shin tu gsal bar bya ba dang / don gyis 'dul ba'i snang ba thob pa dang / chos nyid rab tu thob par bya ba dang / byang chub sems dpa' rnams shin tu dga' bar bya ba dang /
35b3(phal chen): sangs rgyas kyi chos kyi rgyud yang dag par bstan par bya ba dang / sangs rgyas kyi chos mnyam pa nyid du bya ba dang / chos kyi dbyings gnyis su med pa la 'jug par bya ba'i phyir rab tu ston to/ /de nas byang
35b4(phal chen): chub sems dpa' chos kyi blo gros kyis phyogs bcur bltas te/ 'khor thams cad la rnam par bltas nas/ nam mkha'i khams rnams la ni rnam par spyad/ sems can gyi khams ni yongs su smin
35b5(phal chen): par byed/ las dang rnam par smin pa'i khams ni 'gal bar mi byed/ nam mkha'i khams ni yongs su dag par byed/ kun nas nyon mongs pa las byung ba ni rab tu sel/ mos pa yangs pa las byung ba ni shin
35b6(phal chen): tu 'phel bar byed/ sems can gyi dbang po tha dad pa la ni rab tu 'jug /dus gsum ni mnyam par byed/ mya ngan las 'das pa'i dbyings la ni yang dag par rtog cing / rang gi dge ba'i rtsa ba stobs yongs
35b7(phal chen): su dag par bya ba la gzhol ba'i phyir/ de'i tshe sangs rgyas kyi mthus tshigs su bcad pa 'di dag smras so/ /gang zhig phyogs rnams bcu po ma lus rgyas byas shing / /sems can zhing dang chos gsum
35b8(phal chen): dag kyang rtogs gyur pa/ /sangs rgyas mtsho mchog byang chub sems dpa' de bzhin te/ /de dag 'jig rten phan phyir sems kyi dam pa bskyed/ /nam mkha'i dbyings kyis klas pa'i chos dbyings ji bzhin dang /
36a1(phal chen): ji ltar sangs rgyas chos rnams 'gro kun rjes song dang / /sangs rgyas thams cad kun tu khyab brnyes ji bzhin gyi/ /'gro ba myi ldog don du phan par rab tu zhugs/ /'jig rten rnams la byams
36a2(phal chen): pas rtag par rab gnas shing / /'tshe ba med par 'gro la phan phyir su zhugs te/ /snang ba mi zad 'od byed gnas su 'gyur ba rnams/ /bsam gyis mi khyab stobs bcu mnga' bas byin gyis brlabs/ /
36a3(phal chen): de ni zhing rnams tha dad ma yin tshul yang rnyed/ /de ni lus kyi rnam pa kun la rab tu zhugs/ /bsod nams ye shes de yangs sangs rgyas byang chub bzhin/ /de ni chags med gzhol ba ye shes rgyur skyes
36a4(phal chen): so/ /spyi'u tshugs rgyu ba'i 'gro ba sna tshogs ma lus par/ /gzhan yang zhing rnams 'jam klas chags myed mthar thugs pa/ /de dag 'phra sbom rgya che yangs pa thams cad du/ /byang chub sems mchog
36a5(phal chen): de ni gcig pu kun tu 'gro/ /brjod du med pa shin tu phra zhing myi gnas pa'i/ /byang chub sems dpa'i spyad pa mchog la rtag zhugs shing / /mkhas pa gang gis sangs rgyas chos mthong myi ngoms pa/ /de dag chos rnams
36a6(phal chen): rgya mtsho'i rnam par chud pa yin/ /'jig rten lam rgyud kun la su zhig snying brtse zhing / /'jig rten gsum po sbyang bar rtag tu zhugs pa rnams/ /phyi ma'i mthar thug sangs rgyas gdung gi rgyun mi gcod/ /
36a7(phal chen): de ni bdud kyi khyim yang rab tu 'joms pa yin/ /dus gsum rgyal ba rnams dang rgyud gcig dngos gyur cing / /shin tu phra ba'i tshul gyis lam la rtag brtson te/ /su zhig sangs rgyas yul la dad sems dpa'/
36a8(phal chen): de ni chags med thub pa kun gyis dbang yang bskur/ /rdo rje lta bur sra zhing brtan la mi shigs pa/ /rkang gnyis gtso bos mdzad pa rtag tu dran shes shing / /'dren pa'i spyod yul snang rab shin tu rnyed pa rnams/ /
36b1(phal chen): gzhan gyi dring la myi rgyug byang chub sems kyang skye/ /'gro ba rnams kyi 'du shes rnam par mang shes shing / /de bzhin las dang 'bras bu sems kyi rnams kyang ste/ /gzhan yang dbang po'i mthu dang khams
36b2(phal chen): rnams du ma dag / kun kyang byang chub sems dpa' spyod yul gcig yin no/ /gang zhig chos kyi dbyings bzhin byang chub sems yangs shing / /rtag tu chos la mi gnas nam mkha' ji bzhin pa/ /
36b3(phal chen): chags med sems ldan de dag sangs rgyas ye shes zhugs/ /de dag rtog med chos can yang dag mtha' la gnas/ /sems can bsam pa rnams 'byed sems can 'du shes med/ /chos kyi rnam rtog
36b4(phal chen): khrag khrig pha mthar rab tu phyin/ /de dag rtog la mos shing rnam par myi rtog ste/ /de dag zhing rnams bye ba khrag khrig rjes su zhugs/ /gang zhig sangs rgyas bye ba khrag khrig rjes sems shing / /gang
36b5(phal chen): zhig chos dbyings tshul gyi mdzod du zhugs gyur la/ /gang zhig sems can dbang po'i rnam pa mthar phyin pa/ /de dag sems can gtso bzhin chos nyid shes par byed pa yin/ /lhag pa'i bsam pa
36b6(phal chen): dge dang rtag par mngon ldan zhing / /skyes bu seng ge'i bsnyen bkur phyir ldog myi 'gyur la/ /'jig rten gtso bo mkhas pa mthong bas myi ngoms pa/ /de dag sangs rgyas khrag khrig bye bas byin gyis
36b7(phal chen): brlabs/ /zab mo'i chos rnams rnam par 'byed kyang chags pa myed/ /gnas pa med pas sems kyi dam pa rtag tu dag /de dag bskal pa mtha' yas skyes bu'i seng ge rnams/ /dus gsum
36b8(phal chen): chags pa med par rtogs pa'i yid dang ldan/ /myi 'phrogs thub par mi ldan yid kyi dbang po dang / /gsum pa rjes su song dang rtag tu ldan gyur cig /chos rnams 'byam klas shin tu bslabs pas
37a1(phal chen): rmongs med pa/ /de dag chos dbyings 'gengs kyang nam yang mi ngoms so/ /tshig gi lam 'das ji bzhin mkhas pa zhi ba shes/ /de bzhin nyid la nam yang rnam par myi 'byed pa/ /de dag sangs
37a2(phal chen): rgyas thams cad yul la rjes sems shing / /dus gsum chags pa med par rtogs pa'i yid ldan 'gyur/ /mkhas pa gang zhig sems bskyed 'byam klas chos kyi dbyings/ /'gengs shing phyogs bcu'i
37a3(phal chen): sangs rgyas zhing du 'gro ba ni/ /de dag khrag khrig tshul rnams brjod du med pa yi/ /snang ba brnyed par gnas pa'i rgyal ba'i sras yin no/ /chos rab mu stegs snying rje'i tshul gyi rjes song zhing / /byams pa'i
37a4(phal chen): pha rol phyin pa bar snang ji bzhin te/ /sems can khams la rnams kyang yongs su rtog myed pa/ /de dag rnam rtog med la brtson zhing 'jig rten spyod/ /phyogs bcu dag tu bden pas 'gro ba yid

37a6(phal chen): par gyur pa'i dus kyang de dag rjes su dran/ /de bzhin ma 'ongs dus la 'jug pa rnam par bsgom/ /de dag phyogs bcu'i 'jig rten kun na myi gnas te/ /sems can phan dang sgrol phyir kun tu rnam par
37a7(phal chen): rgyu/ /ye shes 'od mchog dam pas chags pa med gyur la/ /rgyu yi rnam pa chos rab nem nur med brtan rnams/ /de dag the tsom thams cad rnam par ldog pa byed/ /chos kyi dbyings 'dir nem
37a8(phal chen): nur med par rab tu 'jug / gang zhig bdud rnams kun gyi gnas rnams 'joms byed dang / /gang yang sems can rab rib shin tu sel byed dang / /gang rnams rtog pa 'jig cing rnam rtog mi 'grogs pa/
37b1(phal chen): sems can gtso bo de dag yul la the tsom med/ /dus gsum ma lus the tsom rnam par ldog byas shing / /bsam pa'i mchog gis de bzhin gshegs pa'i drung 'gro ste/ /dad pa'i stobs dang ldan zhing

37b6(phal chen): snang byas nas/ /'od zer sgo yi pad mo dag la rgyal sras rnams/ /kun tu bstan te rdul dang bral ba'i chos kyang ston/ /spu gcig rtse la zhing rnams rgyal bas brgyan pa dang / /de bzhin
37b7(phal chen): rgyal ba'i sras kyis brgyan pa mngon par mthong / /'khor rnams blo sems gzhan dang gzhan gcan dpe med pa/ /'gro ba de dag sems shes rmongs med ston pa byed/ /sems 'jug gcig
37b8(phal chen): gis phyogs rnams bcu po thams cad kyi/ /brjod du med pa khrag khrig zhing rnams kun bgrod cing / /song ste sangs rgyas 'gro ba'i don du mchod byas nas/ /bye ba khrag khrig don
38a1(phal chen): dang ldan pa sna tshogs 'dri/ /bder gshegs rnams la phan pa'i 'du shes nyer bzhag cing / /chos kyi gter mkhas rtag tu shes rab rnon po can/ /ye shes 'byung gnas mkhas pas
38a2(phal chen): sangs rgyas chags med phyir/ /'gro ba'i don 'dod byang chub mchog gi spyod pa bsgrub/ /gang rnams chos dbyings rnam par phye zhing bsam byas kyang / /bskal pa mang po 'das byas zad par ma gyur te/ /
38a3(phal chen): chos nyid gnas med gang la'ang chud par ma gyur kyang / /chags med ye shes can rnams skyo sems med par spyod/ /dus gsum rgyal ba'i rigs su rigs dang ldan 'gyur zhing / /bder gshegs kun
38a4(phal chen): gyi sku las yang dag byung gyur pas/ /chos kyi lus can de dag 'gro la gzugs lus can/ /sgyu mkhan mkhas pa yid 'ong sgyu ma ston pa bzhin/ /mkhas pa de dag la lar spyod pa mchog brnyes snang / /
38a5(phal chen): la lar mkhas pa skye zhing mya ngan 'das par snang / /byang chub dam pa'i mchog kyang rnam par 'tshang yang rgya/ /mya ngan 'da' ba ston pa 'ang de bzhin la lar snang / /rang rgyal rnams dang nyan thos rgyal ba'i
38a6(phal chen): sa min pa'i/ /chos nyid de la ji ltar rab tu gnas pa ltos/ /glu dang sgra med bsam med 'du shes ldan pa min/ /'on kyang bya ba sna tshogs du ma nye bar ston/ /'gro bar chos rnams rnam par 'byed cing
38a7(phal chen): skyer 'gyur te/ /'jig rten gtso bo myi bzhugs phyi na rgyal sras rnams/ /chags med mthar phyin pa yi ye shes myi gnas te/ /sangs rgyas byin rlabs rnam par 'phrul pa dag kyang ston/ /
38a8(phal chen): 'jig rten 'di na de dag 'dra ba gang yang med/ /de dag bas kyang 'phags pa'i lta go ci zhig smos/ /thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes yangs pa ma thob par/ /thams cad mkhyen pa'i thabs su
38b1(phal chen): rnam 'phrul mchog kyang thob/ /gang rnams chos rab 'phags par rtag tu 'jug byed pa/ /de dag chos rab mchog gi theg pa yin/ /'jig rten dus dang dus min tshod kyang shes byas shing / /de dag
38b2(phal chen): 'gro la phan phyir rnam par 'phrul pa ston/ /dpa' bo gang rnams zhing kun dag gi lus 'gengs shing / /gang rnams 'jig rten 'od zer dra ba mchog gtong ba/ /mun pa gsal cing snang bas 'jig

38b4(phal chen): cad snying rje chen pos khyab byas nas/ /rang bzhin dag pas thar lam bya ba med par ston/ /gang rnams rgyal ba'i stobs rnams ji bzhin tshad med dang / /gang rnams mkha' ltar 'gro ba kun tu
38b5(phal chen): mtha' yas shing / /gang rnams sems can khams rnams yongs su dgrol brtson pa/ /de dag bskal pa bye bar grangs med spyad pa spyod/ /las mchog bla na med pa shin tu sbyangs pa yis/ /
38b6(phal chen): yon tan dam pa sna tshogs rnams kyang kun sems shing / /byang chub sems dpa' de dag spyod pa mchog myi gtong / /thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes 'byung ba rnam par lta/ /sems 'byung gcig gis
38b7(phal chen): 'jig rten bsam gyis mi khyab pa/ /'byam klas kun tu rgyu zhing 'gro ba rab tu snang / /rtog dang rnam rtog myi byed dag pa'i sems dang ldan/ /de dag gcig min lus la lus gcig ston pa byed/ /
38b8(phal chen): de dag 'jig rten kun la rtogs par mi byed de/ /mgon po kun gyi chos nyid yongs su mi rtog go/ /de dag chos kun rnam 'byed 'dod chags bral gyur pa/ /'gro ba thar par bya ba yongasu
39a1(phal chen): mi stong ngo / /'jig rten kun gyi 'du shes rnam pa gang yod pa/ /bzang ngan 'bring dang de bzhin chung dang sna tshogs kyi/ /'du shes thibs po dag dang rab brgal rnam phye ste/ /de dag byin brlabs
39a2(phal chen): rnam par 'phrul pa shin tu ston/ /ji ltar sgyu ma rnam pa sna tshogs tshad med pa/ /de 'dra'i rnam par 'phrul pas chos dbyings 'di dag 'gengs/ /nam mkha'i dbyings kyi mtha' klas lus kyi bye
39a3(phal chen): brag gis/ /'gro ba rnams kyi mos pa ji bzhin ston pa byed/ /de dag gang la ma chags rtog dang rnam rtog med/ /dag pa med cing nyon mongs de bzhin rlom sems med/ /de dag sangs rgyas chags
39a4(phal chen): pa'i blo med thar la min/ /'gro ba kun la'ang bde ba'i 'du shes rab tu bskyed/ /'jig rten kun na shes la mkhas rab mi 'jigs pa/ /'jig rten 'du shes gnas la 'jug par myi byed de/ /
39a5(phal chen): de dag chos kun 'di la 'du shes gang zhes rtog /de ltar zhugs na dus gsum gang yang dmigs pa med/ /sngon gyi mthar thug pa yi dus la rab zhugs ste/ /phyi ma'i mthar thug ma 'ongs pa
39a6(phal chen): la rab zhugs nas/ /zhing rnams kun na ci yod kun kyang de bzhin du/ /shin tu shes kyang rtag par gang yang myi dmyigs so/ /mya ngan 'das pa'i dbyings la'ang brtson par de bzhin gnas/ /
39a7(phal chen): nyon mongs med pa'i tshul gyi rjes song mi gnas ste/ /de dag yang dag mtha' 'dra de la 'dra ba med/ /byang chub spyod pa las kyang dpa' bo myi zlog go/ gang rnams byang chub bstan pa'i ri rab
39a8(phal chen): bzhin gnas shing / /sangs rgyas rgyal sras mkhas pas chos dbyings thams cad dang / /'gro ba kun tu shin tu gang byas pa/ /'di ni dpa' bo rnams kyi spyod pa'i mchog yin no/ /blo mchog dam
39b1(phal chen): pa gang zhig thams cad mkhyen pa yi/ /rnam grol mdzes pa'i tshul mchog yangs pa 'dod pa ni/ /des ni gang las zag zad srid gsum bde 'byung ba'i/ /byang chub sems la rim pa med par
39b2(phal chen): 'jug par gyis/ /gang gi bsam pa rdul bral byang chub sems gnas pa/ /de dag yon tan legs pa zad par brjod mi nus/ /'on kyang 'gro ba'i don du bde gshegs legs brjod phyir/ /yon
39b3(phal chen): tan ldan pa de yi spyod pa mchog kyang nyon/ /gang gis zhing rnams bye ba khrag khrig rdul byas ste/ /phyogs rnams re re kun tu bkang ste bgrang byas shing / /de yi rjes su dpag pas rnam
39b4(phal chen): 'dren zad byed na/ /'du shes rnams ni mthar thug zad par mi 'gyur ro/ /gang zhig sems can grangs mkhas sems can 'du shes med/ /spyod pa rtsam du gzhol zhing sgra la ma chags dang / /
39b5(phal chen): gang zhig 'jig rten khams 'byed chags pa med pa'i sems/ /de dag ldang dang grangs mkhas grangs dmyigs med pa yin/ /yid kyis nam mkha'i dbyings ni mtha' yas rgya che dang / /
39b6(phal chen): dus rnams 'jig rten kun tu rtogs pa'i mkhas pa gang / /spar mos thal gtor bzhin du the tsom rnams gtor ba/ /de dag sangs rgyas chos rtogs yid can chags pa med/ /gang dag phyogs
39b7(phal chen): rnams mtha' yas zhing la rab 'jug cing / /sems bskyed gcig gis blo nyams med par 'dod byed pa/ /de dag tha dad grangs la rtogs pas der zhugs ste/ /skyo ba med pa'i chos la yang
39b8(phal chen): dag mtha' ltar mkhas/ /gang zhig sangs rgyas bye ba khrag khrig bsam yas pa'i/ /'khor du nye bar phyin te zhab ring 'khor gnas shing / /gtso bo dag la 'dri ba'i thog mar gang 'gro ba/ /spyod yul
40a1(phal chen): mchog can de yi smon lam mchog 'di yin/ /gang zhig phyogs rnams kun gyi mgon po kun 'dra zhing / /chos nyid de la nam yang gnas par ma gyur pa/ /khams gsum dge ba
40a2(phal chen): gang yod kun gyi rgyu yin te/ /de dag zhing rnams thams cad yongs su dag par spyod/ /gang rnams skye ba'i rgyud du srid gsum sna tshogs rnams/ /'jig rten kun na yod la ma chags mig gyur
40a3(phal chen): pa/ /de dag bag chags mkhas shing de bzhin dbang po mkhas/ /mos pa bye ba khrag khrig bsam yas de bzhin mkhas/ /'gro ba'i bsam pa ji bzhin gang gis shes gyur cing / /shes rab
40a4(phal chen): chen po de dag de bzhin chos ston pa/ /de dag kun nas nyon mongs rnams dag tshul la mkhas/ /sems can rnams mang rnam par sbyong ba'i lam ldan ston/ /gang zhig ting 'dzin bye ba khrag
40a5(phal chen): khrig brjod yas rnams/ /sems kyi rgyu ba gcig gis rjes su zhugs gyur pa/ /de dag mtshan ma sna tshogs gnas pa rab tu shes/ /ldang ba'i rgyu la mkhas shing blo gros spyod yul shes/ /chags
40a6(phal chen): myed byang chub de la mngon du gang bzhugs shing / /'gro la phan pa'i don du blo yongs su zhugs pa/ /ye shes 'byam klas 'di dang de dag ldan pa yin/ /de phyir de dag skyes bu mchog gi gsung
40a7(phal chen): yang sgrog / gang zhig skal pa ring dang bskal pa thung mkhas shing / /nyin zhag mkhas shing de bzhin zla byed mkhas/ /gang yang 'jig rten rtag tu skye ba mkhas gyur pa/ /zhing gi rnam pa
40a8(phal chen): mkhas shing rnam phye'i chos med pa'o/ /gang rnams phyogs la zhugs ste phyogs kyi rjes 'brang zhing / /phyogs kun tshad ni rjes su shes par ma gyur pa/ /de dag dbus mas phyogs kyi rjes
40b1(phal chen): su 'gro byed cing / /zhing rnams sbyong yang yongs su dag rtogs chags pa med/ /stobs la 'jug pas rgyal ba rnams kyi stobs shes pa/ /'gro ba rnams kyi gnas dang gnas min bsam byas nas/ /
40b2(phal chen): 'das dang ma 'ongs da ltar byung ba'i las kyi sa/ /yang dag rtogs byas las kyi rnam par smin la gnas/ /'jig rten kun mkhas sna tshogs tha dad de bzhin du/ /srid gsum rnam par rgyu ba'i
40b3(phal chen): tshul yang ci bzhin dang / /dbang po rnon po 'bring dang dbang po tha mar yang / /'gro ba ma lus kun gyi dbang po rnam par 'byed/ /mos pa rnam pa sna tshogs dge dang mi dge dang / /bzang ngan de bzhin 'bring
40b4(phal chen): la rnam par sems byed cing / /'gro ba kun tu 'gro ba bstan pa rnam par byed/ /srid gsum rgyu yi rgyud kyang rab tu shes/ /bsam gtan rnam thar nyon mongs ji bzhin mtshan mthong zhing / /nyon mongs
40b5(phal chen): mtshams sbyor rnam byang ci 'gyur dang / /sngon chad gnas kyi bde dang sdug bsngal rgyud rnams kyang / /bstan pa rnams ni sangs rgyas stobs rnams sbyong bar byed/ /ji ltar 'gro ba'i
40b6(phal chen): lam rgyud nyon mongs las 'jug dang / /'gro rgyud thams cad 'jug cing zhir 'gyur thams cad dang / /zag pa sna tshogs rnams kyang ji ltar skyes 'gyur ba/ /bag chags mtshams sbyor ci bzhin de
40b7(phal chen): bzhin rab tu 'jug / ji ltar 'jig rten nyon mongs zad cing dag gyur pa/ /de la skyes bu khyu mchog spyod pa'i blo dang ldan/ /stobs 'chang dag ni stobs bcu rnams kyi 'od snang ste/ /rgyal ba'i stobs
40b8(phal chen): kyang thob min the tsom yod pa min/ /spu rtse gcig la gang rnams rnam par sems byed cing / /la la nyon mongs la la dog dang yangs pa yi/ /sna tshogs zhing rnams tshad las 'das pa kun mthong nas/
41a1(phal chen): las dang bya ba sna tshogs rgyud du rab tu shes/ /gang rnams rdul gcig rtse la rnam sems brjod med pa'i/ /zhing dang bde gshegs sras rnams sems can gtso mthong yang / /
41a2(phal chen): zhing rnams 'khrugs shing 'dres pa'i nyes pa gang med pa/ /gcig nas 'jug pas rnal 'byor ldan pa kun 'jug la/ /spu gcig rtse la phyogs bcu thams cad rnam phye ste/ /nam mkha'i dbyings
41a3(phal chen): thug 'jig rten khams rnams kun zhugs shing / /phyogs 'ga' tsam yang rgyal bas stong par mthong ba med/ /de bzhin zhing dang 'jig rten 'byam klas de dag sbyong / /de ltar bstan pas rgyal bas stong
41a4(phal chen): min zhing shes nas/ /'jig rten kun kyang spu rtse gcig la yod par 'jug /dus gsum rgyud rnams mtshan nyid tha dad khams kun dang / /nyin zhag dus dang zla phyed rgyud kyi rnam thar 'jug /de ltar rgyal sras
41a5(phal chen): 'jigs med byang chub sems dpa' rnams/ /skyes bu khyu mchog ye shes rgyal srid thob zhugs pa/ /de dag 'di 'dra shes nas rjes su sems byed cing / /bde gshegs rnams la dga' ba mtha' yas
41a6(phal chen): yangs pa 'thob/ /gang rnams bye ba khrag khrig sna tshogs lus bsgyur cing / /phyogs bcu'i rgyal ba thams cad mngon par mchod pa'i phyir/ /rnam 'phrul dam pa bzang po kun tu ston byed pa/ /de dag
41a7(phal chen): mgon po rnams kyi spyod yul rab tu zhugs/ /gang rnams sangs rgyas bye ba khrag khrig drung bslabs shing / /gang rnams chos kyi mdzod rtogs yid la ngoms med de/ /gang dag mgon po khyu mchog
41a8(phal chen): rnams la dga' sems pa/ /de dag chos kyi sprin yin spyod pa mang la spyod/ /ye shes 'phel bar 'gyur ba'i chos kyi gnas mkhas pa/ de dag sangs rgyas 'byung gnas ting 'dzin thob pa yin/ /ri rgyal lta bu
41b1(phal chen): de dag dad pa'i 'byung gnas rten/ /ye shes 'byung gnas 'gro ba'i yon tan 'byung gnas so/ /gnas pa med pa dam pa shin tu yangs pa dang / /thams cad mkhyen la mngon gyur mya ngan med pa dang / /
41b2(phal chen): sems can skyob cing nyon mongs rnyog pa med zhugs pa'i/ /byams pa'i bsam pas 'gro ba kun kyang sems 'gengs shing / /de dag snying rje'i blo yang shin tu yangs pa yin/ /bdag la cir sems de bzhin
41b3(phal chen): sangs rgyas sems can la/ /gzhan du nam mkha' lta bur mtshan nyid med par 'jug /nyams par 'gyur ba'i sems can rnams mthong phyir zhing brtson/ /byang chub sems la mkhas pa dag gi tshad dag ni/ /
41b4(phal chen): bskal pa bye ba'i mthas kyang brjod par mi nus ste/ /ci phyir zhe na de las sangs rgyas thams cad 'byung / /dbang des rim gror byas dang rang rgyal kun kyang 'byung / /phyogs bcu'i zhing rnams grangs
41b5(phal chen): med bcur ni med gyur pa'i/ /sems can thams cad bskal pa gcig la der bgod cing / /bslab pa bcu dang dge bcu bsam gtan 'thob pa dang / /tshangs pa dag dang rnam grol zhi ba'i gnas bkod cing / /
41b6(phal chen): de dag bskal pa bye bar bde bar rab bkod de/ /dgra bcom nyon mongs zhi la rab tu bgod byas kyang / /byang chub sems dpa'i dge ba'i tshogs kyi char myi rung / /byang chub sems dpa' bzhugs ma thag tu tshogs chen
41b7(phal chen): tshogs/ /nyon mongs med cing shin tu phra lam rtogs pa yi/ /rang rgyal sems can bye ba khrag khrig bkod gyur kyang / /bsod nams bsags pa des na byang chub sems rab la/ /grangs dang cha dang bgrang ba'i
41b8(phal chen): rnam par nyer myi 'gro/ /zhing gi rdul ni tshad gyis shes par rung yang srid/ /skad cig sems kyis zhing mang yongs su 'das byas shing / /de ltar bskal pa brjod yas zad par 'gro byas na/ /zhing mtha' thug par
42a1(phal chen): rung srid byang chub sems mchog min/ /mtha' rnams kun tu bskal pa mang po'i mtha' med de/ /sngon gyi mtha' gyur bskal pa de bzhin ma 'ongs dang / /da ltar byung ba'i skal pa zad dang
42a2(phal chen): thub med pa'i/ /bskal pa de dag zad srid byang chub sems ma yin/ /ci phyir zhe na 'di ltar phyogs rnams kun bkang shing / /rtog dang rnam rtog yongs su shes par bya ba'i phyir/ /skad cig
42a3(phal chen): gcig gis dus gsum gtogs par bya don tu/ /'gro ba'i don du 'dod cing sems mchog rin chen skye/ /phyogs bcu'i zhing rnams stong mang kun tu mtha' yas pa'i/ /'gro ba rnams kyi mos pa
42a4(phal chen): bsam pa ci 'dra dang / /sbyor ba gang dang sems dang spyod pa de bzhin te/ /mthar thug rung srid mkha' 'gro'i byang chub sems mtha' min/ /de ni 'di ltar phyogs bcu byams dang snying rje dang / /bsam
42a5(phal chen): pa chen pos 'gro ba thams cad rgyas byas shing / /thar pa'i don du sangs rgyas yon tan kun spyod phyir/ /rin chen sems kyi stobs ni tshad med rab tu skyes/ /mos dang bsam pa yid bzhin
42a6(phal chen): yang dag sbyor ba dang / /'gro ba'i dbang po sbyor bar sems dang spyod pa rnams/ /skad gcig gcig gis ji bzhin rtogs par bya ba'i phyir/ /thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes lta bu'i sems skye'o/ /
42a7(phal chen): 'gro ba'i las dang nyon mongs sna tshogs 'byam klas pa/ /gang gis khams gsum 'di dag tu ni skye 'gyur ba/ /de dag mtha' ni phyogs bcur rnyed par rung srid kyis/ /byang chub sems kyi mchog la kun tu
42a8(phal chen): mtha' med do/ /ci phyir zhe na 'di ltar nyon mongs las grol ba'i/ /sems ni de bzhin gshegs pa mchod pa'i don du skye/ /nyon mongs grol byed de bzhin las kyi rgyud kyang bcom/ /dus gsum mun
42b1(phal chen): pa sel cing mi zad snying rjes byung / /phyogs bcu'i sangs rgyas ma lus thams cad dang / /sems can mang po thams cad sems gcig bskyed pa yis/ /spos dang me tog phreng ba byug pa dam pa dang / /
42b2(phal chen): gdugs dang rgyal mtshan bza' btung na bza' mchod par byed/ /gzhan yang gtan gyi rnam pa 'chag sa dam pa dang / /pho brang mang po sna tshogs tsan dan mchog bsams pa/ /nor bu rin chen rnam
42b3(phal chen): par snang bas brgyan pa dang / /yid bzhin nor bu yid 'ong brgyan pas mchod byas ste/ /de ltar bde gshegs sems can mngon par mchod byed pas/ /bskal pa khrag khrig brjod du med par zad byas kyang / /
42b4(phal chen): byang chub sems dpa'i bde brtsags mthar phyin bde ba nyid/ /gang bsgrub byang chub sems la mnyam par nyer 'gro'o/ /ji snyed dper brjod byas pa 'di dag thams cad kyang / /yang dag skyes pa'i byang
42b5(phal chen): chub sems kyi char mi rung / /de yang 'di ltar dus gsum bzhugs pa'i skyes bu mchog /thams cad byang chub sems mchog de las byung ba yin/ /byang chub sems ni chags pa med pa'i mthar
42b6(phal chen): phyin te/ /thams cad gcig la gnas kyang de la tshad yod min/ /thams cad byang chub sems mchog de las tshad med stobs/ /sems can rang bzhin de bzhin byang chub mthar yang phyin/ /byang chub
42b7(phal chen): sems 'di nam mkha'i mtha' dang mnyam pa ste/ /chos rnams kun la khyab pa'i chos dbyings ci bzhin no/ /tshad med de bzhin nyid kun de'i spyod yul gyur/ /des ni kun tu khyab pa'i sems can gtso
42b8(phal chen): bzhin no/ /de ni 'byam klas chos rnams kun la rjes su zhugs/ /des ni zhing rnams 'byam klas kun tu khyab/ /des ni shes pa 'byams klas thams cad rtogs par chud/ /des ni sangs rgyas
43a1(phal chen): 'byam klas kun dang 'gal med thob/ /rtag tu bsod nams bla na med pa dag dang ldan/ /de bzhin rtag tu tshul khrims rnams dag mi gnas ldan/ /rtag tu kun stong rtag par rab tu dge
43a2(phal chen): ba ste/ /ldog pa med pa'i brtson 'grus mchog dang rab tu ldan/ /bsam gtan mdzod la rtag par bsam gtan 'jug par byed/ /shes rab shin tu yangs pa dang yang rtag tu ldan/ /rgyal sras rnams
43a3(phal chen): kyi sa rab dam pa gang yod pa/ /de dag don du ye shes kun tu bzang po byung / /'gro ba kun na skyes bu ye shes gang bzhugs pa/ /de dag gis ni byang chub sems rab byin gyis brlabs/ /ting nge 'dzin dang
43a4(phal chen): gzungs kyi dam par rab tu brgyan/ /de bzhin gshegs pa'i rnam 'phrul rnam pas rab tu brgyan/ /'jig rten kun dang 'gro ba rnams kyi ji tsam tshad/ /nam mkha'i tshad kyang phyogs bcu dag gi ji
43a5(phal chen): tsam pa/ /de dag bas kyang byang chub sems 'di tshad med de/ /de las skyes bu'i seng ge kun kyang skyes shing byung / /byang chub sems 'di stobs bcu rnams kyi rtsa ba ste/ /brten pa bzhi yi gnas
43a6(phal chen): yin so sor shes pa'i tshe/ /rgyal ba'i chos rnams bcwo brgyad yang dag 'byin pa ste/ /skyes bu'i gtso bos mkhyen par bya ba'i chos kun 'byin/ /gzugs kyi sku ni mtshan rab rnams kyis
43a7(phal chen): bstsags pa dang / /chos sku mnyam nyid rtog pa myi mnga' brnyes pa dang / /'gro bas mchod pa'i ye shes chags med gang byung ba/ /kun gyi rtsa ba 'byung gnas byang chub sems 'di yin/ /rang
43a8(phal chen): rgyal theg pa 'byung zhing nyan thos theg pa'ang 'byung / /bsam gtan ting 'dzin bde ba gzugs kyi khams rnams dang / /gzugs med khams dang ting nge 'dzin gyi bde ba dag /kun gyi rtsa ba
43b1(phal chen): byang chub sems mchog 'di yin no/ /mi dang de bzhin lha yi dbang po bde ba dang / /lam rgyud sna tshogs kun kyang 'di la shin tu sbyangs/ /brtson 'grus stobs dang dbang po'i bde ba gang yod pa/ /kun gyi
43b2(phal chen): rtsa ba dang po byang chub sems 'di yin/ /ci phyir zhe na 'di ltar byang chub sems bskyed cing / /pha rol phyin drug brtson par spyad pa rab tu spyod/ /sems can rnams la'ang spyod pa yang dag rab tu ston/ /des
43b3(phal chen): ni khams gsum 'gro ba'i bde ba kun kyang 'byung / /sangs rgyas chags med thugs chud don dam mkhyen pa rnams/ /chos kyi dam pa'i mchog rnams yang dag kun ston cing / /rgya chen nyon mongs las las
43b4(phal chen): sems can grol mdzad de/ /mya ngan 'das pa dam pa mchog la dgod mdzad pa/ /ye shes 'od zer 'od yang nyi ma lta bu ste/ /'gro bar spyod pa dkar pos yongs rgyas zla ba bzhin/ /yon tan shin tu
43b5(phal chen): bsags pa tshad med chu lta bu/ /dri med chags pa mi mnga' tshad med mkha' dbyings 'dra/ /gang zhig yon tan mtha' yas byang chub sems yangs pa/ /shin tu che zhib bde skyid tshad med smon byed cing / /
43b6(phal chen): phyi ma'i mthar thug spyod par smon pas su brtson pa/ /de dag sems can gdul ba'i don phyir rtag tu brtson/ /'jig rten 'byam klas thams cad rnam par snang ba'i phyir/ /smon lam bye ba khrag
43b7(phal chen): khrig bsam gyis mi khyab dang / /stong pa mtshan ma med pa smon med mi gnas pa/ /smon lam bye ba brgyas ni sems kyi bag chags dag par 'gyur/ /chos kyi rang bzhin namakha' lta bu sus rtogs
43b8(phal chen): shing / /zhi dang rab zhi nyer zhir thams cad mnyam gzhog pa/ /de dag chos grangs khrag khrig bsam gyis myi khyab pa'i/ /grangs su 'gro la ston kyang de ni gnas pa med/ /phyogs bcu kun gyi
44a1(phal chen): 'jig rten gtso bo ji snyed pa/ /de dag kun gyi byang chub sems mchog 'di bsngags ste/ /yon tan brgya phrag bsam gyis mi khyab pas kyang brgyan/ /sems can gtso bzhin yang dag pha rol phyin
44a2(phal chen): pa yin/ /bskal pa sems can snyed du gal te legs brjod kyang / /byang chub sems rab de la mthar thug gang yang med/ /rgyal ba 'byung ba'i rin chen der ni gang skyes pa/ /de yi dpe ni khams
44a3(phal chen): gsum glongs kyang gang yang med/ /dus gsum rgyal ba kun gyis gang zhig bstsags pa yi/ /byang chub sems rab de la smon lam kun gyis gyis/ /byang chub sems rab dam pa de ni bsod nams
44a4(phal chen): gter/ /des ni rgyal sras chags pa med pa rab tu 'thob/ /'gro ba'i sems dang spyod pa shes shing mthong rung srid/ /zhing rnams rdul du blags te bgrang bar nus kyang srid/ /bar snang skra yis mnyam par gzhal
44a5(phal chen): bar nus srid kyi/ /byang chub sems mchog yon tan mthar phyin myi nus so/ /'di las dus gsum sangs rgyas thams cad rab tu 'byung / /'di las 'jig rten 'gro ba kun gyi bde ba 'byung / /'di las rgyal
44a6(phal chen): bas bsngags pa'i legs pa thams cad 'byung / /'dis ni sems can gtso la the tsom med par 'gyur/ /'dis ni 'jig rten kun gyi sgrib pa zad par 'gyur/ /'dis ni zhing rnams yongs su dag pa'i
44a7(phal chen): mchog du 'gyur/ /'di las 'jig rten dam pa shes dang ldan pa 'byung / /gang zhig phyogs bcu'i rgyal ba lta bar 'dod pa dang / /gang zhig byin dang bsod nams myi zad mdzod 'dod dang / /gang zhig 'gro ba kun gyi
44a8(phal chen): sdug bsngal zlog 'dod pa/ /des ni yon tan mtha' yas byang chub sems bskyed bya/ /byang chub sems dpa' sems dang po bskyed pa'i bsod nams kyi phung po'i dpe yang dag par bstsags pa
44b1(phal chen): tshigs su bcad pa'i le'u zhes bya ba ste nyi shu gnyis so/ / // sangs rgyas rmad ga cad ces bya ba shin tu rgyas pa chen po'i mdo/ bam po bzhi pa/ de nas chub sems dpa' brtson 'grus blo gros kyi byang chub sems dpa' chos kyi blo gros la 'di skad ces smras so/ /
44b2(phal chen): kye rgyal ba'i sras byang chub sems dpa' thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyi sems bskyed pa rab tu thob pa/ sems dang po bskyed pa la gnas pa/ de ltar tshad med pa'i bsod nams kyi tshogs dang ldan pa/
44b3(phal chen): thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes rgya chen po la yang dag par 'dzeg pa/ byang chub sems dpa'i skyon med par shin tu chud pa/ 'jig rten gyen du khrid par byed pa/ rnam par bzlog pa rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas
44b4(phal chen): kyi 'jig rten las 'das pa'i chos nyid kyi rjes su song ba 'das pa dang / ma byon pa dang / da ltar byung ba'i de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyis byin gyis brlabs pa/ byang chub sems dpa'i rnam par dgod pa
44b5(phal chen): la shin tu nges pa/ rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu rab tu gzhol ba de dag gis de bzhin gshegs pa'i bstan pa la ji ltar brtson pa byas pa'i rnam pa gang gis/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad mnyes par
44b6(phal chen): 'gyur ba dang / byang chub sems dpa'i rnam par dgod pa las 'das par 'gyur ba dang / spyod pa'i dkyil 'khor chen po yongs su dag par 'gyur ba dang / smon lam chen po yongs su rdzogs par 'gyur
44b7(phal chen): ba dang / byang chub sems dpa'i gter chen po rab tu thob par 'gyur ba dang / sems can rnams la snod ji bzhin du sbyin pa byed par 'gyur ba dang / pha rol tu phyin pa'i phyogs yongs su myi
44b8(phal chen): gtong bar 'gyur ba dang / ji ltar dam bcas pa'i sems can rnams sgrol bar 'gyur ba dang / sangs rgyas dang chos dang dge 'dun gdung mi chad par 'gyur ba dang / dge ba'i rtsa ba dmigs pa thams
45a1(phal chen): cad du sbyor ba don med par mi 'gyur ba dang / kye rgyal ba'i sras byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyis de la brtson par byas pas chos kyi yul 'di dag yongs su rdzogs par 'gyur bar ji ltar brtsams
45a2(phal chen): par bya ba de legs par bshad pa mdzod cig / 'khor 'di dag thams cad ni nyan par 'dod do/ /sems can chen po de dag brtson pa'i rnam pa ji lta bus ma rig pa'i mun nag thams cad bsal te/ bdud kyis
45a3(phal chen): dkrugs pa'i 'khor thams cad las shin tu rgyal bar byas nas/ phas kyi rgol ba thams cad zil gyis mnan te/ sems kyi dri ma kun nas nyon mongs pa'i phyogs thams cad kun nas gsal nas/
45a4(phal chen): dge ba'i rtsa ba phun sum tshogs pa thams cad shin tu bsgrubs te/ mi khom pa dang / ngan song dang / ngan 'gro'i lam thams cad rnam par bzlog nas/ ye shes kyi dkyil 'khor chen po rnam par
45a5(phal chen): byang bar byas te/ byang chub sems dpa'i sa dang / pha rol tu phyin pa dang / gzungs dang / ting nge 'dzin dang / mngon par shes pa dang / rig pa dang / mi 'jigs pa yongs su dag pa rnams mngon par
45a6(phal chen): bsgrubs nas/ sangs rgyas kyi zhing thams cad rnam par dag pa dang / mtshan dang dpe byad bzang po dang / sku dang gsung dang thugs kyi brgyan mngon par bsgrub pa yongs su rgyas par byas ste/ de bzhin
45a7(phal chen): gshegs pa thams cad kyi stobs dang / mi 'jigs pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi chos ma 'dres pa mnyam pa nyid kyi rjes su song ste/ thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes kyi yul rtogs par 'gyur ba
45a8(phal chen): dang / de ltar mngon par byang chub nas kyang bsam pa'i tshul bzhin du sangs rgyas kyi zhing yongs su grub par gyur pa dag tu ji ltar yongs su smin par bya ba'i sems can dag la/ dus dang dbang po'i rgyud ji
45b1(phal chen): lta ba bzhin du sangs rgyas kyi mdzad pa mtha' yas pa byin par 'gyur ba de legs par shod cig / 'khor 'di dag thams cad ni nyan par 'gyur ro/ /ji ltar yang byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyis/
45b2(phal chen): yon tan 'di dang gzhan dag dang / byang chub sems dpa'i chos dang / byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa dang / byang chub sems dpa'i lam gyi yul rnams yongs su rdzogs par byas te/ myur du de bzhin
45b3(phal chen): gshegs pa'i mnyam pa nyid 'thob pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas rnams kyi bskal pa brgya stong grangs med par bsgrubs pa'i chos kyi mdzod 'di yang dag
45b4(phal chen): par bsrung zhing / byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa la gnas shing / ston pa dang 'chad pa'i tshe/ bdud dang bdud kyi rigs su rtogs pa dang / phas kyi rgol ba thams cad kyis zil gyis mi mnon pa dang /
45b5(phal chen): 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du yang skyo ba med par dam pa'i chos yongs su 'dzin par byed pa dang / de yang dag par ston pa'i tshe/ lha'i dbang po rnams kyis rim gror bya ba dang / gzhung de bzhin du klu'i
45b6(phal chen): dbang po dang / gnod sbyin gyi dbang po dang / dri za'i dbang po dang / lha ma yin gyi dbang po dang / nam mkha' lding gi dbang po dang / mi 'am ci'i dbang po dang / lto 'phye chen po'i dbang po dang / mi'i
45b7(phal chen): dbang po dang / tshangs pa'i dbang pos rim gror byas la rab tu 'thob pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i chos kyi dbang pos rim gro bya ba rab tu 'thob pa dang / de ltar rim gror byas nas kyang / 'jig rten
45b8(phal chen): 'jig rten thams cad kyis phyag bya ba/ 'jig rten thams cad kyis mngon par mchod pa/ 'jig rten thams cad kyi dbang bskur ba/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyis byin gyi dgongs pa/ byang chub
46a1(phal chen): sems dpa'i tshogs kyi shin tu bsrungs pa/ rang gi dge ba'i rtsa ba dang / smon lam rab tu thob pa/ chos dkar po chen po yang dag par dpel ba rnams/ de bzhin gshegs pa dgra
46a2(phal chen): bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas rnams kyi chos kyi mdzod rnam par 'byed par 'gyur ba dang / dam pa'i chos yongs su 'dzin pa rgya chen po rab tu 'byed pa dang / byang chub sems
46a3(phal chen): dpa'i rim gyis yongs su bsgrub pa/ shin tu ston par 'gyur ba de lta bu'i gnas dag yang dag par bston pa mdzod cig /de nas byang chub sems dpa' brtson 'grus blo gros gyis don 'di nyid bstan te
46a4(phal chen): brjod pa'i phyir/ byang chub sems dpa' chos kyi blo gros la tshigs su bcad de smras pa/ spyod la 'jug pa mtha' yas yangs pa dag /rang 'byung ye shes bsgrub pa dge ba rnams/ /rdzogs pa'i byang
46a5(phal chen): chub sems dpa' yon tan can/ /grags pa chen po rnams la legs par shod/ /byang chub sems dpa' gang rnams sems thob cing / /bsod nams ldan pa ye shes thob pa rnams/ /skyon med
46a6(phal chen): zhugs pa'i 'jig rten rnams bzlog cing / /yang dag sangs rgyas chos mnyam nyid thob rnams/ /de dag gis ni bde gshegs bstan pa la/ /brtson 'grus bstan pas ji ltar brtson par bya/
46a7(phal chen): gang gis phyogs bcu'i rgyal ba mnyes byas shing / /yang dag sangs rgyas sa yang gnan bya dang / /spyod pa dag dang smon lam yongs dag dang / /ye shes gter chen rab tu thob 'gyur zhing / /thob nas
46a8(phal chen): de dag 'gro kun mi gnas pas/ /yongs su blangs pa rtag tu gtong byed dang / /gang yang pha rol phyin pa mchog gi lam/ /de dag mi stong rab tu brjod pa dang / /sems can ji ltar sgrol byed
46b1(phal chen): dam bcas shing / /yang dag sangs rgyas bsam pa mnyam 'dzin dang / /mig gi dmyigs pa bstan pa thams cad kyi/ /'byung ba yon tan can la stobs 'gyur zhing / /skyes bu khyu mchog de dag
46b2(phal chen): brtson gyur pa'i/ /rnam dag lam de khyu mchog khyod kyis ston/ /ji ltar de dag mun pa kun gsal cing / /'khrug pa'i 'khor rnams thams cad pham byas nas/ /dri ma bral ba'i dge ldan mkhas pa rnams/ /
46b3(phal chen): skyes bu khyu mchog ye shes ldan 'gyur dang / /mi khom ngan song lam rnams yongs spangs shing / /ye shes chen po'i dkyil 'khor mchog spyod dang / /yon tan bzang po thams cad ldan gyur cig /rgyal ba'i
46b4(phal chen): ye shes stobs kyi thob 'gyur dang / /skyes bu khyu mchog ye shes zhugs nas kyang / /sems can bsam pa ji bzhin ston byed cing / /mtha' yang yas pa'i zhing rnams bsam yas su/ /ston pa chen po'i
46b5(phal chen): las kyang byed pa dang / /ci nas de dag spyod pa mchog thob nas/ /mi yi khyu mchog mdzod rnams ston byed de/ /phal gyis myi non gzhan gyis mi pham par/ /rgyal ba'i chos nyid rtag tu 'dzin byed ston/
46b6(phal chen): seng ge bzhin du ji ltar 'jigs pa med/ /khyu mchog mdzod bzhin dag pa'i mdog du spyod/ /chu la pad mo bzhin du chags med pa/ /de dag rgyal ba'i yon tan ji ltar spyod/ /de skad ces smras pa dang /
46b7(phal chen): byang chub sems dpa' chos kyi blo gros gyis/ byang chub sems dpa' brtson 'grus blo gros la 'di skad ces smras so/ /kye rgyal ba'i sras khyod ni skye bo mang po la phan pa dang / skye bo mang po
46b8(phal chen): bde ba dang / 'jig rten la snying brtse ba dang / lha dang mi rnams kyi don dang / phan pa dang bde ba'i phyir bzhugs pa ste/ kye rgyal ba'i sras de ltar khyod byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa shin tu brtags
47a1(phal chen): shing / rnam par dag pa brtsams te/ 'dri zhing de ltar rgyal ba'i sras khyod/ de bzhin gshegs pa dri ba chos mang po la rab tu gnas pa/ brtson 'grus chen pos shin tu bstsags
47a2(phal chen): pa/ brtson 'grus ldog pa myed pas shin tu 'byung ba 'dri bar byed pa ni/ kye rgyal ba'i sras legs so legs so/ /kye rgyal ba'i sras de'i phyir shin tu legs par nyon la yid la zung shig dang /
47a3(phal chen): sangs rgyas kyi mthu dang sangs rgyas kyi byin gyis brlabs kyis phyogs tsam bstan par bya'o/ /kye rgyal ba'i sras 'di la byang chub sems dpa' thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du sems bskyed pa thob pa rnams
47a4(phal chen): kyis thog mar sems bskyed pa de mi nyams par yongs su bsrung ba dang / rim gror bya ba'i phyir bag yod par bya'o/ /kye rgyal ba'i sras de la rnam pa bcus na byang chub sems dpa' bag yod pa
47a5(phal chen): la gnas pa shes bya ste/ bcu gang zhe na/ tshul khrims kyi phung po shin tu srung ba dang / byang chub kyi sems ma nyams shing shin tu sbyangs pa dang / byang chub sems dpa' bsam pa g.yo dang sgyu
47a6(phal chen): med pa dang / dge ba'i sbyor ba phyir mi ldog pa dang / rang gi sems bskyed pa shin tu rtog pa dang / phyogs khyim pa dang / so so'i skye bo dang ma 'dres pa dang / dge ba'i rtsa ba'i las 'jig rten
47a7(phal chen): gyi 'du shes dang / 'dod pa thams cad dang bral ba dang / byang chub sems dpa'i lam nyan thos dang / rang sangs rgyas kyi theg pa spangs pa rab tu thob pa dang / dge ba'i rtsa ba brtsams
47a8(phal chen): pa nan tan rgyun chad pa med pa dang / bdag gi rgyud kyi stobs kyi shugs shin tu rtogs pa dag ste/ kye rgyal ba'i sras rnam pa bcu po 'di dag dang ldan pa'i byang chub sems dpa' ni
47b1(phal chen): bag yod pa la gnas pa shes bya'o/ /kye rgyal ba'i sras de la byang chub sems dpa' bag yod pa la gnas pa ni/ rnam pa bcus na yongs su dag par 'gyur te/ bcu gang zhe na 'di lta ste/
47b2(phal chen): kye rgyal ba'i sras 'di la byang chub sems dpa' ji ltar smras pa de ltar byed pa yin/ shes bzhin dran pa can yin/ khengs pa med cing g.yo ba med de/ bsam gtan bzang po la
47b3(phal chen): rab tu gnas pa yin/ sangs rgyas kyi chos zab mo btsal ba la nan tan du byed cing rgyun mi gcod pa yin/ lhag mthong mngon par bsgrub pa la mkhas shing ji ltar thos pa'i chos la
47b4(phal chen): tshul bzhin du rtogs par zhugs pa yin/ bsam gtan gyi rjes su song ba'i sems kyis/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i rnam par 'phrul pa zab mo'i rjes su song ba yin/ sa dang mnyam zhing
47b5(phal chen): mthon dman dang bral ba yin/ sbyor ba bzang ngan dang bar ma la sems nyams pa med pa yin/ sems can kun gyi nang na thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du sems gcig bskyed pa la 'ang ston pa'i bsam pa thob
47b6(phal chen): pa yin/ mkhan po dang slob dpon dang dge ba'i bshes gnyen dang / byang chub sems dpa' dang / chos smra ba rnams la rim gro dang bkur sti'i ngang tshul can du gnas pa yin te/ kye rgyal ba'i sras rnam pa bcu
47b7(phal chen): po de dag gis byang chub sems dpa' bag yod pa la gnas pa/ yongs su dag par 'gyur ro/ /kye rgyal ba'i sras de la byang chub sems dpa' bag yod pa brtson 'grus brtsams pa/ dran pa
47b8(phal chen): nye bar gzhag pa dang / mos pa che ba dang / rnal 'byor rgyun ma bcad pa chos thams cad la mi gnas pa/ chos thams cad la brtson pa/ nyon mongs pa med pa'i tshul la zhugs pa/
48a1(phal chen): sems yangs pa sangs rgyas kyi chos mtha' dang dbus med pa'i rjes su song ba rnams kyis ni/ de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas rnams mnyes par
48a2(phal chen): 'gyur te/ kye rgyal ba'i sras byang chub sems dpa' chos bcus de bzhin gshegs pa rnams mnyes par bya'o/ /bcu gang zhe na/ byang chub sems dpa' brtson 'grus thams cad la phyir myi
48a3(phal chen): ldog pa dang / lus dang srog la mi lta ba dang / 'tsho ba'i yo byad dang / 'tsho ba'i rkyen la don du gnyer ba med pa dang / chos thams cad rnam par bsgom pas nam mkha' dang mnyam pa dang / chos
48a4(phal chen): kyi dbyings la yang dag par gzhol ba'i lhag mthong la mkhas pa dang / mi gnas pa'i chos rnam par bsgom pa'i phyag rgya dang / rtag tu rgyun mi 'chad par bsgrubs pa'i smon lam chen po dang / yongs su
48a5(phal chen): sbyangs pa'i bzod pa shes pa'i snang ba dang / rang gi dge ba'i chos bstsags pa dang / ma bstsags pa shin tu brtags pa dang / mngon par 'du bya ba med pa'i sgo shin tu byang ba ste/ kye rgyal ba'i sras
48a6(phal chen): bcu po de dag gis de bzhin gshegs pa mnyes par bya'o/ /kye rgyal ba'i sras de la byang chub sems dpa' chos bcu la gnas pa rnams kyis ni/ de bzhin gshegs pa rnams mnyes par 'gyur
48a7(phal chen): ba yin te/ bcu gang zhe na/ 'di lta ste bag yod pa la gnas pa dang / myi skye ba'i bzod pa la gnas pa dang / snying rje chen po la gnas pa dang / pha rol tu phyin pa yongs su rdzogs par bya ba
48a8(phal chen): la gnas pa dang / spyod pa yongs su rdzogs par bya ba la gnas pa dang / smon lam mngon par bsgrub pa la gnas pa dang / thabs mkhas pa la gnas pa dang / brten pa'i stobs kyi
48b1(phal chen): shugs la gnas pa dang / chos thams cad nam mkha'i rang bzhin lta bu la gnas pa dang / len pa med pa la gnas pa ste/ kye rgyal ba'i sras chos de dag la gnas pa'i byang chub sems dpa' rnams
48b2(phal chen): kyis ni/ de bzhin gshegs pa mnyes par 'gyur ro/ /kye rgyal ba'i sras de la chos bcu dang ldan pa'i byang chub sems dpa' rnams ni sa rnam par dgod pa las 'da' ba yin te/ bcu gang zhe na 'di lta
48b3(phal chen): ste/ bsod nams dang ye shes kyi tshogs shin tu bstsag pa dang / pha rol tu phyin pa rnam par phye ba tshad med pa lam gzhan gyis dring mi 'jog pa'i ye shes snang ba dang / dge ba'i bshes gnyen dang
48b4(phal chen): 'grogs pa rgyun mi chad pa dang / brtson 'grus zhig pa med pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i byin gyis brlabs kyis legs par brlabs pa dang / dge ba'i rtsa ba sbyor bas mi skyo ba dang /
48b5(phal chen): theg pa'i rgyan shin tu bshams pa dang / ye shes kyi bsam pa rab tu rno ba dang / sa dang sa' ma yin pa'i chos kyi sgo la mi gnas pa dang / 'das pa dang ma byon pa dang / da ltar byung ba'i
48b6(phal chen): sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das thams cad dang / dge ba'i rtsa ba'i rgyud kyi tshul gcig tu gyur pa dag ste/ kye rgyal ba'i sras chos bcu po de dag gis byang chub sems dpa' rnams/ sa nas
48b7(phal chen): sar rnam par dgod pa las 'da' ba yin no/ /kye rgyal ba'i sras byang chub sems dpa' de dag ni thog ma nas/ sa rnam par dgod pa thams cad la mkhas pa rnam par dpyod pa yin te/
48b8(phal chen): chos kyi sgo gang gis gang khong du chud par 'gyur ba dang / ye shes kyi sgo gang gis thob par 'gyur ba dang / bsgrub pa gang yin pa dang / rgyu mthun pa gang yin pa dang / spyod yul
49a1(phal chen): gang yin pa dang / rnam par 'phrul pa gang yin pa dang / yang dag par mthong ba gang yin pa dang / chos kyi sgo rnam par dbye ba'i khyad par gang yin pa dang / ji ltar thob par bya ba thams
49a2(phal chen): cad kyi rnam par dpyod do/ /de dag la shin tu rnam par dgod pas/ chos thams cad la mi gnas shing sems kyi rang bzhin gyi chos thams cad khong du chud pas byang chub sems dpa'i sa yang dag par
49a3(phal chen): 'da' 'o/ /kye rgyal ba'i sras byang chub sems dpa' rnams ni 'di ltar bdag cag gis ji nas kyang myur du 'da' bar bya'o/ /snyam nas myi sems te/ de ci'i phyir zhe na/ 'di ltar de dag 'di
49a4(phal chen): snyam du sems te/ bdag cag sa nas sa la rnam par gnas pas/ ji lta ji ltar yang dag par gnas pa de lta de ltar bsod nams kyi tshogs chos che ba skye bar 'gyur te/ ji lta ji ltar bsod nams kyi tshogs
49a5(phal chen): chen po skyes par gyur pa/ de lta de ltar de bzhin gshegs pa'i sa'i rjes su bsngos zhing sangs rgyas kyi mdzad pa tshad med pas nye bar gnas par gyur to/ /snyam ste de dag sbyor ba rgyun mi chad cing skyo ba med pa'i yid
49a6(phal chen): dang ldan pa dang / tshogs kyi rgyan chen pos byang chub sems dpa'i rnam par bkod pa las yang dag par 'da'o/ /kye rgyal ba'i sras de la byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyis rnam pa bcus spyod pa'i dkyil 'khor
49a7(phal chen): yongs su sbyang bar byas te/ bcu gang zhe na yo byad yongs su gzung ba med pa dang / 'gro ba thams cad tshim par byed pa dang / tshul khrims yang dag par blangs pa kha na ma tho ba med pa dang / bzod pa
49a8(phal chen): dang des pa mi zad pa'i sa'i rjes su song ba dang / brtson 'grus rtsom pa phyir mi ldog pa'i sbyor ba dang ldan pa dang / dran pa'i stobs kyi shugs rmongs pa med pa dang / gcig las rnam pa tha dad
49b1(phal chen): pa'i chos kyi rjes su song zhing khong du chud pa dang / gnas med pa'i spyod pa bsgrub dka' ba thams cad la sems ri'i rgyal po lta bu dang / sems can thams cad dang ma 'dres pa'i
49b2(phal chen): mu stegs su gyur pa dang / 'gro ba thams cad du sangs rgyas thams cad dang / rgyud kyi tshul gcig tu gyur pa ste/ kye rgyal ba'i sras rnam pa bcu po de dag gis/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyis spyod
49b3(phal chen): pa'i dkyil 'khor yongs su sbyong bar bya'o/ /de dag gi byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa de ltar yongs su sbyangs pa de rnam pa bcus shin tu dag par gyur te/ bcu gang zhe na sems can gyi gtso bo 'jig rten gyi khams
49b4(phal chen): na bzhugs pas yang dag par dgongs pa dang / 'das pa'i byang chub sems dpa'i grogs kyis dge ba'i rtsa ba bskyed pa dang / sangs rgyas kyis byin gyis brlabs yang dag par gzung ba dang mkhas pa dang /
49b5(phal chen): dge ba'i bshes gnyen la yang dag par brten pa dang / mos pa dang brtson 'grus dang / bag yod pa la rab tu gnas pa dang / chos tha dad pa thams cad la tha mi dad par rtogs pa dang / snying rje'i byin
49b6(phal chen): gyis brlabs shin tu che ba dang / chos thams cad yang dag pa ji lta ba bzhin du rnam par lta ba'i shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa mngon par bsgrub pa dang / thabs la mkhas par rnam par spyod pa'i sbyor ba
49b7(phal chen): dang / sbyor ba thams cad la de bzhin gshegs pa'i stobs kyi rjes su 'brang ba dag ste/ kye rgyal ba'i sras rnam pa bcu po de dag gis/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyis spyod pa'i dkyil
49b8(phal chen): 'khor yongs su sbyang bar bya'o/ /kye rgyal ba'i sras de la byang chub sems dpa'i smon lam rnam par dag pa bcu ste/ bcu gang zhe na 'di lta ste skyo ba med par sems can gyi khams
50a1(phal chen): yongs su dag par bya ba'i smon lam dang / dge ba'i rtsa ba sna tshogs bstsags pas 'jig rten gyi khams yongs su dag par bya ba'i smon lam dang / lus dang srog gi bsngo zhing dam pa'i chos
50a2(phal chen): yongs su 'dzin pa'i smon lam dang / ye shes kyi sgo rnam par dbye ba khong du chud pas sangs rgyas kyi zhing la 'jug pa'i smon lam dang / byang chub sems dpa' thams cad dang gnyis su med pas
50a3(phal chen): tshul gcig gi rgyud du 'gro ba'i smon lam dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i sgo la 'jug pas chos thams cad khong du chud pa'i smon lam dang / mos pa rnam par sbyangs pas blta na don yod pa'i smon lam
50a4(phal chen): dang / phyi ma'i mthar byin gyi brlab pa'i bskal par gnas pa'i smon lam dang / byang chub sems dpa' kun tu bzang po'i theg pa'i rgyan rnam pa thams cad kyi sgo nas rnam par sbyang ba'i smon
50a5(phal chen): lam dag ste/ kye rgyal ba'i sras byang chub sems dpa' rnams ni de ltar smon lam rnam par sbyong ngo / /de dag rnam pa bcus smon lam yongs su rdzogs par byed de/ bcu gang zhe na yongs su skyo ba
50a6(phal chen): med pa dang / rgyan chen po mngon par bsgrub pa dang / byang chub sems dpa'i smon lam khyad par du 'phags pa rnams kyi rjes su 'jug pa dang / 'jig rten gyi khams gzhan na bzhugs pa'i
50a7(phal chen): de bzhin gshegs pa'i sangs rgyas kyi zhing thos nas/ rang gi smon lam du mngon par bsgrub pa dang / bsam pa phyi ma'i mtha' mur thug pa dang / sems can gyi khams thams cad yongs su
50a8(phal chen): smin par bya bar gtugs pa'i smon lam chen po dang ldan pa dang / bskal pa thams cad du gnas pas mi 'jig pa dang / sdug bsngal thams cad kyis ji mi snyam pa dang / bde ba thams
50b1(phal chen): cad la yongs mi brngam pa dang / bsam pa mnyam pa med pa'i rnam par thar pa yongs su bsrung ba dag ste/ de ltar smon lam chen po de ltar yongs su sbyong zhing / yongs su rdzogs par byed pa'i tshe/
50b2(phal chen): sangs rgyas mthong ba'i gter zad mi shes pa 'ang rab tu 'thob bo/ /gzungs 'khrul pa med pa'i gter zad mi shes pa 'ang rab tu 'thob bo/ /smon lam zad mi shes pas chos thams cad shin tu
50b3(phal chen): rtogs pa'i gzungs kyang rab tu 'thob bo/ /snying rje chen pos 'gro ba thams cad yongs su skyob pa'i gter zad mi shes pa 'ang rab tu 'thob bo/ /ting nge 'dzin gyi rgyud kyi gter zad mi shes pa 'ang rab tu 'thob bo/ /
50b4(phal chen): 'gro ba thams cad tshim par bya ba'i bsod nams kyi gter zad mi shes pa 'ang rab tu 'thob bo/ /chos yang dag pa ji lta ba bzhin du brtags pa'i ye shes kyi gter zad mi shes pa 'ang rab tu 'thob bo/ /
50b5(phal chen): rnam par smyin pa la gnas pa mngon par bsgrub pa'i gter zad mi shes pa'ang rab tu 'thob bo/ /sangs rgyas kyi byin gyi rlabs mtha' yas pa'i gter zad myi shes pa'ang rab tu 'thob bo/ /'jig
50b6(phal chen): rten gyi khams mtha' dang dbus med par gtogs pa la 'jugs pa'i gter zad mi shes pa'ang rab tu 'thob bo/ /de ltar gter rab tu thob cing bsod nams dang ye shes kyi tshogs zad mi
50b7(phal chen): shes pa dang ldan pa de dag ye shes chen po'i dkyil 'khor yongs su dag pas/ sems can rnams la bsam pa ji lta ba bzhin du chos kyi gter gyi sbyin pa byed do/ /de la rgyal ba'i sras byang chub
50b8(phal chen): sems dpa' rnams sems can gyi bsam pa bzhin du ji ltar 'jug ce na/ sbyor ba ji ltar rgyu ba dang / rgyu dang rkyen ji lta ba dang / sems dang sems las byung ba'i sbyor ba ji lta ba las/
51a1(phal chen): sems can rnams kyi bsam pa ji lta ba bzhin du 'jug ste/ de dag de ltar bsam pa la zhugs pa rnams sems can rnams kyi bsam pa ji lta ba bzhin du shes shing chos yang dag par ston to/ de dag
51a2(phal chen): 'dod chags kyi bsam pa rnam par bzlog pa'i phyir mi sdug pa yang dag par ston to/ /zhe sdang gi bsam pa rnam par bzlog pa'i phyir/ byams pa chen po'i sbyor ba yang dag par ston to/ /gti mug gi bsam
51a3(phal chen): pa rnam par bzlog pa'i phyir chos rnam par 'byed pa la mkhas pa yang dag par ston to/ /cha mnyam pa rnam par bzlog pa'i phyir ye shes kyi khyad par dang ldan pa'i chos kyi sgo yang dag par ston to/ /'khor
51a4(phal chen): ba'i bsam pa rnam par bzlog pa'i phyir/ sdug bsngal rnam pa gsum dang ldan pa yang dag par ston to/ /gnas kyi bsam pa rnam par bzlog pa'i phyir gnas med pa'i chos kyi sgo yang dag par ston to/ /
51a5(phal chen): zhum pa'i bsam pa rnam par bzlog pa'i phyir/ rgya chen po'i yul yang dag par ston to/ /bdag gi nga rgyal gyis bcom pa'i bsam pa rnam par bzlog pa'i phyir/ chos kyi mnyam pa nyid yang dag
51a6(phal chen): par ston to/ /g.yo dang sgyus mi mnyam pa'i bsam pa rnam par bzlog pa'i phyir/ byang chub sems dpa'i bsam pa mnyam pa nyid dang / zhi ba'i gnas kyi bsam pa mngon par bsgrub pa yang
51a7(phal chen): dag par ston to/ /de dag ni de ltar sems can rnams la bsam pa ji bzhin du chos kyi gter yang dag par ston to/ /de yang don dbyer med pa yang dag par ston te/ yi ge'i mtshams sbyor bar
51a8(phal chen): sbyar bas yang dag par ston to/ /shes pa rnam par dbye bas yang dag par ston to/ /bstan pa snga phyi ma 'dres pas yang dag par ston to/ /chos kyi tshul dang tshul ma yin pa'i bye brag dbyer
51b1(phal chen): med pas yang dag par ston to/ /mtshan nyid kyi phyag rgya rnam par mi 'khrugs pas yang dag par ston to/ /chos rab tu dgod pa rgyun chad pa med pas yang dag par ston to/ /mtha' yas pa sbyang bas yang
51b2(phal chen): dag par ston to/ /the tsom thams cad shin tu gcad pa'i phyir yang dag par ston to/ /dbang po'i rgyud la 'jug pa'i phyir yang dag par ston to/ /de bzhin gshegs pa'i phyag rgya la dgod par gzhol bas yang dag
51b3(phal chen): par ston to/ /yang dag pa'i mtha' mtshan nyid med pa rnam par mi 'khrugs pas yang dag par ston to/ /chos kyi dbyings la yang dag par gzhol bas yang dag par ston to/ /chos kyi rnga yang dag par brdung bas
51b4(phal chen): yang dag par ston to/ /gnas thams cad yang dag par spang bas yang dag par ston to/ /de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad rjes su dran pa mi gtong bas yang dag par ston to/ /tshig dang skad dang sgra dang ngag gi
51b5(phal chen): las thams cad mnyam pa nyid la mi gnas pas yang dag par ston to/ /rnam par mi rtog pa'i dbyings kyi rjes su 'gro bas yang dag par ston to/ /dpe thams cad rnam par dgod pas rgyud dang mi
51b6(phal chen): 'gal bar brtan par bya bas yang dag par ston to/ /de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi ye shes kyi dkyil 'khor rang gi lus su sems pa la yang dag par gzhol bas yang dag par ston to/ /
51b7(phal chen): de ltar sems can la chos yang dag par ston pas/ rtag tu rgyun myi 'chad par chos kyi nan tan gyi mtshan nyid kyi rjes su 'brang ba dang / rang gi don rting tshugs par byed pa dang / pha rol tu phyin
51b8(phal chen): pa'i phyogs mi gtong bas rgyan chen po'i pha rol tu phyin pa'i theg pa yang dag par bsgrub bo/ /de la 'ang sems can thams cad tshim par bya ba dang / yo byad kyis yongs su bsdud pa dang
52a1(phal chen): sbyor ba mnyam par yongasu gtong bas sbyin pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa yongs su dag par byed do/ /yang dag par blangs pa mi gtong ba dang / gnas pa med pa dang / nga rgyal med pas tshul khrims kyi pha rol tu
52a2(phal chen): phyin pa yongs su dag par byed do/ /nyes pa thams cad khyad du gsod pa dang / sems can thams cad kyis mi 'khrugs pa dang / mnyam pa nyid la gzhol ba dang / mthon dman med pa dang /
52a3(phal chen): zad myi shes pa'i sa mnyam par 'dzin pas bzod pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa yongs su dag par byed do/ /brtsom pa chen po brtsams pa dang / brtsom pa thams cad la zhum pa med pa dang / sbyor ba phyir mi ldog
52a4(phal chen): pa dang / yid la byed pa phyir mi 'gyur ba dang / mthu mtha' yas pa dang / stobs la thub pa med pa dang / sngon du 'dor ba mi 'phrogs pa dang / dad pa'i mthu chen po dang / blang ba dang / dor ba med pa'i
52a5(phal chen): tshogs thams cad yongs su rgyas par bya ba dang / thams cad mkhyen pa'i sgo nyams pa med pa la yang dag par 'jug pas brtson 'grus kyi pha rol tu phyin pa yongs su dag par byed do/ /'dod pa'i
52a6(phal chen): yon tan thams cad kyi 'du 'dzi yongs su sbyong ba dang mi 'bral ba dang / rim gyis bsam gtan dang ting nge 'dzin mngon par bsgrub pa dang / gnas med cing blang ba med pa shin tu rtogs pa dang / nyon mongs pa
52a7(phal chen): thams cad rab tu sel ba dang / ting nge 'dzin gyi sgo mtha' yas pa mngon par bsgrub pa dang / mngon par shes pa chen pos rnam par 'phrul pa'i rjes su 'gro ba dang / rim gyis rnam par spong ba'i
52a8(phal chen): ting nge 'dzin gyi sgo la rab tu 'jug pa dang / ting nge 'dzin gcig la sgo mtha' yas par rab tu 'jug pa dang / ting nge 'dzin gyi spyod yul thams cad shes pa dang / de'i yul gyi rjes su rab tu
52b1(phal chen): zhugs pa dang / ting nge 'dzin dang / snyoms par 'jug pa thams cad ye shes kyi phyag rgya mi 'khrugs pa thams cad mkhyen pa'i sa la nye bar gyur pas bsam gtan gyi pha rol tu phyin pa yongs
52b2(phal chen): su dag par byed do/ /sangs rgyas kyi chos thams cad mnyan pa dang / bzung ba dang / blang ba dang / bcang ba dang / dge ba'i bshes gnyen thams cad bsnyen bkur bas yongs su mi skyo ba dang /
52b3(phal chen): chos thams cad kyi mi ngoms pa dang / ji ltar thos pa la tshul bzhin du rtogs pa dang / de la mngon sum du mnyam par gzhog pa dang / sgro 'dogs pa'i lta ba thams cad dang bral ba dang /
52b4(phal chen): chos thams cad rnam par 'byed pa la mkhas pa dang / mtshan nyid kyi phyag rgya tha mi dad pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i sgo nas lhun gyis grub par sgom zhing bsgom pa dang / stobs la 'jug
52b5(phal chen): pa dang / thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes la 'jug pa rgyun mi chad pa dang / shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa sgo kun dang ldan pas/ thams cad mkhyen pa'i sgor 'jug pas shes rab kyi pha rol tu
52b6(phal chen): phyin pa yongs su dag par byed do/ /'jig rten gyi bya ba'i rgyud thams cad ston pa dang / sems can gyi rgyud yongs su smyin pas yongs su mi skyo ba dang / bsam pa bzhin du bya ba ston
52b7(phal chen): pa dang / bya ba thams cad la mngon par chags pa med pa dang / byis pa'i spyod pa dang / 'phags pa'i spyod pa bsam pa ji lta ba bzhin du ston pa dang / 'khor ba dang mya ngan las 'das pa
52b8(phal chen): nye bar ston pa dang / sbyor ba thams cad shin tu brtags pas rgyu ba dang / rgyan thams cad bstan pa gnas med pa dang / 'gro ba thams cad kyi rjes su 'gro zhing rjes su 'brang ba dang /
53a1(phal chen): sems can thams cad sgrol ba'i spyod pas thabs mkhas pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa yongs su sbyong ngo / /sems can gyi khams mthar thug par yongs su smyin par bya ba dang /
53a2(phal chen): 'jig rten gyi khams mthar thug par yongs su sbyang ba dang / de bzhin gshegs pa mthar thug par mchod pa dang / chos chags pa med pa'i mthar thug par rnam par 'tshang rgya ba dang / chos kyi dbyings
53a3(phal chen): kyi mthar thug par spyod pa'i dkyil 'khor yongs su rdzogs par bya ba dang / bskal pa phyi ma'i mthar thug par rab tu gnas pa dang / sems bskyed pa'i mthar thug par stobs la rab tu 'jug pa
53a4(phal chen): dang / 'gro ba dang ldog pa mthar thug par mngon par 'tshang rgya ba dang / zhing gi gnas kyi mthar thug par thams cad mthong ba dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i ye shes kyi mthar thug pa rab tu thob
53a5(phal chen): par bya bas smon lam gyi pha rol tu phyin pa yongs su dag par byed do/ /bsam pa'i stobs kun nas nyon mongs pa med pa dang / lhag pa'i bsam pa'i stobs dbang du gyur cing thub pa med pa dang /
53a6(phal chen): snying rje chen po'i stobs skyo ba med pa dang / byams pa chen po'i stobs snyoms pa'i sbyor ba can dang / gzungs kyi stobs don thams cad kyi sbyor ba la sgrib pa med pa dang / spobs pa'i stobs
53a7(phal chen): 'gro ba thams cad tshim par byed pa dang / pha rol tu phyin pa'i stobs theg pa thams cad kyi rgyan byed pa dang / smon lam gyi stobs bcad du mi rung ba dang / mngon par shes pa'i
53a8(phal chen): stobs tshad med pa mngon par bsgrub pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi byin gyi brlabs la mos pa dam pa'i stobs rab tu 'dzin pas/ stobs kyi pha rol tu phyin pa yongs su dag par byed do/ /
53b1(phal chen): 'dod chags kyi spyod pa khong du chud pa dang / zhe sdang gi spyod pa rjes su rtogs pa dang / gti mug gi spyod pa rab tu rtogs pa dang / cha mnyam pa'i spyod pa rjes su shes pa dang / slob pa'i
53b2(phal chen): sems can gyi spyod pa rab tu rtogs pa dang / skad cig cig gis sems can mtha' yas pa'i spyod pa rnam par rtog pa dang / sems dang bsam pa mtha' yas pa thams cad shes par byed pa dang / chos
53b3(phal chen): thams cad la yang dag pa ji lta ba bzhin du rtogs pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i stobs kyi rjes su 'jug pa dang / chos kyi dbyings kyi sgo thams cad dang ldan pa khong du chud pas/ ye shes kyi pha rol
53b4(phal chen): tu phyin pa yongs su dag par byed do/ /de dag de ltar pha rol tu phyin pa rnams yongs su sbyong zhing pha rol tu phyin pa de dag yongs su rdzogs par byed pa dang / pha rol tu phyin pa'i phyogs mi gtong bar byang chub
53b5(phal chen): sems dpa'i theg pa rgyan chen po'i rgyan dang ldan pa la gnas shing / sems can gyi khams ji ltar dam bcas pa bzhin du yang dag par sgrol lo/ /de dag dge ba'i las shin tu bstsags pa ston pas/ ngan
53b6(phal chen): song du 'gro ba'i sems can sgrol lo/ /brtsams pa chen po la gzung bas sems can gyi mi khom par 'gro ba sgrol lo/ /lhag mthong nye bar stob pas gzugs kyi khams na 'khod pa'i sems can gyi
53b7(phal chen): khams sgrol lo/ /phra ba'i ye shes nye bar stob pas gzugs med pa'i khams su skyes pa'i sems can rnams sgrol lo/ /zhi ba'i tshul nye bar stobs pas nyan thos dang rang sangs rgyas kyi theg pa la
53b8(phal chen): mos pa'i sems can gyi khams sgrol lo/ /stobs bcu'i rgyan chen po dang ldan pa bstabs pas/ theg pa chen po la myos pa'i sems can gyi khams sgrol lo/ /de ltar na sngon las dang po pa'i sa la
54a1(phal chen): gnas pa'i tshe/ sems can g.yang sa chen po nas lhung ba rnam pa tha dad par gyur pa ji lta ba bzhin du shes te/ sgo sna tshogs nas gzung bar bya'o/ /zhes seng ge'i sgra sgrags pa
54a2(phal chen): de bzhin du ye shes thob pa rnams thams cad bsgral ba'i phyir rab tu zhugs pa yin no/ /kye rgyal ba'i sras byang chub sems dpa' ye shes de lta bu la zhugs pa ni rtag tu rgyun mi gcod par sangs rgyas
54a3(phal chen): kyi rigs dang chos kyi rigs dang dge 'dun gyi rigs mi gcad pa'i phyir zhugs pa yin te/ de dag byang chub kyi sems gzhan gyi rgyud la gzhol bas sangs rgyas kyi rigs mi gcod pa yin/ chos kyi mdzod rnam
54a4(phal chen): par 'grel pas chos kyi rigs mi gcod pa yin/ bstan pa'i tshul dang 'gal bar mi byed pas/ dge 'dun gyi rigs mi gcod pa yin/ smon lam chen po yang dag par brjod pas sangs rgyas kyi
54a5(phal chen): rigs mi gcod pa yin/ rten cing 'brel par 'byung ba'i tshul yang dag par ston pas chos kyi rigs mi gcod pa yin/ snying po thob par byed pa'i chos la brtson pas dge 'dun gyi rigs mi gcod pa yin/ de bzhin
54a6(phal chen): gshegs pa'i sa bon sems can gyi zhing la 'debs pas/ sangs rgyas kyi rigs mi gcod pa yin/ dam pa'i chos yongs su 'dzin pas chos kyi rigs mi gcod pa yin/ tshogs chen po yongs su sdud pas mi bskyo bas dge
54a7(phal chen): 'dun gyi rigs mi gcod pa yin/ 'das pa dang ma byon pa dang / da ltar byung ba'i sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyis mdzad pa dran pa'i phyir/ rtag tu de bzhin gshegs pa'i gdams ngag dang / rjes su
54a8(phal chen): bstan pa mi gtong bas/ sangs rgyas dang chos dang dge 'dun gyi rigs mi gcod pa yin/ de dag de ltar skyabs gsum gyi rigs mi gcad pa'i phyir zhugs pas rtsom pa thams cad kha na ma tho ba med pa yin te
54b1(phal chen): brtsams pa gang ci rtsom yang rung / de dag thams cad du thogs pa med par thams cad mkhyen pa'i sgor 'byung ba thob par byed do/ /de dag de ltar lus kyi las kha na ma tho ba med pa dang / ngag gi las kha na ma tho ba med
54b2(phal chen): pa dang / yid kyi las kha na ma tho ba med pa la gnas pas dge ba'i rtsa ba brtsom pa don yod par brtsom pa yin te/ sems can gyi don sbyor ba don yod par brtsom mo/ /sems can don yod par 'dul bar byed do/ /chos don
54b3(phal chen): yod par ston to/ /de'i chos ston pa thams cad kyang sems can gyi bsam pa tshim par bya ba la thogs pa med pas khong du chud par 'gyur ro/ /de'i sems bskyed pa gcig rtsam yang log par mi 'gyur te
54b4(phal chen): sems bskyed pa gzhan thabs dang shes rab kyis yongs su zin pa thams cad kyang thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du yongs su bsngo'o/ /de de ltar chos dkar po bstsags pa don yod pa lta bu la gnas pas rgyan rnam par phye ba
54b5(phal chen): bcus sems bskyed pa thams cad yongs su bsngo ste/ bcu gang zhe na 'di ltar lus kyi rgyan sems can bsam pa ji lta ba bzhin du yang dag par ston pa dang / ngag gi rgyan the tsom thams cad gcod pa dang / sems kyi rgyan
54b6(phal chen): skad cig gcig gis ting nge 'dzin rjes su rtogs par byed pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi zhing gi rgyan kun nas nyon mongs pa med pa dang / 'od kyi rgyan 'od zer gyi dra ba mtha' dang dbus med pa kye ba 'gro ba thams cad snang
54b7(phal chen): bar byed pa dang / 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor gyi rgyan sems can gyi rnam pa tshad med pa'i tshogs yongs su mgu bar byed pa dang / rdzu 'phrul rnam par 'phrul pa'i rgyan sems can gyi bsam pa ji lta ba bzhin du rdzu 'phrul
54b8(phal chen): gyis rnam par 'phrul pa dang / bstan pa'i rgyan mkhas pa'i skye bo thams cad kyis yongs su gzung ba dang / mya ngan las 'das pa'i rgyan mngon par sangs rgyas pa gcig cig gis phyogs bcu ma lus par rgyas par
55a1(phal chen): 'gengs pa dang / chos byin gyis brlabs pa'i rgyan yul dang / dus dang snod ji lta ba bzhin du sdod pa dag ste/ de dag rgyan de lta bus sems bskyed pa thams cad du mngon par bsgrub pas lus
55a2(phal chen): dang ngag dang yid kyi las don yod pa dang / ye shes chen po don yod pa rab tu 'thob ste/ de dag mthong bas kyang 'di ltar bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu yongs su smyin par 'gyur ba'i phyir
55a3(phal chen): sems can rnams la don yod pa yin te/ thos pa dang bsnyen bkur ba dang / 'grogs pa dang / rjes su dran pa dang / rjes su rab tu byung ba dang / chos ston pa dang / dge ba'i rtsa ba la rjes su yid rang
55a4(phal chen): ba dang / dad cing mos pa dang / chung ngu na ming brjod pa tsam yang 'di ltar bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu yongs su smyin pa'i phyir sems can rnams la don du 'gyur ba yin no/ /kye rgyal ba'i sras 'di
55a5(phal chen): lta ste dper na rtsi'i ming mthong na bde ba zhes bya ba de mthong ma thag tu sems can rnams kyi lus la zhen pa 'am ltor zos pa'i dug rab tu zhi bar 'gyur ro/ /kye rgyal ba'i sras de bzhin du chos de lta bu dang ldan pa'i byang
55a6(phal chen): chub sems dpa' yang mthong ma thag tu sems can rnams kyi nyon mongs pa'i dug thams cad byang bar 'gyur te/ chos dkar po'i stobs kyi shugs kyang skye bar 'gyur ro/ /kye rgyal ba'i sras de ltar byang chub sems
55a7(phal chen): dpa' sems dpa' chen po chos nyid de lta bu dang ldan zhing chos de dag la gnas te/ shes rab kyi 'od chen pos ma rig pa'i mun pa bsal nas/ bdud kyi dkrugs ma'i 'khor thams cad byams pa dang / snying rje
55a8(phal chen): chen po'i stobs kyi pham par byas te/ ye shes dang bsod nams kyi stobs kyi shugs kyi phas kyi rgol ba thams cad kyi zil gyis mnan nas/ rdo rje lta bu'i ting nge 'dzin la 'jug pas/ sems kyi
55b1(phal chen): dri ma thams cad dang / nyon mongs pa'i phyogs thams cad bsal nas/ skye ba med pa'i stobs dang shugs kyis dge ba'i rtsa ba phun sum tshogs pa thams cad rab tu bsgrubs te/ sngon bcad sangs rgyas kyi zhing
55b2(phal chen): yongs su dag par spyad pa'i stobs dang shugs kyis mi khom pa dang / ngan song dang ngan 'gro'i lam thams cad rnam par bzlog nas/ mngon par zhen pa med pa'i stobs dang shugs kyis ye shes kyi dkyil 'khor yongs su sbyangs te/
55b3(phal chen): rim gyis thabs dang shes rab kyi stobs dang / shugs kyis byang chub sems dpa'i sa dang pha rol tu phyin pa dang / ting nge 'dzin dang / mngon par shes pa dang / rig pa dang mi 'jig pa yongs su dag pa mngon par bsgrubs
55b4(phal chen): nas/ chos dkar po thams cad kyi stobs dang shugs kyis sangs rgyas thams cad kyi mtshan dang dpe byad bzang po dang / sku dang gsung dang thugs kyi rgyan yongs su dag pa mngon par bsgrub pa rab tu rgyas par byas ste/
55b5(phal chen): ye shes kyis shes par bya ba'i dbang po dang / byin gyi brlabs kyis de bzhin gshegs pa'i stobs dang / sangs rgyas kyi chos ma 'dres pa thams cad mnyam pa nyid khong du chud par byas nas/ bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs
55b6(phal chen): pa'i byang chub kyang myur du 'thob cing thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes kyi yul yang smon lam gyi khyad par ji lta ba bzhin du 'thob par 'gyur ro/ /sngon gyi byin gyis brlabs dang / ye shes kyi byin gyi brlabs kyis mngon par
55b7(phal chen): sangs rgyas nas/ sems can rnams kyi bsam pa ji lta ba bzhin/ sangs rgyas kyi zhing ston te/ 'dul ba ji lta ba bzhin du sems can rnams la chos kyi 'khor lo chen po bskor cing / mtha' yas pa'i sems can rnam par
55b8(phal chen): 'dul lo/ /kye rgyal ba'i sras de ltar byang chub sems dpa'i chos de lta bu dang ldan pa dag tshul de lta bus sangs rgyas thams cad dang mnyam pa nyid kyi bar du thob par 'gyur te/ byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa thob nas kyang /
56a1(phal chen): 'jig rten gyi khams mtha' yas pa dag tu dam pa'i chos yongs su 'dzin cing / chos smra ba chen po yang byed do/ /de ltar chos smra ba byed pa'i tshe de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas kyi
56a2(phal chen): byin gyi brlabs pa de dag chos kyi mdzod chen po gzung zhing bsrung ba'i phyir/ tha dad pa yang dag par shes pa'i chos kyi tshul rab tu dbye ba'i rjes su song ba'i byang chub sems dpa'i tshig gis 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor mtha' yas par bdag gi
56a3(phal chen): lus kyis rgyan byin gyi brlabs kyis bstan pa mngon par bsgrub pa'i rnam pa'i mchog thams cad dang ldan pa/ tha dad pa yang dag par shes pa'i mkhas pa mtha' yas pa dang / ye shes mi zad pa'i sgor 'jug pa dang / dbyings kyi dkyil
56a4(phal chen): 'khor shin tu rnam par phye ba'i byin gyi brlabs pa dang / dbyangs gcig bsgrags pas 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor thams cad mgu bar byed pa'i dbyangs kyi yan lag rnam par dag pa bsam pa dang / bag la nyal ba dang / shes pa'i sa
56a5(phal chen): ji lta ba bzhin du rjes su 'brang ba dang / lus kyi byin gyi brlabs 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor thams cad kyi nang du phyin kyang zil gyis mi mnon pa dang / lus kyi rgyan sgo thams cad du rnam par bstan pa dang / 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor thams
56a6(phal chen): cad kyi sems dang / bsam pa khong du chud pas rab tu rtogs pa dang / tshig grol ba'i byin gyis brlabs kyis bstan pa dang chos 'chad pa'i byin gyi brlabs la/ mkhas pas chos kyi gtam chen po byed de/ stobs dang shugs
56a7(phal chen): kyi dbang thub pa med pa dang / 'jigs pa med pa'i dbang du zhum pa med pa dang / chos kyi dbang zil gyis mi non pa dang / ye shes kyi dbang gzhan gyis mi thub pa dang / shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i dbang chos kyi
56a8(phal chen): mtshan nyid 'khrug pa med pa dang / tha dad pa yang dag par shes pa'i dbang mtshams sbyor ba rgyun chad pa med par bsam pa shin tu rtogs pa dang / gzungs kyi dbang chos thams cad rnam par gdon myi za ba la 'jug
56b1(phal chen): pa dang / smon lam gyi dbang dpe sna tshogs kyis bstan pa'i tshul nye bar bsgrub pa shin tu bstan pa dang / snying rje chen po'i dbang phyir mi ldog cing rgyun ma chad pa dang / byams pa chen po'i dbang sngon shin tu bskyed pas bsam pa
