56b2(phal chen): thams cad tshim par byed pa dang / 'od zer gyi dra ba chen po gtong bas chos kyis gtam chen po byed do/ /de dag ni de bzhin gshegs pa seng ge'i gdan la bzhugs shing chos kyi gtam gsung ba dang / byang chub sems dpa'
56b3(phal chen): ye shes dang smon lam gyi khyad par dang ldan pa ma gtogs par sems can gyi ris na/ byang chub sems dpa' de la phyir brgol ba'am/ spyi gtsug blta ba 'am/ zil gyis gnan pa 'am/ dri ba'i tshogs yongs
56b4(phal chen): su dri bas thub par bya bar nus pa'i sems can gang yang med de/ de ni gnas med do/ /kye rgyal ba'i sras gal te byang chub sems dpa' dbang de lta bu thob pa la 'jig rten gyi khams brjod du med pa tsam du yangs pa'i
56b5(phal chen): 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor gyi cig yod pa 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor de yang sems can stong gsum gyi bdag po'i gzi brjid thob pa sha stag gis gang ba zhig yin na yang / de dag thams cad byang chub sems dpa'i 'khor
56b6(phal chen): gyi dkyil 'khor du 'ongs ma thag tu lus bstan pa'i dbang gis zil gyis mnan te/ byams pa chen po'i dbang gis lus kyi gzhi tshim par byas nas ye shes chen po'i dbang gis sems dang bsam pa
56b7(phal chen): rnam par shes par byas te/ mi 'jigs pa'i bsam pa chen pos chos ston par byed cing / spobs pa chen po'i dbang gi/ sems can tshim par byed do/ /kye rgyal ba'i sras de ci'i phyir zhe na/ 'di ltar
56b8(phal chen): byang chub sems dpa' de ni ye shes kyi dkyil 'khor tshad med pa dang ldan pa/ chos rnam par 'byed pa shin tu rnam par phye ba la mkhas pa dang ldan/ dran pa'i stobs dang shugs ma nyams pa rgya che ba dang ldan
57a1(phal chen): chos thams cad kyi tshul rnam par gdon mi za bar bzung zhing blangs pas rtogs par mkhas pa dang ldan/ byang chub sems dpa'i mkhas pa mtha' dang dbus med pa dang ldan/ chos kyi mtshan nyid
57a2(phal chen): sgrib pa med pa'i chos ston pa la mkhas pa dang ldan/ mos pa la mkhas pa sangs rgyas thams cad kyi byin gyis brlabs kyis blangs pa dang ldan/ dus gsum gyi de bzhin gshegs pa'i dkyil 'khor du yang
57a3(phal chen): dag par gzhol ba'i ye shes kyi byin gyis brlabs la mkhas pa dang ldan/ sems can thams cad kyi gtso bo 'das pa dang / ma byon pa dang / da ltar byung ba rnams dang / rgyud kyi tshul gcig tu rgyu ba'i bsam pa
57a4(phal chen): bzang po rnam par dag pa la mkhas pa dang ldan pas/ chos smra ba chen po byed cing / de bzhin gshegs pa rnams kyi chos kyi mdzod kyang rnam par 'byed do/ /'das pa dang / ma byon pa dang / da ltar byung ba'i de bzhin gshegs
57a5(phal chen): pa rnams kyi ye shes kyi byin gyis brlabs pa'i byang chub sems dpa'i yid kyi smon lam dang / ye shes 'byam klas pas dam pa'i chos kyang yongs su 'dzin to/ /de nas byang chub sems dpa' chos kyi blo gros gyis
57a6(phal chen): yang byang chub sems dpa'i rim gyis yang dag par 'byung ba'i chos kyi sgo'i le'u yang dag par bstan pa'i phyir/ sangs rgyas kyi byin gyi brlabs kyis de'i tshe tshigs su bcad pa 'di dag smras so/ /bsod nams
57a7(phal chen): tshogs bstsags byang chub sems la gnas pa rnams/ /rtag tu bag yod blo brten mthu chen bdog pa dag /dran dang ldan zhing byang chub sems rab mi gtong bas/ /phyogs rnams bcu por bde
57a8(phal chen): gshegs rnams ni mnyes par byed/ /brtson 'grus rtsams pa dran ldan mos pa brtan pa can/ /'jig rten kun la rtag tu mi gnas mi ldog pa/ /zab pa'i chos zhugs mya ngan med pa'i tshul mkhas rnams
57b1(phal chen): phyogs rnams bcu por bde gshegs rnams ni mnyes par byed/ /brtson 'grus brten pas bde gshegs mnyes par byas nas kyang / /dus gsum bsod nams tshogs dang ye shes ldan pa rnams/ /sa rnams gnon
57b2(phal chen): byed spyod mchog nyams pa med par byed/ /thub pa'i smon lam rdzogs byed ston pa 'ang de bzhin byed/ /ye shes gcig la zhugs pa de dag thob bya ba/ /thob nas 'gro ba kun la sbyin pa rab tu gtong / /bsam pa
57b3(phal chen): dag dang khams dang sbyor ba shes byas nas/ /dbang po ji bzhin mkhas pa de ltar chos kyang ston/ /pha rol phyin la brtson pa mthu chen ldan pa rnams/ /'gro ba rnams la chos ston dag gi don mi gtong / /pha rol
57b4(phal chen): phyin rdzogs grol ba mthu chen ldan pa rnams/ /khyu mchog mthu yis 'khor ba'i mtsho las sems can sgrol/ /de ltar nyin mtshan skyo ba med par brtson byed cing / /drang srong rgyal ba chos rigs mi gtsang zhugs
57b5(phal chen): pa yis/ /dkar po'i spyod pa gang yang rung ste spangs pa rnams/ /thams cad don yod rgyal ba rnams kyi sar 'gro'o/ /de dag ji spyod thams cad 'gro ba rnams la yang / /rnam smin don yod nyon mongs
57b6(phal chen): dri ma sbyong bar 'gyur/ /'di 'dra'i chos ldan de dag mun pa bsal byas shing / /bdud 'khrugs 'khor lo pham byas byang chub thob par byas/ /de ltar brtson zhing ye shes thob pa'i bde gshegs sras/ /bde
57b7(phal chen): gshegs rnams kyi chos rab mdzod kyang rab tu ston/ /de dag chos smra'i bya ba kun kyang shin tu byed/ /bdud rtsi mchog zhim sprin gyi char yang mngon par 'bebs/ /de dag snying rje byams pas 'gro ba kun bkang zhing / /
57b8(phal chen): brtan pa de rnams 'khor gyi bsam pa shes byas nas/ /gang gi bsam pa glo gros sems rgyud ci 'dra ba/ /de bzhin rgyal ba'i chos ni stong phrag du ma ston/ /glang po'i stobs sdug tshul
58a1(phal chen): bzang 'gro ba brtan pa rnams/ /seng ge'i rtsal ltar rtag tu sus kyang mi thub cing / /ye shes rgya mtsho lta bu ri rab bzhin gnas pa/ /sprin ltar 'gro ba kun gyi nyon mongs zhi bar byed/ /byang chub
58a2(phal chen): sems dpa' chos kyi blo gros kyis de skad ces smras pa dang / de la ston pas rjes su dgyes par mdzad do/ /chos snang ba'i le'u zhes bya ba ste/ nyi shu gsum pa'o// // sangs rgyas rmad ga cad ces bya ba shin tu rgyas pa chen po'i mdo/ bam po lnga pa/
58a3(phal chen): de nas sangs rgyas kyis mthus/ shar phyogs kyi 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad dang / lho phyogs kyi 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad dang / gzhung de bzhin du steng gi phyogs kyi 'jig rten gyi khams
58a4(phal chen): kyi bar thams cad na/ gling bzhi pa 'di la stsogs pa gling bzhi pa re re na/ de bzhin gshegs pa mang po bzhugs par snang ngo / /byang chub sems dpa' de dag kyang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i byin gyis brlabs
58a5(phal chen): kyis chos ston to/ /bdag kyang de bzhin gshegs pa'i byin gyis brlabs kyis chos ston to/ /bdag kyang de bzhin gshegs pa'i zhabs kyi drung na 'khod par shes so/ /bcom ldan 'das kyis rdzu
58a6(phal chen): 'phrul mngon par 'du mdzad pa ma bshig ma btang bar byang chub kyi shing drung yang ma spangs par ri rab kyi rtse mo nas/ mtshe ma'i gnas kyi lha'i bu rab mtshe ma'i khang pa nor bu sna tshogs gang na ba der gshegs
58a7(phal chen): par snang ngo / /ji ltar gling bzhi pa 'di na bcom ldan 'das rab mtshe ma'i gnas su gshegs par snang ba de bzhin du 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad na yang / rab mtshe ma'i gnas su gshegs par snang ste/
58a8(phal chen): byin gyis brlabs snga ma rnams kyang de bzhin mi 'khrug par snang ngo / /de nas lha'i rgyal po rab mtshe mas/ bcom ldan 'das rgyang ring po nas khang pa nor bu sna tshogs logs su mngon par gshegs pa mthong
58b1(phal chen): nas/ rings pa'i gzugs su khang pa nor bu sna tshogs kyi nang du/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i gdan rdzu 'phrul gyis bsgrubs pa'i seng ge'i khri pad mo'i snying po can/ lha rdzas kyi rin po che las byas pa pog reg brgya
58b2(phal chen): stong phrag bcus kun nas brgyan pa/ gser gyi dra ba brgya stong phrag bcus kun nas mngon par bres pa/ me tog gi bla re brgya stong phrag bcus kun nas khyab par byas pa/ phreng ba'i bla re brgya stong phrag bcus kun nas
58b3(phal chen): rgyas pa/ spos kyi bla re brgya stong phrag bcus spos thams cad kun tu 'thul bar btug pa/ rin po che'i bla re brgya stong phrag bcus kun tu bres pa/ me tog gi gdugs brgya stong phrag bcus kun nas bzung ba/
58b4(phal chen): phreng ba'i gdugs brgya stong phrag bcus kun nas bzung ba dang / rin po che'i gdugs brgya stong phrag bcus kun nas bzung ba dang / 'od gzer brgya stong phrag bcus snang bar byas pa dang / rab mtshe ma'i lha'i rgyal
58b5(phal chen): po brgya stong phrag bcus rab tu gdud pa/ tshangs pa brgya stong phrag bcus mngon par phyag bya ba/ byang chub sems dpa' brgya stong phrag bcus mngon par bstod pa/ rol mo brdung ba brgya stong phrag bcu'i sgra phyung ba/
58b6(phal chen): chos kyi glu'i dbyangs brgya stong phrag bcu'i glu'i dbyangs dang ldan pa/ me tog gi sprin gyi char brgya stong phrag bcu rab tu phab pa/ rgyan gyi sprin gyi char brgya stong phrag bcu rab tu phab pa/ gos kyi sprin gyi char brgya stong phrag
58b7(phal chen): bcu rab tu phab pas kun nas g.yog pa/ nor bu rin po che'i sprin brgya stong phrag bcu'i char rab tu phab pas kun tu snang bar byas pa/ dge ba'i rtsa ba brgya stong phrag kun nas byung ba/ sangs rgyas brgya stong
58b8(phal chen): phrag bcus byin gyi brlabs pa/ bsod nams brgya stong phrag bcus bstsags shing bsgrubs pa/ lhag pa'i bsam pa brgya stong phrag bcus shin tu sbyangs pa/ smon lam brgya stong phrag bcus rnam par dag par
59a1(phal chen): byas pa/ spyod pa brgya stong phrag bcus kun nas bslang ba/ chos brgya stong phrag bcus rab tu brtan pa/ rnam par 'phrul pa brgya stong phrag bcu dang ldan pa/ yon tan brgya stong phrag bcus shin tu 'phags
59a2(phal chen): pa/ brjod pa brgya stong phrag bcus shin tu brjod pa bshams so/ /ji ltar gling bzhi pa 'di rab mtshe ma'i gnas kyi lha'i rgyal po rab mtshe ma'i khang pa nor bu sna tshogs su de bzhin gshegs pa'i gdan gting ba/ de bzhin du
59a3(phal chen): 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad kyi gling bzhi pa dag gi/ rab mtshe ma'i gnas su yang / khang pa nor bu sna tshogs su lha'i rgyal po rab mtshe ma rnams kyis de bzhin gshegs pa'i gdan rgyan 'di 'dra ba dang / bsham
59a4(phal chen): pa'i tshul 'di 'dra ba dag kyang bting bar gyur to/ /de nas lha'i rgyal po rab mtshe mas bcom ldan 'das kyi gdan bting nas/ zhe sa dang rim gror bcom ldan 'das gang na ba der logs su thal mo sbyar te phyag 'tshal
59a5(phal chen): nas/ bcom ldan 'das la 'di skad ces gsol to/ /bcom ldan 'das gshegs su gsol/ bde bar gshegs pa gshegs su gsol/ de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas
59a6(phal chen): bde bar gshegs sam/ de nas bcom ldan 'das lha'i rgyal po rab mtshe mas spyan drangs pa bzhin du khang pa nor bu sna tshogs su gshegs so/ /ji ltar gling bzhi pa 'di rab mtshe ma'i gnas su lha'i rgyal po rab
59a7(phal chen): mtshe ma'i khang pa nor bu sna tshogs su gshegs pa de bzhin du 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du yang rab mtshe ma'i gnas su khang pa nor bu sna tshogs su gshegs par snang ngo / /de nas lha'i rgyal po rab
59a8(phal chen): mtshe ma'i lha'i dbang po'i gnas thams cad du sgra bsgrags te/ lha'i rgyal po rab mtshe mas bcom ldan 'das la gsol ba btab po/ /de nas lha'i rgyal po rab mtshe mas sngon gyi de bzhin gshegs pa dgra
59b1(phal chen): bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas rnams la/ dge ba'i rtsa ba ji ltar bskyed pa de rjes su dran nas/ sangs rgyas kyi byin gyi brlabs kyis de'i tshe tshigs su bcad pa 'di dag smras so/ /bkra shis dam pa gang
59b2(phal chen): zhig gis/ /sangs rgyas grags pa'i dam par mtshan btags mtshan gsol pa/ /nor bu'i gtsug tu gshegs pa ltar/ /de ni 'dir yang bkra shis mchog gyur cig /bkra shis dam pa gang zhig gis/ /'jig rten
59b3(phal chen): sgron ma bla zhes mtshan btags pa/ /rgyan gcig ldan par gshegs pa ltar/ /des ni 'dir yang bkra shis mchog gyur cig /bkra shis dam pa gang zhig gis/ /sgrib med gzigs pa 'dzum pa'i spyan du
59b4(phal chen): mtshan btags pa/ /rgyan gcig ldan par gshegs pa ltar/ /des ni 'dir yang bkra shis mchog gyur cig /bkra shis dam pa gang zhig gis/ /'jig rten sgron ma mar me mdzad ces mtshan btags pa/ /
59b5(phal chen): rnam par rgyal ba gshegs pa ltar/ /des ni 'dir yang bkra shis mchog gyur cig /bkra shis dam pa gang zhig gis/ /bde gshegs yang dag don gzigs pa zhes mtshan btags pa/ /dri med rtse mor gshegs
59b6(phal chen): pa ltar/ /des ni 'dir yang bkra shis mchog gyur cig /bkra shis dam pa gang zhig gis/ /de bzhin gshegs pa rang 'byung mchog ces mtshan btags pa/ /rin chen spos su gshegs gyur pa/ /
59b7(phal chen): des ni 'dir yang bkra shis mchog gyur cig /bkra shis dam pa gang zhig gis/ /'jig rten sgron ma dbyig gi lha zhes mtshan btags pa/ /dri myed sna tshogs gshegs pa ltar/ /des ni 'dir yang bkra
59b8(phal chen): shis mchog gyur cig / bkra shis dam pa gang zhig gis/ /'gro ba med pa'i smra ba'i stag ces mtshan btags pa/ /thams cad tshul du gshegs pa ltar/ /des ni 'dir yang bkra shis mchog gyur cig /
60a1(phal chen): bkra shis dam pa gang zhig gis/ /yon tan kun mnga' dpal gyis rgyal bar mtshan btags pa/ /dge ba'i rgyan du gshegs pa ltar/ /des ni 'dir yang bkra shis mchog gyur cig /bkra shis dam pa
60a2(phal chen): gang zhig gis/ /'jig rten phan brtson dka' thug drag pa mtshan btags pa/ /kun nas mdog du gshegs gyur pa/ /des ni 'dir yang bkra shis mchog gyur cig /ji ltar lha'i rgyal po rab mtshe mas sangs rgyas
60a3(phal chen): kyi byin gyi brlabs kyis/ sngon gyi rgyal ba gshegs pa brjod de mngon par bstod pa de bzhin du 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad kyi rgyal po rab mtshe ma rnams kyang sangs rgyas kyi byin gyis brlabs kyis sngon gyi
60a4(phal chen): yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas gshegs pa brjod cing / glu'i dbyangs kyis tshigs su bcad de mngon par bstod do/ /de nas bcom ldan 'das khang pa nor bu sna tshogs su gshegs nas gdan bting ba la
60a5(phal chen): skyil mo grung bcas te bzhugs so/ /ji ltar bcom ldan 'das bzhugs pa de bzhin du 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du yang gdan gting ba de dag la bzhugs par snang ngo / /bcom ldan 'das bzhugs ma thag tu
60a6(phal chen): khang pa nor bu sna tshogs de 'di lta ste/ dper na rab mtshe ma'i lha'i rigs thams cad tsam du che bar gyur pa snang ste/ 'di na ji lta ba bzhin du 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad na yang de bzhin no/ /rab mtshe ma'i gnas na
60a7(phal chen): rnam par 'phrul pa'i le'u zhes bya ba ste/ nyi shu bzhi pa// // de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis mthus phyogs bcu nas/ byang chub sems dpa' mang po lhags par gyur te/ byang chub sems dpa' re re zhing
60a8(phal chen): yang 'khor sangs rgyas kyi zhing stong phrag stong gi rdul shin tu phra ba snyed dang lhan cig tu 'ongs te/ byang chub sems dpa' sangs rgyas kyi zhing gi rdul shin tu phra ba snyed dang / lhan cig tu phyin to/ /byang chub sems dpa'
60b1(phal chen): de dag thams cad kyang ming 'di zhes bya ba dag ste/ 'di ltar yon tan dang ldan pa dang / blo gros dang ldan pa dang / dpal dang ldan pa dang / dga' ba dang ldan pa dang / khrel dang ldan pa dang / brtson 'grus dang ldan pa dang / stobs
60b2(phal chen): dang ldan pa dang / rig pa dang ldan pa dang / blo dang ldan pa dang / ye shes dang ldan pa dag go/ /byang chub sems dpa' de dag thams cad kyang 'jig rten gyi khams ming 'di zhes bya ba dag nas 'ongs pa ste/ 'di ltar gnyan
60b3(phal chen): dang ldan pa dang / me tog dang ldan pa dang / nor dang ldan pa dang / dpal dang ldan pa dang / sgron ma dang ldan pa dang / rdo rje dang ldan pa dang / bde ba dang ldan pa dang / nyi ma dang ldan pa dang / dge ba dang ldan pa dang /
60b4(phal chen): tshangs pa dang ldan pa dag go/ /byang chub sems dpa' de dag thams cad de bzhin gshegs pa mtshan 'di zhes bya ba dag gi zham ring na tshangs par spyod pa dag ste/ 'di ltar nyams pa med pa'i spyan dang / gzhan ma yin
60b5(phal chen): pa'i spyan dang / mi g.yo ba'i spyan dang / mi skyod pa'i spyan dang / chu'i spyan dang / bcings pa med pa'i spyan dang / kun tu spyod pa'i spyan dang / 'od kyi spyan dang / dam pa'i spyan dang / mthon mthing gi spyan dag go/ /de nas
60b6(phal chen): byang chub sems dpa' de dag bcom ldan 'das la phyag 'tshal nas/ sangs rgyas kyi mthus phyogs bcu rgyas par byas te/ gang nas 'ongs pa'i phyogs su brten nas seng ge'i khri rin po che'i snying po can dag
60b7(phal chen): bshams te skyil mo krung bcas nas 'khod do/ /ji ltar gling bzhi pa 'di rab mtshe ma'i gnas su byang chub sems dpa' 'ongs par gyur pa de bzhin du/ 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad kyi gling bzhi pa kun tu
60b8(phal chen): yang / rab mtshe ma'i gnas gyi khang pa nor bu sna tshogs su yang lhags par gyur te/ byang chub sems dpa'i ming yang de skad ces bya ba sha stag /de bzhin gshegs pa'i mtshan kyang de skad ces bya ba'i
61a1(phal chen): zham ring na/ tshangs par spyod pa sha stag go/ /de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis zhabs kyi bol gnyis nas 'od zer bye ba brgya stong bkye ste/ phyogs bcu thams cad snang bar byas nas/ 'jig rten gyi khams thams
61a2(phal chen): cad bstan te/ byang chub sems dpa' de dag gis/ 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad kyi gling bzhi pa kun gyi rab mtshe ma'i gnas thams cad na yang de bzhin gshegs pa'i rnam par 'phrul pa yod par mthong ngo /
61a3(phal chen): de nas byang chub sems dpa' yon tan dang ldan pas/ sangs rgyas kyi mthus phyogs bcur rnam par bltas te/ de'i tshe tshigs su bcad pa 'di dag smras so/ /sangs rgyas 'od gzer 'od snang bas/ /phyogs rnams
61a4(phal chen): thams cad rnam par snang / /des ni rab tu gsal byas pas/ /mig la rab rib gang yang med/ /mtshe ma rab kyi gnas 'di na/ /gang zag dam pa sangs rgyas bzhugs/ /de bzhin kun na 'ang gsal bar snang / /de ni
61a5(phal chen): 'jig rten ngo mtshar to/ /sems can gtso bo bcu yi rnams/ /gshegs par gyur pa mngon par bstod/ /de dag 'khor kyang ci 'dra ba/ /de bzhin kun na rab tu snang / /phyogs rnams bcu po thams cad na/ /
61a6(phal chen): chos kyi dam pa rab tu ston/ /de kun ming yang 'di bzhin te/ /bdag cag rnams kyi kun rdzob bzhin/ /'jig rten khams kyi ming dag kyang / /de zhes bya ba kun nas 'ongs/ /gang zag dam pa de dag ni/ /tshangs pa'i
61a7(phal chen): spyod pa de na spyod/ /bdag cag rnams la gang brtags pa/ /kun gyi ming yang de dang mthun/ /sangs rgyas zhing rnams 'phrul ldan pa/ /de dag sangs rgyas rnam 'phrul lo/ /mi yi 'jig rten kun na yang / /'di ni
61a8(phal chen): rgyal ba bzhugs par shes/ /gzhan gyis de yi rgyal po yi/ /gnas na de bzhin bzhugs pa mthong / /'jig rten khams rnams thams cad na/ /gang zag dam pa de bzhugs kyang / /rgyal ba mtshe ma rab gnas na/
61b1(phal chen): bzhugs par bdag cag kun kyang sems/ /'jig rten khams rnams thams cad na/ /sangs rgyas gzi brjid bsam mi khyab/ /de dag smon lam bskul ba'i phyir/ /'jig rten khams su rab tu bkye/ /sems can
61b2(phal chen): gtso bo'i rnam 'phrul pas/ /'di dag de rnams kun gyis mthong / /sangs rgyas yon tan mtha' yas ste/ /'jig rten zang zing thub pas spangs/ /phyogs rnams thams cad kun tu rgyu/ /chags pa med pa nam mkha'
61b3(phal chen): bzhin/ /de ni gcig las shin tu 'das/ /mang po dag tu'ang mi dmigs so/ /mtha' yas legs mnga' sangs rgyas rnams/ /de dag shes par ji ltar rung / /gnas pa med cing len pa med/ /chos dbyings rtogs
61b4(phal chen): par thugs su chud/ /de nas byang chub sems dpa' blo gros dang ldan pas/ /sangs rgyas kyi byin gyi brlabs kyis phyogs bcur rnam par bltas te/ /de'i tshe tshigs su bcad pa 'di dag smras so/ /'jig rten mgon po
61b5(phal chen): 'phrul chen rnams/ /rdul med gang zag dam pa dag /'dus shing tshogs pa bsam yas pa'i/ /bskal pa dag tu shin tu dkon/ /de dag thams cad kun gzigs pa/ /sems can gtso bo 'od mdzad de/ /srog chags
61b6(phal chen): kun la phan pa'i phyir/ /sems can rnams la chos ston to/ /'jig rten mun nag 'di dag tu/ /'jig rten mgon po byung gyur pa/ /'jig rten sgron ma de dag ni/ /blta bar shin tu dka' ba yin/ /sbyin pa tshul khrims
61b7(phal chen): bzod pa'i rab/ /brtson 'grus bsam gtan bsgoms pa dang / /shes rab sngon chad spyad pas na/ /'gro ba thams cad snang ba mdzad/ /sangs rgyas 'dra ba gang yang med/ /de phyir de yi mnyam pa med/ /chos rnams yod
61b8(phal chen): pa ma yin pas/ /skyes bu dam pa mthong ba med/ /sangs rgyas shes rab chen po rnams/ /mtshan gyi tshogs ni bsam mi khyab/ /sku yi tshogs kyis shin tu 'phags/ /chos rnams kun gyis yang dag byung / /
62a1(phal chen): 'jig rten grags chen dag pa rnams/ /dpa' bo chen po de dag snang / /de dag mtshan tsam thos pas kyang / /ngan song thams cad spangs par 'gyur/ /bskal pa rnams ni brjod med par/ /byang chub don du 'khor
62a2(phal chen): byas kyang / /'di yi tshul ni ma shes na/ /byang chub don du zhugs pa myin/ /sangs rgyas bsam gyis mi khyab pa/ /bskal pa bye bar bkur ba dang / /gang gis tshul 'di bsam pa gnyis/ /'di ni de las khyad du 'phags/ /
62a3(phal chen): gang gis brjod byas zhing gi rnams/ /rin chen gang ste thub gsol kyang / /'di'i tshul ni ma shes na/ /sangs rgyas byang chub de la ring / /de nas byang chub sems dpa' dpal dang ldan pas/ sangs rgyas kyi byin gyis
62a4(phal chen): brlabs kyis/ phyogs bcur rnam par bltas te/ de'i tshe tshigs su bcad pa 'di dag smras so/ /nam mkha' dri ma med pa la/ /nyi ma'i 'od zer mtha' yas pa/ /dpyid kyi zla ba tha ma la/ /phyogs bcu dag tu rab
62a5(phal chen): tu snang / /de tshe smyig rgyu ci 'dra ba/ /de dag bgrang bar mi nus te/ /myig can rnams kyang de la rmongs/ /long ba rnams kyi spyod yul min/ /de bzhin sems can gtso bo yis/ /yon tan mtha' dang dbus med pa/
62a6(phal chen): bskal pa bsam gyis mi khyab par/ /sus kyang shes par mi nus so/ /de dag gang nas blangs pa myed/ /de ni ci las skyes pa myed/ /rnam par bsgoms na yod pa myin/ /'ong ba med pa'i chos rnams la/ /
62a7(phal chen): 'gro ba de bzhin myi dmyigs ste/ /de phyir de dag rgyu yang med/ /de bzhin 'jig pa'ang yod pa myin/ /'jig pa med pa'i chos rnams kyi/ /rang bzhin gang gis shes pas ni/ /gang la skye ba med pa yi/ /yang dag
62a8(phal chen): sangs rgyas mthong ba yin/ /skyes pa med pa'i chos rnams kyi/ /rang bzhin dngos po mi dmigs te/ /de 'dra'i don du shes pas ni/ /dmigs pa med pa shes pa yin/ /'di la shes byed gang yang med/ /
62b1(phal chen): chos rnams thams cad mtshan nyid med/ /chos nyid 'di ni shes gyur la/ /yongs su shes pa gang yang med/ /skye ba dag ni brjod pa ste/ /de phyir zhing rnams rab tu brjod/ /zhing gi rang bzhin shes gyur pa/ /'khrug pa med pa rab tu
62b2(phal chen): shes/ /gang tshe 'jig rten zhing yin par/ /tshul bzhin du ni rtogs byed na/ /de tshe thams cad don bstan pa/ /byang chub sems dpas rab tu shes/ /de nas byang chub sems dpa' dga' ba dang ldan pas/ sangs rgyas kyi
62b3(phal chen): mthus phyogs bcur rnam par bltas te/ de'i tshe tshigs su bcad pa 'di dag smras so/ /gnas 'di shin tu rgya che ste/ /chos kyi dbyings kyis klas pa yin/ /rtag tu kun tu song ba ste/ /yid du 'ong zhing gnas kyang
62b4(phal chen): med/ /de la yang dag brtag byas shing / /rim gro yod par dad byed na/ /sdug bsngal nam yang mi mthong ste/ /ngan song rnams kyang mi mthong ngo / /tshad med de bzhin grangs med pa'i/ /'jig rten khams su su 'gro bas/
62b5(phal chen): gang rnams 'di na snang ba yin/ /sangs rgyas byin brlabs thos par 'gyur/ /drang srong chen po'i byin gyis brlabs/ /gang gis thos par gyur nas kyang / /'di 'dra sangs rgyas chos so zhes/ /rtog med bla med byang chub
62b6(phal chen): po/ /gang rnams 'das pa'i sangs rgyas kyi/ /chos nyid la ni yid ches pas/ /de kun 'jig rten sgron ma ste/ /rkang gnyis ldan pa'i dam par gyur/ /sangs rgyas rnam par 'phrul pa 'di/ /la la zhig gis thos
62b7(phal chen): gyur cing / /thos nas dad par byed gyur na/ /de dag mi yi dam par 'gyur/ /brten pa gang rnams da ltar yang / /sangs rgyas chos la dad byed pa/ /de dag don gzigs mi 'jigs pa'i/ /de bzhin gshegs par 'gyur
62b8(phal chen): ba yin/ /bskal pa bsam gyis myi khyab par/ /'di 'dra thos pa shin tu dkon/ /smon lam dbang ni ma gtogs par/ /blo gros 'di 'drar 'gyur ba myin/ /sangs rgyas dam chos 'di las kyang / /legs par bshad
63a1(phal chen): pa gzung byas shing / /gzhan la ston pa su byed pa/ /de dag bsam gyis mi khyab 'gyur/ /de la brtson 'grus bskyed byas shing / /yid la go ca bgo byas te/ /gang las sangs rgyas brjod pa yi/ /shes pa 'di 'dra
63a2(phal chen): mnyan par bya/ /de nas byang chub sems dpa' khrel dang ldan pas/ sangs rgyas kyi byin gyi brlabs kyis phyogs bcur rnam par bltas te/ de'i tshe tshigs su bcad de smras pa/ /gang zhig thos nas 'di 'dra ba'i/ /
63a3(phal chen): dga' ba yangs pa skye ba dang / /the tsom rnam par gcad pa ni/ /'jig rten na ni ngo mtshar che/ /'di ltar thams cad gzigs pa'i rnams/ /nyid kyis 'gro la bka' stsal na/ /sangs rgyas mi mkhyen gang yang med/ /
63a4(phal chen): de ltar sangs rgyas bsam mi khyab/ /mi shes pa yi rgyu las ni/ /ye shes 'jug par mi 'gyur te/ /mun pa'i mthu dang snang ba gnyis/ /lhan cig 'byung bar mi 'gyur bstan/ /ji ltar gzugs dang gzugs med pa/ /bskal
63a5(phal chen): ba mnyam pa med par bshad/ /de ltar shes dang mi shes pa/ /'grogs par shin tu mi 'gyur ro/ /'khor dang mya ngan 'das pa dag /ji ltar med las brtags pa ltar/ /de bzhin shes dang mi shes pa/ /mtshan nyid
63a6(phal chen): bzhin du dmigs pa med/ /ji ltar 'jig rten 'jigs pa dang / /'du bar 'gyur ba ring ba ste/ /phan tshun 'grogs par mi 'gyur ba/ /shes dang mi shes de bzhin no/ /ji ltar byang chub sems dpa' yi/ /thog
63a7(phal chen): ma'i sems dang tha ma'i sems/ /lhan cig myi gnas 'byung ba ltar/ /shes dang mi shes de bzhin no/ /ji ltar lus dang rnam shes pa/ /gzhan dang gzhan las 'byung 'gyur ba/ /de bzhin shes dang mi shes
63a8(phal chen): gnyis/ /'grogs par 'gyur ba nam yang med/ /ji ltar dug la phan pa'i rtsi/ /'phral du dug ni kun myin byed/ /de ltar shes pa mi shes pas/ /shin tu sel ba byed par mdzod/ /sangs rgyas bla na gang yang med/ /

65b2(phal chen): kha dog kun tu rab tu snang / /de la kha dog yod pa myin/ /sangs rgyas yon tan de bzhin no/ /ji ltar nam mkha' dri med cing / /gzugs med bstan du med yin yang / /gzugs rnams thams cad ston par byed/ /

65b6(phal chen): sems dpa' 'dus pas/ tshigs su bcad pa bstan pa'i le'u zhes bya ba ste/ nyi shu lnga pa// //sangs rgyas rmad ga gcad ces bya ba shin tu rgyas pa chen po'i mdo/ sangs rgyas rmad ga cad ces bya ba shin tu rgyas pa chen po'i mdo/ bam po drug pa/

66a1(phal chen): kyi zhing stong phrag bcu'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed 'das pa'i pha rol nas/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i mtshan yon tan dang ldan pa zhes bya ba/ sangs rgyas kyi zhing stong phrag bcu'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyis zhal bstan

66a4(phal chen): de bzhin gshegs pa rnam par snang mdzad kyi sngon gyi smon lam dang sngon gyi byin gyis brlabs dang / byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi dge ba'i rtsa bas shin tu bstan pas na 'di ltar chos bstan pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi

66a6(phal chen): nas rab tu sbyor ba dang / thams cad mkhyen pa rab tu bsgrub pa dang / chos thams cad khong du chud par bya ba dang / dbang po thams cad yongs su shes par bya ba dang / chos bstan pa thams cad yongs su gzung bar

66a8(phal chen): brlabs kyis/ chos bstan pa la spobs par gyis shig /de nas sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das de dag gis byang chub sems dpa' yon tan dang ldan pa la chags pa med pa nyid nye bar bsgrub pa mdzad do/ /
66b1(phal chen): bsgrubs pa med pa nyid nye bar bsgrub pa mdzad do/ /byin gyis brlabs pa nyid nye bar bsgrub pa mdzad do/ /slob dpon med pa nyid nye bar bsgrub pa mdzad do/ /rmongs pa med pa nyid nye bar bsgrub pa mdzad do/ /tha dad pa med
66b2(phal chen): pa nyid nye bar bsgrub pa mdzad do/ /kha na ma tho ba med pa nyid nye bar bsgrub pa mdzad do/ /tshad myed pa nyid nye bar bsgrub pa mdzad do/ /zil gyis myi non pa nyid nye bar bsgrub pa mdzad do/ /zhum pa med pa nyid nye bar
66b3(phal chen): bsgrub pa mdzad do/ /de ci'i phyir zhe na/ ting nge 'dzin 'di nyid kyi chos ny-id thob pa'i phyir ro/ /de nas sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das de dag gis/ phyag g.yas pa brkyang ste/ byang chub sems dpa' yon tan dang
66b4(phal chen): ldan pa'i mgo la byug pa mdzad do/ /sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das de dag gis de ltar reg ma thag tu/ byang chub sems dpa' yon tan dang ldan pa/ ting nge 'dzin de las langs te byang chub sems dpa' rnams
66b5(phal chen): la smras pa/ kye rgyal ba'i sras dag /byang chub sems dpa'i las ni bsam gyis mi khyab ste/ de ni 'di ltar chos kyi dbyings kyis klas so/ /nam mkha'i dbyings kyi mthar thug go/ /kye rgyal ba'i sras dag /
66b6(phal chen): de ci'i phyir zhe na/ de ni 'di ltar byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rnams ni/ 'das pa'i sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi spyod pa la yang slob bo/ /ma byon pa'i sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das
66b7(phal chen): rnams kyi spyod pa la yang slob po/ /da ltar byung ba'i sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi spyod pa la yang slob po/ /kye rgyal ba'i sras dag /byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi spyod pa gang la bsam te/
66b8(phal chen): de skad du smras pa de dag gang zhe na/ kye rgyal ba'i sras dag /bcu po 'di dag ni byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi spyod pa/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das/ 'das pa dang / ma byon pa dang / da ltar byung ba rnams
67a1(phal chen): kyis gsungs pa dang / gsung ba dang / gsung bar 'gyur ba ste/ bcu gang zhe na 'di lta ste dga' bar byed pa zhes bya ba/ byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa dang po dang / bde ba bskyed pa zhes bya ba byang chub sems dpa'i
67a2(phal chen): spyod pa gnyis pa dang / mi mthun pa med pa zhes bya ba byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa gsum pa dang / mi zad pa zhes bya ba byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa bzhi pa dang / rmongs pa med pa zhes bya ba byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa
67a3(phal chen): lnga pa dang / lta ba bzang po zhes bya ba byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa drug pa dang / gnas med pa zhes bya ba byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa bdun pa dang / thub par dka' ba zhes bya ba byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa brgyad pa dang /
67a4(phal chen): chos bzang po zhes bya ba byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa dgu pa dang / bden pa dang ldan pa zhes bya ba byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa bcu pa dag ste/ kye rgyal ba'i sras dag /bcu po de dag ni byang chub sems dpa' rnams
67a5(phal chen): kyi spyod pa/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das/ 'das pa dang / ma byon pa dang / da ltar byung ba rnams kyis gsungs pa dang / gsung ba dang / gsung bar 'gyur ba'o/ /kye rgyal ba'i sras dag /de la byang chub sems dpa'i
67a6(phal chen): spyod pa dang po dga' ba byed pa zhes bya ba gang zhe na/ kye rgyal ba'i sras dag /'di la byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sngon gyi spyod pa'i rjes su slob cing rjes su
67a7(phal chen): dran par bya ba dang / yid zhum pa med pa dang / yid dang bas kun tu 'phel bar bya ba dang / yongs su gzung ba dang / yang dag par bstan pa dang / rjes su rgya che bar byed cing / sdug bsngal ba'i sems can bde
67a8(phal chen): bar bya ba'i phyir/ sems can thams cad la bdog pa thams cad yongs su gtong ba dang / 'gyod pa med pa'i sems kyi sbyor ba dang / rnam par smyin pa la ye brngam pa med pa dang / grags pa 'dod pa med pa dang /
67b1(phal chen): gnyen 'dod pa med pa dang / khe 'dod pa med pa dang / gzhan rjes su bsrung ba dang / pha rol la phan gdags pa dang / sems can thams cad la phan gdags pa'i sems kyis/ sbyin pa'i bdag po sbyin pa byed pa dang /
67b2(phal chen): kye rgyal ba'i sras dag /'di ni byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa dang po'o/ /spyod pa de la gnas pa'i byang chub sems dpa' ni/ skye bo mang po'i yid du 'ong ba yin te/ de ni sems can dbul po gang dang gang na yod
67b3(phal chen): pa de dang der smon lam gyi dbang gis rab tu skyes ste/ skyes nas kyang zad mi shes pa'i longs spyod dang ldan zhing shin tu phyug pa yin te/ de la gal te dus gcig du/ slong ba'i srog chags bye ba khrag khrig brgya stong grangs
67b4(phal chen): med pa zhig 'ongs te/ 'di skad du kye shes par gyis shig /bdag cag thams cad ni bkres pas mchi'o/ /gal te bdag cag khyod kyi sha zos na ni 'tsho bar 'gyur ro zhes/ tshig tu smra bar gyur kyang / byang chub
67b5(phal chen): sems dpa' ni sbyin pa phun sum tshogs pa rnam pa 'di lta bu dang ldan pa/ slong ba'i srog chags bye ba khrag khrig brgya stong grangs med pa de snyed cig nye bar lhags kyang / byang chub sems dpa' la de'i phyir sems
67b6(phal chen): bskyed pa gcig kyang zhum pa'i bsam pa mi 'gyur gyi/ sems can de dag thams cad la snying rje chen po rab tu skye ste/ gzhan mang po zhig 'ongs kyang de bas ches dga' ba dang / spro ba 'byung zhing 'di ltar bdag gis
67b7(phal chen): gsol ba ma btab par/ sangs rgyas kyi chos la yang dag par spobs pa'i dge ba'i bshes gnyen sdug bsngal zhing slong ba sbyin pa'i gnas su gyur pa 'di lta bu dag dang 'grogs par gyur pa ni/ bdag gis thob pa
67b8(phal chen): legs par thob ste/ ji nas kyang sems can 'ga'i yid kyang mi nyams par bya ba de ltar bdag gis bya'o/ /bdag gis dge ba'i rtsa ba ci byas pa dang / ci byed pa dang / dge ba'i rtsa ba ci byed par 'gyur ba des
68a1(phal chen): ji tsam gyis sems can de dag thams cad 'grangs shing dus byed par 'gyur ba de tsam du che ba'i lus su gyur cig / sems can de dag 'grangs shing tshim par ma gyur gyi bar du gcad cing skye bas mi zad
68a2(phal chen): pa de tsam gyi lus su gyur cig / dge ba'i rtsa ba des kyang bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu yang dag par bsgrubs te/ phung po ma lus pa'i mya ngan las 'das pa'i khams su mya ngan las 'das par
68a3(phal chen): bya'o/ /rnam grangs 'di bzhin du ma 'ongs pa'i dus kyi 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad kyi sems can de dag thams cad las 'di 'dra ba dang ldan par gyur te/ de dag thams cad kyang bdag gi sha zos nas
68a4(phal chen): bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu yang dag par bsgrubs te/ sangs rgyas kyi chos thams cad dang mnyam pa'i ye shes kyis sangs rgyas kyi mdzad pa byas nas/ phung po'i lhag ma ma lus pa'i
68a5(phal chen): mya ngan las 'das pa'i dbyings su mya ngan las 'da' bar gyur cig / bdag nyid kyang sems can gyi bsam pa yongs su rdzogs par ma gyur gyi bar du/ bdag du 'du shes pa 'am/ sems can du 'du shes
68a6(phal chen): pa 'am/ srid par 'du shes pa 'am/ srog du 'du shes pa 'am/ so so'i skye bor 'du shes pa 'am/ gang zag du 'du shes pa'am/ shed can du 'du shes pa 'am/ shed bdag du 'du shes pa 'am/ byed
68a7(phal chen): pa por 'du shes pa 'am/ tshor ba por 'du shes pas/ gzhan du chos kyi dbyings nye bar bzung ba dang / sems can gyi khams mtha' yas pa'i chos nyid nye bar bzung ba dang / stong pa'i chos nyid nye bar
68a8(phal chen): bzung ba dang / 'dod chags dang bral ba'i chos nyid nye bar bzung ba dang / mtshan nyid med pa'i chos nyid nye bar bzung ba dang / dngos po med pa'i chos nyid nye bar bzung ba dang / gnas med pa'i chos nyid nye bar
68b1(phal chen): bzung ba dang / gzhi med pa'i chos nyid nye bar bzung ba dang / mngon par 'du bya ba med pa'i chos nyid nye bar bzung ba ma gtogs par mngon par 'tshang rgya bar gyur cig ces ste/ de ni bdag kyang yang dag par rjes su
68b2(phal chen): mi mthong / bdag gis lus kyang yang dag par rjes su mi mthong / len to zhes bya bar yang dag par rjes su mi mthong / len pa yang dag par rjes su mi mthong / sbyin pa'i gnas kyang yang dag par rjes su mi
68b3(phal chen): mthong ste/ de ni las kyang yang dag par rjes su mi mthong / rnam par smyin pa yang dag par rjes su mi mthong / 'bras bu yang dag par rjes su mi mthong / 'bras bu chen po yang dag par rjes su mi mthong /
68b4(phal chen): 'bras bu chung ngu yang dag par rjes su mi mthong ngo / /de 'das pa'i dus kyi sems can thams cad kyi lus zhig par yid la byed do/ /ma 'ongs pa dang / da ltar byung ba'i sems can thams cad kyi lus 'jig
68b5(phal chen): par yid la byed do/ /de 'di snyam du sems te/ kye ma sems can 'di dag rang gi lus grangs med pa zhig ni 'gags ste/ 'gag cing 'gag par 'gyur yang / snying po med pa'i lus las snying po mi len pa ni
68b6(phal chen): ngo mtshar che'o/ /de lta yin gyis bdag gis sems can thams cad bde bas rim gror bya ba'i phyir/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i rjes su bslab par bya'o/ /thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes kyang mngon par sangs
68b7(phal chen): rgyas te/ chos thams cad rnam par sbyang ba'i phyir/ chos nyid mi 'jig pa nye bar gzung ste/ dus gsum mnyam pa nyid du 'thun pa'i tshul gyis zhi bar byas pas sems can rnams la chos bstan par bya'o/ /
68b8(phal chen): snyam du sems ste/ kye rgyal ba'i sras dag 'di ni byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa dang po ste/ dga' bar byed pa zhes bya'o/ /kye rgyal ba'i sras dag /byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi spyod pa gnyis pa bde ba
69a1(phal chen): skyed pa zhes bya ba gang zhe na/ kye rgyal ba'i sras dag 'di la byang chub sems dpa' tshul khrims dang ldan pa yin te/ de ni mi gnas pa yin/ gzugs dang sgra dang dri dang ro dang / reg la mi gnas pa ston pa yin/
69a2(phal chen): rigs kyi bdag nyid che ba la mi gnas pa yin/ rgyud kyi bdag nyid che ba la mi gnas pa yin/ zas kyi bdag nyid che ba la mi gnas pa yin/ gzugs kyi bdag nyid che ba la mi gnas pa yin/ longs spyod kyi bdag
69a3(phal chen): nyid che ba la mi gnas pa yin te/ de ltar de ni tshul khrims las yongs su nyams pa med cing / 'di ltar kun nas 'khor ba med pa dang / kun tu btsal ba med pa dang / yongs su gdung ba med pa dang / bar chad med
69a4(phal chen): pa dang / gtse ba med pa dang / 'khrug pa med par bya'o/ /snad pa med par bya'o/ /sangs rgyas kyis sngags pa'i chos rnams yongs su gzung snyam du sems te/ kye rgyal ba'i sras dag byang chub sems dpa' de lta
69a5(phal chen): bu'i tshul khrims dang ldan pa'i drung du/ gal te nyin gcig tu bdud bye ba khrag khrig brgya stong zhig 'ongs te/ bdud re re zhing yang lha'i bu mo bye ba khrag khrig brgya stong 'dod pa'i cho ga thams cad la mkhas pa/ bde
69a6(phal chen): bar rim gror bya ba thams cad thogs pa med pa/ lus kyi rgyan gyis yongs su rgyas pa bye ba khrag khrig brgya stong re re snyed kyang / byang chub sems dpas 'dod pa ni/ bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub la
69a7(phal chen): bar du gcod pa yin par shes nas/ ston pa mngon du gyur pa'i phyir 'dod pa dang ldan pa'i sems bskyed pa gcig kyang mi 'byung ste/ byang chub sems dpa' ni thams cad mkhyen pa nyid yid la bya ba dang mi 'bral lo/ /'dod pa'i
69a8(phal chen): don du sems can 'ga' la yang sdug bsngal gyi rgyur 'gyur ba mi byed de/ chung ngu na srog gi dbang po 'gags par gyur kyang gzhan la mi dga' ba mi bskyed do/ /kye rgyal ba'i sras dag /byang chub sems dpa' rnams ni
69b1(phal chen): de bzhin gshegs pa mthong nas/ chung ngu na sems kyi rgyud gcig tsam gyis 'dod pa la mi spyod na/ gnyis kyis gnyis sbyar ba lta smos kyang ci dgos ste 'di ni gnas med do/ /byang chub sems dpa' ni 'di ltar sems skye ste/
69b2(phal chen): sems can 'di dag ni yun ring po nas de ltar gzhol ba dang / de ltar 'bab pa/ de ltar bab pa/ de ltar mos pa/ de lta bu'i spyod yul can/ de ltar nges pa/ de ltar bying ba/ de ltar non pa/ de ltar chags pa/ de ltar zhugs pa
69b3(phal chen): yin gyis/ bdag gis ni bdud 'di dag dang / bdud kyi bu mo 'di dag dang / sems can thams cad ci nas kyang bla na med pa'i tshul khrims yongs su dag pa la bkod de/ thams cad mkhyen pa las phyir mi ldog par
69b4(phal chen): byas nas/ bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu mngon par 'tshang rgya bar byas ste/ phung po lhag ma ma lus pa'i mya ngan las 'das pa'i dbyings su yongs su mya ngan las 'da' bar 'gyur ba de ltar bya'o/ /
69b5(phal chen): de ci'i phyir zhe na/ 'di ltar sangs rgyas thams cad kyi rjes su bslabs te/ mi bya ba thams cad yongs su spang ba dang / lus kyis mi shes pa thams cad yongs su spang ba ma yin pa dang / sems kyis kyang
69b6(phal chen): ma yin pa de ni bdag cag gi las yin gyis/ kye rgyal ba'i sras dag bdag cag gis sangs rgyas kyi chos thams cad kyi rjes su song ba'i ye shes kyis sems can thams cad kyi phyin ci log rab tu spang ba'i phyir
69b7(phal chen): chos bstan par bya'o/ /phyin ci log ni sems can rnams las gzhan na'ang med de/ phyin ci log rnams las kyang sems can rnams gud na med do/ /phyin ci log tu yang sems can 'dus pa ma yin/
69b8(phal chen): sems can du yang phyi ci log 'dus pa ma yin no/ /phyin ci log rnams kyang sems can ma yin/ sems can rnams kyang phyin ci log ma yin no/ /phyin ci log rnams ni nang na yang med/ phyin ci log
70a1(phal chen): rnams ni phyi rol na yang med do/ /sems can rnams kyang nang na yang med/ sems can rnams ni phyi rol na yang med de/ chos de dag thams cad gsog gsob brdzun pa bslu ba'i chos can te/ sgyu ma lta bu
70a2(phal chen): byis pa bslu ba dang / ngan pa chung ba snying po med pa dang / rmi lam lta bu mig yor lta bu ste/ de dag khong du chud par bya ba'i phyir 'du byed rjes su rtogs pa'o/ /'du byed rjes su rtogs pa'i phyir mya ngan las 'das
70a3(phal chen): pa ste/ de ni sangs rgyas kyi byang chub tu rnam par 'tshang rgya bar byed de/ rgal bas ni sgrol bar byed/ grol bas ni 'grol bar byed/ zhi bas ni zhi bar byed/ dbugs phyin pas ni dbugs 'byin par byed/
70a4(phal chen): bkrus pas ni 'khru bar byed/ dag pas ni dag par byed/ mya ngan las 'das pas ni mya ngan las 'da' bar byed/ bde bar gyur pas ni bde bar byed pa ste/ bdag cag gis de bzhin gshegs pa dang
70a5(phal chen): bskal ba mi mthun par gnas par mi bya ste/ bdag cag gis ni 'jig rten gyi spyod pa thams cad spang bar bya'o/ /bdag cag gis ni sangs rgyas kyi chos thams cad dang ldan par bya'o/ /bdag cag gis
70a6(phal chen): ni bla na med pa'i chos nyid la gnas par bya'o/ /bdag gis ni sems can thams cad la sems mnyam pas yang dag par 'jug par bya'o/ /bdag cag gis ni yul thams cad yongs su shes pa dang ldan par bya'o/ /
70a7(phal chen): bdag cag gis ni yongs su spyod pa kha na ma tho ba med pa'i bag chags dang ldan par bya'o/ /bdag cag gis ni rtogs pa thams cad dang ldan par bya'o/ /bdag cag gis ni 'byung ba thams cad la mkhas pa dang
70a8(phal chen): ldan par bya'o/ /bdag cag g-is ni bla na med pa'i ye shes kun tu mtha' yas pa brjod du med pa/ mi gnas pa/ 'phos pa med pa/ mtha' dang dbus med pa/ mi zad pa gzugs med pa/ bstan du

70b3(phal chen): dang ldan zhing mngon par smra ba'i ngang tshul can te/ de yang bdag la gnod par ma yin/ pha rol la gnod par ma yin/ gnyis ka la gnod par ma yin/ bdag bsdu bar ma yin/ gzhan bsdu bar
70b4(phal chen): ma yin/ gnyis ka bsdu bar ma yin/ bdag yongs su gzung bar ma yin/ gzhan yongs su gzung bar ma yin/ gnyis ka yongs su gzung bar ma yin/ yang dag par blangs pa grags pa'i
70b5(phal chen): phyir ma yin gyi/ byang chub sems dpa' ni sems 'di ltar skye ste/ bdag cag gis sems can la mi dge ba thams cad spang ba'i phyir chos bstan par bya'o/ /'dod chags spang ba dang / zhe sdang spang
70b6(phal chen): ba dang / gti mug spang ba dang / nga rgyal spang ba dang / 'chab pa spang ba dang / phrag dog spang ba dang / ser sna spang ba dang / g.yo dang sgyu spang ba dang / bzod pa dang nges pa la gzhag pa'i phyir/ bdag cag gis
70b7(phal chen): sems can thams cad la chos bstan par bya'o/ /zhes te kye rgyal ba'i sras dag byang chub sems dpa' ni de lta bur bzod cing nges pa dang ldan pa yin pas/ de la gal te srog chags brgya stong bye
70b8(phal chen): ba grangs med pa zhig 'ongs la srog chags de dag re re zhing yang kha bye ba khrag khrig brgya stong grangs med par sprul te/ drung du phyin pa kha re re nas kyang mi snyan par brjod pa bye ba khrag khrig brgya stong grangs
71a1(phal chen): med pas mi snyan cing yid du mi 'ong ba dang / mi 'dod pa dang / mi sdug pa dang / mi dga' ba dang / mi tshul ba dang / 'phags pa ma yin pa dang / 'phags pa ma yin pas brjod pa dang / 'phags pa ma

71a3(phal chen): gcig tu ji ltar de bzhin du bskal pa grangs med par yang mtshams med cing ngal mi shes/ skyo mi shes/ rgyun mi 'chad/ gtong ba med/ sdod pa med/ gtsugs su med/ dbugs 'byin pa med/ phyir

71a8(phal chen): de bzhin no zhes nas/ phyir zhing sems dang bar byed/ rab tu dang bar byed/ dga' bar byed/ rab tu dga' bar byed/ tshim par byed/ gzeng mtho' bar byed/ spro bar byed/ rab tu spro bar byed/

71b2(phal chen): lus 'di ni bdag dang bdag gis stong pa/ rang bzhin gyis stong pa ste stong pa nyid la bde ba 'am/ sdug bsngal ba 'am/ gnyis su brjod pa gang yang med do/ /gang stong pa de la ci yang med de/ chos thams cad

71b4(phal chen): 'di la byams pa'i sems dang / phan pa'i sems dang / bde ba'i sems dang / snying rje ba'i sems dang / snying brtse ba'i sems dang / phan par dga' ba'i sems dang / yongs su mi gtong ba'i sems dang /

77b4(phal chen): rnams la gnas mi skyed pa yin/ dpe byad bzang po rnams la gnas mi skyed pa yin/ sangs rgyas kyi 'od la gnas mi skyed pa yin/ sangs rgyas kyi chos bstan pa la gnas mi skyed pa yin/ phyogs la gnas mi skyed

78a3(phal chen): yang med/ rnam par phye ba yang med/ rnam pa tha dad pa yang med/ rnam par rtog pa yang med/ gzhan du 'gyur ba yang med/ bde ba yang med/ mi bde ba yang med/ lam yang med/ lam ma yin pa yang med de/ byang chub

78a6(phal chen): brjod de/ tshig gi lam la gnas par mi byed do/ /sems can gyi rgyud la yang 'jug ste/ sems can gyi rgyud la yang gnas par mi byed do/ /ting nge 'dzin kyang rab tu shes shing de dag la yang mnyam par gzhog ste/

78b5(phal chen): po med pas 'jigs pa/ rigs pas spangs pa/ tshul bzhin ma yin pa la zhugs pa/ mnyam pa nyid las log par lhung ba/ g.yang sa chen por rab tu lhung ba/ bdud kyi bsam pa la zhugs pa/ sangs rgyas
78b6(phal chen): kyi bsam pa las ring du gyur pa/ srid pa la mngon par chags pa sha stag go/ /zhes de ltar byang chub sems dpa' sems can gyi khams la 'jug cing snying rje chen po de bas kyang cher bskyed nas snying rje chen po rgya cher
78b7(phal chen): byas te/ gnas med pa'i dge ba'i rtsa ba yang dag par bstsags nas/ 'di snyam du sems bskyed do/ /gal te sems can re re'i phyir yul re re dang / phyogs re rer yang bskal pa brjod du med par sems can re re
78b8(phal chen): 'dul ba'i phyir 'dug la/ sems can gcig la ji lta ba de bzhin du sems can gyi khams thams cad kyi don du 'dug kyang bdag gis de'i phyir mi dga' ba mi bskyed de/ yul de dang phyogs de nas kyang bdag
79a1(phal chen): gud du g.yo bar mi bya'o/ /gud du 'gro bar mi bya'o/ /skra'i rtse mo tsam la chos kyi dbyings thams cad 'dus par byas te/ skra'i rtse mo'i tshul de lta bus skra'i rtse mor chud pa re re yang sems can gyi khams yongs su

82b3(phal chen): du mi rung bas yongs su gang ba dang / byis pas yongs su gang ba dang / ma dad pas yongs su gang ba dang / gzhan gyi dring la rgyug pas yongs su gang ba dang / shes rab dman pas shin tu byung ba dang / 'jig rten

82b5(phal chen): rten gnas pa drin du gzo bas yongs su gang ba dang / mdza' bos yongs su gang ba dang / mkhas pas yongs su gang ba dang / byang chub sems dpa'i spyad pa spyod pa lta ba ngo mtshar du yang ci che ste/ de ji lta zhe na/
82b6(phal chen): bdag ni sems can mdza' ba 'am/ mi mdza' ba gang las kyang chung ngu na skra'i rtse mo gcig tsam 'am/ chung ngu na dge bar bya ba sbyin pa tsam yang mi 'dod mi tshol te/ phyi ma'i mtha'i mur thug pa'i bskal par
82b7(phal chen): byang chub sems dpa'i spyad pa spyod kyang / gzhan du na sems can de dag yongs su 'grol ba dang / sems can de dag yongs su dad par 'gyur ba dang / sems can de dag 'byung bar 'gyur ba ma gtogs
82b8(phal chen): par de dag las sems skad cig tsam du bde bar 'gyur ba yang mi tshol lo/ /de ci'i phyir zhe na/ bdag ni sems can la len pa med cing / thams cad la 'dod pa med pas/ sems can gyi gtso bor
83a1(phal chen): 'gyur bar byed pa ste/ 'di ltar bdag gis kyang sems can de dag bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub kyi mthas gtugs te/ shin tu bde ba'i pha rol tu phyin par 'gyur bar nan tan du bya'o snyam mo/ /

83a3(phal chen): byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa dgu pa chos bzang po zhes bya ba gang zhe na/ kye rgyal ba'i sras dag 'di la byang chub sems dpa' lha dang 'jig rten du bcas pa/ bdud du bcas pa/ tshangs par bcas pa/ dge
83a4(phal chen): sbyongs dang bram zer bcas pa'i skye dgu lha dang dri za dang / mi dang lha ma yin du bcas pa ni/ chos kyi mu stegs bzang por gyur pa yin te/ de sangs rgyas kyi rigs mi gcad pa'i phyir dam pa'i chos yongs su 'dzin
83a5(phal chen): par byed pa yin/ gzungs kyi snang ba rnam par dag pa thob pas/ gtam bya ba dang / lung bstan pa la spobs pa yin/ chos dang ldan pa'i gzungs thob pas don la spobs pa yin/ chos ji lta ba bzhin du
83a6(phal chen): gzungs yang dag par bskul ba thob pas/ chos la spobs pa yin/ tshig dang smra ba thams cad kyi gzungs rab tu thob pas nges pa'i tshig la spobs pa yin/ tshig dang yi ge'i don kun tu mtha' yas shing
83a7(phal chen): zad mi shes pa la thogs pa med pa'i sgo'i gzungs thob pas spobs pa dang ldan pa yin/ sangs rgyas dbang bskur ba'i gzungs kyi dbang bskur bas mngon par dga' bar byed pa'i spobs pa dang ldan pa yin/ gzhan
83a8(phal chen): gyi dring la mi 'jog pa'i gzungs kyi sgo thob pas snang ba thob pa'i spobs pa dang ldan pa yin/ spobs pa thun mong ba'i tshul la zhugs pas thun mong gi spobs pa dang ldan pa yin te/ don mang po dang tshig mang po dang /
83b1(phal chen): yi ge mang po de dag /de dag la nges pa'i tshig gi gzungs kyi sgor tshud pas nges pa'i spobs pa dang ldan pa yin/ rgyud mtha' yas pa'i gzungs thob pas mtha' yas pa'i spobs pa dang ldan pa yin te/ des ni stong gsum

83b4(phal chen): dang / snying rje chen po 'gal ba med pas shin tu bstan pa dang / tshig gcig gi sgra brjod pas 'dul ba ji lta ba bzhin du tshim par 'gyur zhing / mtha' yas par snang bas ston pas/ sangs rgyas kyi mdzad pa la spyod do/ /

83b6(phal chen): brgya stong bsam gyis mi khyab pa grangs med pa rnam par phye ba/ rnam pa tha dad pa brjod du med pa dang ldan pa/ de lta bu'i sems can sha stag byang chub sems dpa'i 'khor du gyur la/ 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor yang
83b7(phal chen): 'jig rten gyi khams brjod du med pa tsam du yangs pa zhig yin te/ 'dul ba brjod du med pa zhig 'dus nas/ sems can re re la yang kha'i sgo bye ba khrag khrig brgya stong grangs med pa brjod du med pa yod par
83b8(phal chen): gyur te/ sems can gcig ji lta bar sems can de dag thams cad kyang de bzhin du de snyed du kha'i sgo dang ldan pa/ sems can de dag thams cad kyis byang chub sems dpa' la skad du brjod pa/

84a6(phal chen): 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor de dag byung bas/ phyi ma'i mtha'i bskal pa'i mur thug pa zad par gyur te/ 'khor de rnams ni zad mi shes par 'byung la skye ba'i rgyun mi 'chad pa zhig yod du zin na yang bstan par bya ba'i

84b1(phal chen): tshig gi lam gyis yongs su mgu bar byas te/ chos bshad pa'i mthar thug par mi bya/ chos la rnam par thogs par mi bya'o zhes nas/ des brjod pa de dag thams cad kyang rab tu shes te/ sems can de dag la

87b7(phal chen): mngon par bab bo/ /lha rdzas kyi phreng ba'i sprin gyi char yang mngon par bab bo/ /lha rdzas kyi gos kyi sprin gyi char yang mngon par bab bo/ /lha rdzas kyi rin po che'i sprin gyi char yang mngon par bab bo/ /lha rdzas kyi rgyan gyi
87b8(phal chen): sprin gyi char yang mngon par bab bo/ /lha rdzas kyi rol mo'i sgra yang mngon par byung ngo / /lha rdzas kyi snang ba yang rab tu byung ngo / /lha rdzas kyi sgra yang rab tu byung ngo / /gling bzhi pa 'di'i lha'i dbang po rab mtshe ma'i
88a1(phal chen): gnas na/ ji lta ba de bzhin du phyogs bcu thams cad kyang rgyas par byas te/ thams cad na yang sangs rgyas kyi mthus chos nyid bstan par snang ngo / /phyogs bcu'i 'jig rten gyi khams sangs rgyas kyi zhing brgya
88a2(phal chen): stong gi rdul shin tu phra ba snyed de 'das pa'i pha rol nas/ byang chub sems dpa' sangs rgyas kyi zhing brgya stong gi rdul shin tu phra ba snyed 'ongs te/ phyogs bcu rgyas par byas nas 'di skad ces smras so/ /kye rgyal ba'i
88a3(phal chen): sras/ de ltar khyod byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi spyod pa'i chos nyid 'di ston pa legs so legs so/ /kye rgyal ba'i sras/ bdag cag kun kyang ming yon tan dang ldan pa zhes bya ba dag ste/ de bzhin gshegs
88a4(phal chen): pa'i mtshan kun tu yon tan zhes bya ba dag gi drung nas 'jig rten gyi khams yon tan rgyal mtshan zhes bya ba dag nas phyin te/ thams cad na'ang sangs rgyas kyi mthus 'khor 'di 'dra ba dag na tshig 'di dag dang /
88a5(phal chen): yi ge 'di dag dang / bstan pa 'di dag dang / don 'di nyid brjod pas lhag chad med par chos bstan pa 'di ston to/ /kye rgyal ba'i sras/ de ltar bdag cag thams cad kyang sangs rgyas kyi byin gyis brlabs kyis 'khor
88a6(phal chen): ' dir bdag cag phyin pa de bzhin du phyogs bcu'i 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad kyi gling gzhi pa'i 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad rab mtshe ma'i gnas lha'i rgyal po rab mtshe ma'i khang pa nor bu sna tshogs shes bya ba
88a7(phal chen): kun tu yang / byang chub sems dpa' sangs rgyas kyi zhing brgya stong gi rdul shin tu phra ba snyed phyin par gyur to/ /sangs rgyas rmad ga cad ces bya ba shin tu rgyas pa chen po'i mdo/
88a8(phal chen): bam po brgyad pa/ de nas byang chub sems dpa' yon tan dang ldan pas phyogs bcur bltas te/ 'khor yod pa thams cad la rnam par bltas nas/ chos kyi dbyings la rnam par blta zhing / de bzhin
88b1(phal chen): gshegs pa'i rigs yang dag par gzung ba dang / byang chub sems dpa'i rigs yongs su spyod pa dang / smon lam gyi rigs phyir mi ldog par bya ba dang / spyod pa'i rigs rgyun tu bsab pa dang / dus gsum gi rgyud
88b2(phal chen): mnyam par bya ba dang / 'das pa dang / ma byon pa dang / da ltar byung ba'i sangs rgyas thams cad kyi rigs yang dag par gzung ba dang / dge ba'i rtsa ba ji ltar bskyed pa'i rgyud brjod pa dang / dus dang ji ltar 'byor
88b3(phal chen): pa'i yan lag dang dbang po dang / bsam pa dang mos pa dang / nyon mongs pa dang / bag chags dang / sems dang spyod pa dang / rnam par g.yos pa'i rgyud thams cad yongs su brtag pa dang / sangs rgyas dang

88b5(phal chen): pa rdul rnams sbyangs gyur pa/ /kun tu mtha' yas spyod yul can/ /stobs bcu mnga' ba de la phyag 'tshal lo/ /gang yang rgyal ba mi yi mchog /chags pa mi mnga' yon tan tshad med mnga' ba ste/ /'das dus mnyam

88b8(phal chen): du med pa yin/ /rang byung gti mug rnam par stsal ba ji snyed pa/ /thams cad chos nyid mnyam pa ste/ /stobs mnga' de dag spyod pa 'di yin no/ /gang rnams mtha' dbus med pa yi/ /'jig rten khams kyi srid
89a1(phal chen): pa'i rgyud rnams rab gzigs shing / /gzigs nas rtog pa mi mnga' ba/ /mi g.yo de dag spyod pa 'di yin no/ /gang rnams chos kyi dbyings mkhyen cing / /rnam dag don gyi dam pa gzigs pa brten pa rnams/ /
89a2(phal chen): gti mug tha ba nga rgyal sel mdzad pa/ /legs mnga' de dag spyod pa 'di yin no/ /gang rnams sems can kun mkhas shing / /chos kyi dbyings la ngo bo nyid kyis zhugs gyur pa'i/ /bde gshegs gzhan dring mi
89a3(phal chen): 'jog pa/ /mkha' mnyam de dag spyod pa 'di yin no/ /'jig rten kun tu mtha' yas pa/ /nam mkha' klas pa yang dag thugs su chud gyur te/ /zil gyis mi non chos mnga' ba/ /thub mchog de dag spyod pa 'di

89a6(phal chen): bar mdzad pa yin/ /gang zhig phyogs bcu'i zhing gi rnams/ /khrag khrig bsam gyis mi khyab thams cad skyod byed kyang / /'jig par 'gyur bar mi byed de/ /'jig rten phan pa bskyed la rtag tu brtson/ /tshig

89a8(phal chen): rnam par dbye ba'i pha rol phyin pa'i rnams/ /mi zad sa la zhugs pa'i dag /pham med blo gros de dag spyod 'di'o/ /yon tan khrag khrig tshad med pa/ /byang chub rab la gzhol zhing spyad pa spyod pa dag /yon tan
89b1(phal chen): thams cad mthar phyin pa/ /legs pa mi zad de dag spyod 'di'o/ /'jig rten 'das pa sgrub pa rnams/ /smra ba'i dam pa smra ba'i seng ger gyur pa dag /'gro ba dag bya'i mthar phyin pa/ /rnam dag sems ldan de dag

89b6(phal chen): rnams/ /dpal gyi tshul can de dag spyod 'di'o/ /bde bar gshegs pa'i zhing gcig tu/ /bsam gyis mi khyab pa yi dus rnams chud byed cing / /bskal pa grangs su 'dzud byed pa/ /skyo med brtson pa de dag
89b7(phal chen): spyod 'di'o/ /tha dad mtshan can mi yi dbang / /skra yi rtse mo gcig la sangs rgyas brjod yas pa/ /gang gis de dag mthong gyur rnams/ /spyod pa bzang ldan de dag spyod 'di'o/ /gang gis skra yi cha tsam la/ /brjod
89b8(phal chen): du med pa'i 'dren pa rnams ni mthong gyur cing / /de bzhin chos dbyings thams cad de/ /rgyal sras de dag spyod pa 'di yin no/ /bskal pa brjod du med pa rnams/ /sems bskyed cig gis rab tu shes par gyur pa rnams/ /
90a1(phal chen): ring dang thung bar nges med pa/ /rnam thar spyod pa de dag spyod 'di'o/ /lta zhing don med mi 'gyur la/ /sangs rgyas spyod pa dag la don yod las ldan rnams/ /chags pa med pa'i yid can dag /rgyal ba dam pa

93a7(phal chen): kyis rgol ba'i lam la 'jigs med spyod pa dang / /mtha' yas blo yi spyod pa dang / /sangs rgyas byang chub rjes su zhugs pa rnams/ /mtha' dbus med pa zhing gi rnams/ /thams cad kun tu snang ba cig gis gsal bar

93b3(phal chen): kun tu mtha' yas shing / /yon tan mchog rnams thams cad mtha' yas pa'i/ /yon tan kun ni brjod byas te/ /thub pas bskal par gsungs kyang zad mi 'gyur/ /rang rgyal rnams dang nyan thos la/ /

103b1(phal chen): 'du shes kyang med de/ kye rgyal ba'i sras dag /'di ni byang chub sems dpa'i gtong ba'i gter drug pa'o/ /kye rgyal ba'i sras dag /de la byang chub sems dpa'i ye shes gyi gter gang zhe na/ 'di la byang chub sems dpa'
103b2(phal chen): gzugs rab tu shes so/ /gzugs kun 'byung ba rab tu shes so/ /gzugs kyi 'gog pa rab tu shes so/ /gzugs 'gog par 'gro ba'i lam yang dag par ji lta ba bzhin du rab tu shes so/ /de bzhin du tshor ba dang /
103b3(phal chen): 'du shes dang / 'du byed dang / rnam par shes pa yang dag pa ji lta ba bzhin du rab tu shes so/ /rnam par shes pa'i kun tu 'byung ba yang dag pa ji lta ba bzhin du rab tu shes so/ /rnam par shes pa 'gog pa yang dag pa ji
103b4(phal chen): lta ba bzhin du rab tu shes so/ /rnam par shes pa 'gog par 'gro ba'i lam yang dag pa ji lta ba bzhin du rab tu shes so/ /ma rig pa rab tu shes so/ /ma rig pa kun 'byung ba rab tu shes so/ /ma rig pa 'gog pa yang dag
103b5(phal chen): pa ji lta ba bzhin du rab tu shes so/ /ma rig pa 'gog par 'gro ba'i lam yang dag pa ji lta ba bzhin du rab tu shes so/ /sred pa rab tu shes so/ /sred pa kun 'byung ba rab tu shes so/ /sred pa 'gog pa rab tu shes so/ /
103b6(phal chen): sred pa 'gog par 'gro ba'i lam yang dag pa ji lta ba bzhin du rab tu shes so/ /nyan thos rab tu shes so/ /nyan thos kyi chos rab tu shes so/ /nyan thos kyi kun 'byung ba rab tu shes so/ /nyan thos kyi mya ngan
103b7(phal chen): las 'da' ba yang dag pa ji lta ba bzhin du rab tu shes so/ /rang sangs rgyas rab tu shes so/ /rang sangs rgyas kyi chos rab tu shes so/ /rang sangs rgyas kun 'byung ba rab tu shes so/ /rang sangs rgyas kyi yongs su
103b8(phal chen): mya ngan las 'da' ba yang dag pa ji lta ba bzhin du rab tu shes so/ /byang chub sems dpa' rab tu shes so/ /byang chub sems dpa'i chos rab tu shes so/ /byang chub sems dpa'i kun 'byung ba rab tu shes so/ /
104a1(phal chen): byang chub sems dpa' yongs su mya ngan las 'da' ba yang dag pa ji lta ba bzhin du rab tu shes so/ /ji ltar shes she na las dang las kyi rnam par smin pa dang bya ba dang / mngon par 'du byed pa dang / gsob dang /
104a2(phal chen): gsog dang / snying po med pa dang / bdag med par rab tu shes te/ chos gang yang snying po can du shes pa med do/ /chos gang la yang rang bzhin du 'dogs pa med de/ ngo bo ny-id mthas gtugs pa thams cad rab tu shes so/ /
104a3(phal chen): sems can rnams la yang de bzhin nyid kyi don du chos ston te de ci ston ce na/ 'jig pa med pa'i phyir chos ston te/ gang 'jig pa med pa'i phyir zhe na/ gzugs 'jig pa med pa'i phyir/ tshor ba 'jig pa med
104a4(phal chen): pa'i phyir/ 'du shes 'jig pa med pa'i phyir/ 'du byed 'jig pa med pa'i phyir/ rnam par shes pa 'jig pa med pa'i phyir chos ston to/ /ma rig pa 'jig pa med pa'i phyir/ nyan thos kyi chos dang / rang sangs
104a5(phal chen): rgyas kyi chos dang / byang chub sems dpa'i chos 'jig pa med pa'i phyir chos ston to/ /de ci'i phyir zhe na/ chos 'di ma skyes pa'i 'du ma byas pa/ byed pa po med pa/ brtsod pa med pa/ gnas med pa/ ma skyes pa/
104a6(phal chen): mi 'byung ba/ ma blangs pa/ nye bar ma blangs pa/ byed pa med pa ste/ de shes rab kyi gter de lta bu dang ldan pa las gron chungus chos thams cad la mkhas pa/ gzhan gyi dring mi 'jog pa/ yang dag pa ji lta ba
104a7(phal chen): bzhin du rab tu shes so/ /shes rab kyi gter te yang mi zad pa yin te/ de yang shin tu bstan pa bcus mi zad pa yin no/ /bcu gang zhe na/ thos pa la mkhas pas mi zad do/ /dge ba'i bshes gnyen
104a8(phal chen): la bsnyen pas mi zad do/ /tshig rab tu dbye ba la mkhas pas mi zad do/ /chos kyi dbyings la 'jug pa mngon par sgrub pa mi zad do/ /rgyan gcig pa'i ye shes kyi rjes su zhugs pas mi zad do/ /bsod nams
104b1(phal chen): thams cad shin tu bstsags pas mi zad do/ /skyo ba med par mngon par bsgrubs pas mi zad do/ /gzungs thams cad kyi sgor zhugs pas mi zad do/ /sems can thams cad kyi skad dang sgra dang brjod pa sna tshogs kyi phyir
104b2(phal chen): mi zad do/ /'gro ba thams cad kyi yid gnyis dang / nem nur dang the tsom yang dag par gcod pa'i phyir mi zad do/ /sangs rgyas kyi rnam par 'phrul pa thams cad yongs su bstan pas/ sems can thams cad
104b3(phal chen): nye bar 'tsho ba dang / yongs su smyin par bya ba dang / gdul ba'i spyod pa shin tu rtogs pa'i phyir mi zad pa de/ mi zad pa shin tu bstan pa bcu po de dag gis shes rab kyi gter te mi zad pa yin no/ /
104b4(phal chen): kye rgyal ba'i sras dag /'di ni byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi shes rab kyi gter yin te/ de la gnas pa'i byang chub sems dpa' rnams shes rab dang ye shes bla na med pa rnam par 'tshang rgya'o/ /
104b5(phal chen): kye rgyal ba'i sras dag /de la byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi dran pa'i gter gang zhe na/ kye rgyal ba'i sras dag /'di la byang chub sems dpa' dran pa dang ldan pa yin te/ de yang rgyud
104b6(phal chen): rmongs pa med pa'i dran pas sngon gyi gnas su dran te/ 'di ltar tshe gcig gi gnas kyang rjes su dran no/ /gnyis dang / gsum dang / bzhi dang / lnga dang / tshe brgya dang stong dang / tshe brgya phrag du ma dang /
104b7(phal chen): tshe stong phrag du ma dang / tshe brgya stong phrag du ma dang / 'jig pa'i bskal pa 'am/ 'du ba'i bskal pa 'am/ 'jig pa dang 'du ba'i bskal pa 'am/ 'jig pa'i bskal pa du ma dang / 'du ba'i bskal pa du ma dang /
104b8(phal chen): 'du ba dang / 'jig pa'i bskal pa du ma dang / bskal pa brgya dang / bskal pa stong dang / bskal pa brgya stong dang / bskal pa bye ba khrag khrig tshad med pa dang / bskal pa bye ba khrag khrig
105a1(phal chen): brgya stong grangs med pa bsam gyis mi khyab pa/ mtshungs pa med pa/ kun tu mtha' yas pa/ mu med pa/ sa mtshams med pa/ gzhal du med pa/ brjod du med pa/ gnyis dang / gsum dang /
105a2(phal chen): bzhi dang / lnga dang / gzhung de bzhin du brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa dang / sangs rgyas skye bar lung bstan pa shin tu brjod pa gcig dang / gnyis dang / gsum dang / bzhi dang / lnga nas/ sangs rgyas skye
105a3(phal chen): bar lung bstan pa shin tu brjod pa brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa dang / sangs rgyas skye ba cig bstan te/ de dang mtshams sbyor ba'i lung bstan pa gcig dang / gnyis dang / gsum dang / bzhi dang / lnga nas/
105a4(phal chen): sangs rgyas skye ba shin tu bstan te/ de dang mtshams sbyor ba lung bstan pa brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa dang / mdo sde gcig dang / gnyis dang / gsum dang / bzhi dang / lnga nas/ brjod du med pa'i yang
105a5(phal chen): brjod du med pa'i bar dang / dbyangs kyis bsnyad pa'i sde dang / lung bstan pa'i sde dang / tshigs su bcad pa'i sde dang / gleng gzhi'i sde dang / ched du brjod pa'i sde dang / 'di ltar 'das pa'i sde dang / skyes pa
105a6(phal chen): rabs kyi sde dang / shin tu rgyas pa'i sde dang / chos rmad du byung ba bstan pa'i sde dang / man ngag bstan pa'i sde gcig dang / gnyis dang / gsum dang / bzhi dang / lnga nas/ brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med
105a7(phal chen): pa'i bar dang / 'khor 'dus pa gcig dang / chos kyi mtshams sbyar ba gcig nas/ chos kyi mtshams sbyar ba brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa'i bar dang / dbang po sna tshogs gcig nas dbang po sna tshogs brjod
105a8(phal chen): du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa'i bar dang / dbang po rnam pa tha dad pa sna tshogs gcig nas/ dbang po tha dad pa sna tshogs brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa'i bar dang / nyon mongs pa sna tshogs gcig nas nyon mongs
105b1(phal chen): pa brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa'i bar dang / ting nge 'dzin sna tshogs gcig nas/ ting nge 'dzin sna tshogs brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa'i bar dag kyang dran pa dag dang / dang ba rnyog pa med pa dang / rnam par
105b2(phal chen): gsal ba rdul med pa/ rdul dang bral ba/ dri ma med pa/ 'od gsal ba/ sang sang po/ sgrib pa med pas rjes su dran no/ /byang chub sems dpa'i dran pa de ni 'jig rten gyi 'khrug pas mi 'phrogs pa yin/
105b3(phal chen): phas kyi rgol ba thams cad kyis nye bar nyon mongs par mi nus pa yin/ sngon gyi dge ba'i rtsa bas shin tu sbyangs pa yin/ 'jig rten gyi chos thams cad kyis ma gos pa yin/ bdud dang mu stegs can dmigs
105b4(phal chen): pa la gnas pa gzhan gyis mi chod pa yin/ tshe rabs kun tu 'pho ba'i lus shin tu bstan pa thams cad kyis brjod par mi nus pa yin/ sngon gyi mtha' dang / phyi ma'i mtha' dang / da ltar byung ba'i mthas
105b5(phal chen): rnam par mi chod pa yin/ 'jig rten gyi khams su skye ba dang / gnas pa thams cad kyis skyon du ma gyur pa yin/ sangs rgyas skyes pa'i 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor du 'jug pa shin tu bstan pa thams cad kyis
105b6(phal chen): thogs pa med pa yin/ sangs rgyas kyi chos thams cad kyi rjes su song ba yin te/ kye rgyal ba'i sras dag /'di ni byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi dran pa'i gter te brgyad pa'o/ /kye rgyal ba'i sras
105b7(phal chen): dag / de la byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi rtogs pa'i gter gang zhe na/ kye rgyal ba'i sras dag /'di la byang chub sems dpa' rtogs pa dang ldan pa yin te/ de yang yi ge de bzhin gzhan ma
105b8(phal chen): yin pas/ mdo'i tshul gyi chos ston to/ /de ni tshe'i rgyud gcig pa yang yongs su 'dzin te/ /tshe'i rgyud brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa'i bar du yongs su 'dzin to/ /sangs rgyas kyi
106a1(phal chen): mtshan gcig kyang yongs su 'dzin to/ /sangs rgyas kyi mtshan brjod du med pa yang brjod du med pa'i bar du yang yongs su 'dzin to/ /bskal pa grangs med pa bstan pa gcig kyang yongs su 'dzin to/ /bskal
106a2(phal chen): pa grangs med pa bstan pa brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa'i bar du yang yongs su 'dzin to/ /de bzhin gshegs par lung bstan pa brjod pa gcig kyang yongs su bstan to/ /de bzhin gshegs par lung bstan
106a3(phal chen): par brjod pa brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa'i bar du yang yongs su 'dzin to/ /mdo gcig kyang yongs su 'dzin to/ /mdo brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa'i bar du yang yongs su 'dzin to/ /'dus pa gcig kyang
106a4(phal chen): yongs su 'dzin to/ /'dus pa brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa'i bar du yang yongs su 'dzin to/ /chos kyi mtshams sbyar ba gcig kyang yongs su 'dzin to/ /chos kyi mtshams sbyar ba brjod du med pa'i yang
106a5(phal chen): brjod du med pa'i bar du yang yongs su 'dzin to/ /dbang po rnam pa tha dad pa sna tshogs gcig kyang yongs su 'dzin to/ /dbang po rnam pa tha dad pa sna tshogs brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa'-i bar du yang yongs su
106a6(phal chen): 'dzin to/ /nyon mongs pa sna tshogs gcig kyang yongs su 'dzin to/ /nyon mongs pa sna tshogs brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa'i bar du yang yongs su 'dzin to/ /ting nge 'dzin sna tshogs gcig kyang
106a7(phal chen): yongs su 'dzin to/ /ting nge 'dzin sna tshogs brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa'i bar du yang yongs su 'dzin to/ /kye rgyal ba'i sras dag /'di ni byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po
106a8(phal chen): rnams kyi rtogs pa'i gter te mi zad pa/ kun tu mtha' yas pa dgang dka' ba/ gting rnyed par dka' ba/ mi 'phrogs pa thub pa med pa/ bdag nyid che ba'i sangs rgyas kyi yul gyi rjes su
106b1(phal chen): song ba ste/ 'di ni gter dgu pa'o/ /kye rgyal ba'i sras dag /de la byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi blo gros kyi gter gang zhe na/ kye rgyal ba'i sras dag /'di la byang chub sems dpa' yang dag
106b2(phal chen): par rtogs par byed pa'i rtog pa dang ldan zhing blo gros dang ldan pa yin te/ mdo sde thams cad dang mi 'gal bas de chos ston pa'i tshe/ dngos po yongs su ldog pa gcig kyang brtsams ste/ chos
106b3(phal chen): ston pa nas dngos po yongs su ldog pa brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa'i bar du chos ston to/ /sangs rgyas kyi mtshan gcig nas tshul de bzhin du brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa'i bar dang /
106b4(phal chen): 'jig rten gyi khams gcig dang / sangs rgyas su lung bstan pa gcig dang / mdo gcig dang / 'khor 'dus pa gcig dang / chos kyi mtshams sbyar ba gcig dang / dbang po rnam
106b5(phal chen): pa tha dad pa sna tshogs gcig dang / nyon mongs pa sna tshogs gcig dang / ting nge 'dzin sna tshogs gcig kyang brtsams te/ chos ston pa nas/ ting nge 'dzin sna tshogs brjod du med pa'i yang brjod
106b6(phal chen): du med pa'i bar du brtsams te chos ston to/ /nyi ma gcig kyang zad par byed cing chos ston pa nas/ zla ba phyed dang / zla ba gcig dang / lo gcig dang / lo brgya dang / lo stong dang / lo brgya phrag
106b7(phal chen): stong dang / bskal pa dang / bskal pa brgya dang / bskal pa stong dang / bskal pa brgya phrag stong dang / bskal pa bye ba khrag khrig brgya phrag stong dang / bskal pa tshad med pa dang / bsam gyis
106b8(phal chen): mi khyab pa dang / bskal pa dpag tu med pa dang / grangs med pa dang / mtshungs pa med pa dang / kun tu mtha' yas pa dang / mu med pa dang / sa mtshams med pa dang / gzhal du med pa dang /
107a1(phal chen): brjod du med pa dag kyang zad par byed cing chos ston to/ tshig dang yi ge gcig brtsams kyang don dang yi ge'i mthar thug pa med de/ de ci'i phyir zhe na/ de ni 'di ltar byang chub sems dpas byang chub
107a2(phal chen): sems dpa'i gter bcu rab tu thob pa'i phyir te/ gter de dag thob pas gzungs kyi snying po'i sgo chos thams cad la yang dag par gzhol ba zhes bya ba/ gzungs brgya stong grangs med pa'i 'khor can mngon du gyur
107a3(phal chen): te/ de gzungs kyi 'khor brgya stong grangs med pa ston par byed do/ /chos snang ba shin tu bstan pa thob pas sems can thams cad la chos ston to/ /chos kyi sgo snang ba'i chos can lce yangs pas 'jig rten gyi khams
107a4(phal chen): thams cad du mngon par go bar byed pa dang / dbyangs kyi yan lag la mkhas pas 'gro ba thams cad tshim par byed pa dang / dbang po ji lta ba bzhin du mgu bar byed pa dang / nyon mongs pa dang kun nas 'khor ba
107a5(phal chen): thams cad rnam par bzlog pa dang / sgra dang tshig rnam pa tha dad pa thams cad la rab tu zhugs pa dang / yi ge thams cad kyi spobs pas ston pa'i rjes su song ba dang / sems can thams cad kyi
107a6(phal chen): sa bon grung po yongs su shes pa'i bsam pa can du byed pas chos ston te thogs par mi byed do/ /skyo bar mi 'gyur ro/ /de ci'i phyir zhe na/ de ni 'di ltar byang chub sems dpas nam mkha'i khams dang /
107a7(phal chen): chos kyi dbyings mtha' dang dbus med par byed pa'i lus rab tu thob pa'i phyir ro/ kye rgyal ba'i sras dag /'di ni byang chub sems dpa'i gter bcus blo gros mi zad pa/ thub pa med pa 'dres pa med pa rnam
107a8(phal chen): par mi chod pa/ rgyun gcad par mi nus pa phyir mi ldog pa/ gting rnyed par dka' ba/ ring du gyur pa/ sgo kun nas ldan pa/ sangs rgyas thams cad kyi chos la zhugs pa'o/ /kye rgyal ba'i
107b1(phal chen): sras dag / bcu po de dag ni byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi gter te/ mi zad pa'i rnam pa bcus mi zad pa yin no/ /bla na med pa yin no/ /mthar rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas su 'gyur ba yin no/ /bcu gang zhe na/
107b2(phal chen): sems can thams cad nye bar 'tsho ba dang / sngon gyi smon lam legs par yongs su bsngos pa dang / bskal pa thams cad kyi grangs gcad du med pa dang / nam mkha'i dbyings dang mnyam pa nyid du khong du
107b3(phal chen): chud pa'i phyir/ sems tshad med pa dang / 'dus byas kyis ma gos pa'i phyir/ 'dus ma byas la yongs su bsngo ba dang / de ma thag pa'i yul du gyur pas chos thams cad zad mi shes pa dang / smon
107b4(phal chen): lam chen po tha dad pa med pa dang / spyod pa la gnas pa'i stobs shin tu 'dzin pa dang / sangs rgyas thams cad kyis yongs su gzung ba dang / chos thams cad sgyu ma lta bur 'jug pa mtha' dang dbus med
107b5(phal chen): pa la zhugs pa ste/ mi zad pa'i rnam pa bcu po 'di dag gis/ 'jig rten gyi bya ba thams cad kyi mthar phyin pa zad mi shes pa'i gter chen por 'gyur ro/ /gter mi zad pa bcu bstan pa'i le'u ste/
107b6(phal chen): nyi shu bdun pa'o// // de nas sangs rgyas kyi mthus shar phyogs kyi 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad dang / de bzhin du lho phyogs dang / nub phyogs dang / byang phyogs dang / byang shar gyi
107b7(phal chen): phyogs mtshams dang / shar lho'i phyogs mtshams dang / lho nub kyi phyogs mtshams dang / nub byang gi phyogs mtshams dang / 'og dang steng gi phyogs kyi 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad na
107b8(phal chen): yang gling bzhi pa 'di las stsogs pa gling re re na yang / de bzhin gshegs pa rnams bzhugs par snang ngo / /byang chub sems dpa' de dag kyang de bzhin gshegs pa'i byin gyis brlabs kyis chos
108a1(phal chen): ston to/ /de bzhin gshegs pa'i zhabs kyi drung na 'ang 'khod par shes so/ /bcom ldan 'das kyi rdzu 'phrul mngon par 'du mdzad pa de phyir ma brtul/ byang chub kyi shing drung yang phyir ma brtul/
108a2(phal chen): ri rab kyi rtse mo yang phyir ma brtul bar rab mtshe ma'i gnas nas dga' ldan gyi gnas kyi lha'i rgyal po rab dga' ldan gyi khang pa rin po che'i rgyan ces bya ba gang na ba der gshegs par snang ngo / /ji ltar gling bzhi
108a3(phal chen): pa 'di na bcom ldan 'das dga' ldan gyi gnas su gshegs par snang ba/ de bzhin du 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad kyi gling gzhi pa dag na yang bcom ldan 'das dga' ldan gyi gnas su gshegs
108a4(phal chen): par snang ngo / /byin brlabs snga ma de dag kyang ma 'khrugs par snang ngo / /de nas lha'i rgyal po rab dga' ldan gyis/ rgyang ma nas bcom ldan 'das khang pa rin po che thams cad kyis rgyan par gshegs
108a5(phal chen): pa mthong nas/ rings pa'i gzugs su khang pa rin po che thams cad kyis rgyan pa'i nang du de bzhin gshegs pa'i seng ge'i gdan nor bu rin po che las byas pa/ lha rdzas kyi rin po che'i rgyu las grub
108a6(phal chen): pa/ dge ba'i rtsa ba thams cad kyi rgyu las yongs su grub pa/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i byin gyis brlabs kyis byung ba/ dge ba'i rtsa ba bye ba khrag khrig brgya stong grangs med pa mang pos byung ba/
108a7(phal chen): sangs rgyas thams cad las byung ba'i chos dkar po las byung ba'i/ bsod nams kyi stobs mtha' yas pa sna tshogs thams cad dang ldan pa/ kha na ma tho ba med pa'i rnam par smyin pa thams cad kyis
108a8(phal chen): rnam par dag pa/ mi mthun pa med pa'i 'jig rten las 'das pa'i chos kyis byung ba/ gos pa med pa/ 'gro ba thams cad du byung ba/ thub pa med pa/ 'gro ba thams cad kyis blta na sdug pa/
108b1(phal chen): pog re bye ba brgya stong phrag bcus brgyan pa/ gser gyi dra ba bye ba brgya stong phrag bcus kun tu bris pa/ me tog gi bla re bye ba brgya stong phrag bcus kun nas bris pa/ phreng ba'i bla re bye ba brgya stong phrag
108b2(phal chen): bcus kun nas lding ba/ spos kyi bla re bye ba brgya stong phrag bcus spos kun tu 'thul bar sbyar bas/ rin po che'i bla re bye ba brgya stong phrag bcu steng nas bkab pa/ me tog gi gdugs bye ba brgya stong phrag
108b3(phal chen): bcus kun nas bsgreng ba/ rin po che'i gdugs bye ba brgya stong phrag bcus kun nas bkab pa/ gdan bye ba khrag khrig brgya stong mngon par gting ba/ rin po che'i phu shu bye ba brgya stong phrag bcus
108b4(phal chen): rgyan du bsgrub pa/ nor bu'i dra ba bye ba brgya stong phrag bcus shin tu rnam par phye bas g.yog par byas pa/ rin po che'i dra ba bye ba brgya stong phrag bcus shin tu 'khor kun tu g.yogs pa/ rin po che'i
108b5(phal chen): phreng ba 'phyang ba'i dra ba bye ba brgya stong phrag bcu shin tu spyangs pas bkab pa/ lhab lhub kyi dra ba bye ba brgya stong phrag bcus shin tu klubs shing brgyan pa/ gdugs kyi dra ba bye ba brgya stong phrag
108b6(phal chen): bcus kun nas khebs par bkab pa/ gos sna tshogs kyi dra ba bye ba brgya stong phrag bcus sna tshogs su g.yogs pa/ rin po che'i pad mo'i dra ba bye ba brgya stong phrag bcu shin tu rgyas par
