119b3(phal chen): kun nas g.yog par byas so/ /lha rdzas las 'das pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa las byung ba'i me tog gi bla re sna tshogs kyis chos kyi dbyings kun nas khebs par byas so/ /lha rdzas las 'das pa mos pa
119b4(phal chen): rnam par dag pa/ sangs rgyas thams cad kyi yul rgyas par 'gengs pa'i na bza' sna tshogs mngon par dga' bas chos kyi dbyings brgyan par byas so/ /chags pa myed pa'i chos kyi rang bzhin rdo rje
119b5(phal chen): la yang dag par zhugs pa'i sems kyis lha rdzas las 'das pa'i myi skye ba'i chos las byung ba'i dril bu tshom bur gcad pa'i dra bas chos kyi dbyings brgyan par byas so/ /chos thams cad sgyu ma lta
119b6(phal chen): bur rtogs pa'i sems kyis lha rdzas las 'das pa'i spos thams cad kyi mchog gis bdug pa'i rgyan gyis chos kyi dbyings brgyan par byas so/ /de bzhin gshegs pa bzhugs pas chos kyi dbyings
119b7(phal chen): rgyas par byas pa'i sems kyis lha rdzas las 'das pa'i rin po che thams cad kyi khri sangs rgyas kyi gdan du bting ba'i rgyan kyis chos kyi dbyings brgyan pa byas so/ /sangs rgyas kyi mchod pa rang bzhin 'gag
119b8(phal chen): pa myed pa'i sems kyis lha rdzas las 'das pa'i rin po che sna tshogs kyi rgyal mtshan yang dag par bsgreng ba'i rgyal mtshan gyis chos kyi dbyings brgyan pa byas so/ /rmi lam lta bu'i chos nyid kyis bsam
120a1(phal chen): pa tshim pas lha rdzas las 'das pa'i rin po che sna tshogs kyis sangs rgyas kyi pho brang brgyan pas chos kyi dbyings brgyan pa byas so/ /myi gnas pa'i dge ba'i rtsa ba blang ba myed pa las byung bas/
120a2(phal chen): lha rdzas las 'das pa'i rin po che sna tshogs kyi pad mos kun nas g.yog pa'i rgyan kyis chos kyis dbyings brgyan par byas so/ /lha rdzas las 'das pa'i spos thams cad kyi mchog gi sprin gyis chos
120a3(phal chen): kyi dbyings thams cad rgyas par byas pa dang / me tog kha dog mtha' yas pa sna tshogs kyi sprin dang / na bza' kha dog rnam pa sna tshogs rnam pa tha dad pa thams cad kyi sprin dang / tsan dan gyi dri zhim po mtha' yas par
120a4(phal chen): 'phro ba thams cad kyi sprin dang / lha rdzas las 'das pa'i rin po che thams cad kyi gdugs rnam pa sna tshogs kyi sprin dang / spos dang bdug pa sna tshogs kyi ngad kun tu ldang ba'i sprin dang / phreng ba yid du 'ong ba thams
120a5(phal chen): cad kyi sprin dang / lha rdzas las 'das pa'i lhab lhub rnam par dag pa thams cad kyi sprin dang / byang chub sems dpa' bye ba khrag khrig brgya stong brjod du myed pa'i rang gi lus gtong ba'i sprin dang / sangs rgyas
120a6(phal chen): kyi yon tan brjod pa las 'das pas bstod cing bsngags pa'i brjod pa zad myi shes pa'i sprin dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i bstod pas brjod pa ji lta ba bzhin du yang dag par bsngags pa'i chos ma
120a7(phal chen): lags pa las byung ba'i/ sangs rgyas kyi stobs mtha' dang dbus myed pa las rgyu bas 'gro ba thams cad bde ba'i lam bstan pa dang / tshig rnam par 'byed pa brjod du myed pa'i mos pas chos tshad
120a8(phal chen): myed pa la gzhol ba'i gzugs kyi rgyud thams cad las byung ba'i tha dad pa yang dag par shes pa la mkhas pa myi zad pa dang myi 'jigs pas yid dga' bar gyur pa'i rim gro ngoms mi shes pas/ de bzhin gshegs pa la mngon par bstod pa/
120b1(phal chen): tshig rnam par dbye zhing brjod pas/ byang chub sems dpa' de dag chos kyi dbyings kyi lus nam mkha'i khams rgyas par byed pa byin gyis brlabs te/
120b2(phal chen): sangs rgyas 'das pa dang / ma byon pa dang / da ltar byung ba thams cad kyis yongs su gzung ba'i yid kyis dbang pos mngon par bstod do/ /lha'i ris gzhan dang gzhan nas 'dus pa'i lha'i 'khor de dag
120b3(phal chen): thams cad dang / sangs rgyas kyi zhing brjod du myed pa nas 'dus pa'i byang chub sems dpa'i 'khor rnams kyang / de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas kyi khyu mchog gi
120b4(phal chen): mthu phyung ba/ bsam gyis myi khyab pa yongs su bstod cing / de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku yang dag par 'byung ba dang / bsam gyis myi khyab pa'i rdzu 'phrul yang dag par ston pa dang / sems can grangs myed pa'i rgyud
120b5(phal chen): tshim par mdzad pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi brgyan rnam par phye bas nam mkha'i khams thams cad dang / chos kyi dbyings thams cad rgyas par mdzad pa 'gro ba thams cad kyi dge ba'i rtsa ba mtha' yas pa brtan
120b6(phal chen): par mdzad pa/ sangs rgyas kyi cho 'phrul gzhal du myed pa las byung ba/ tshig gi lam thams cad las yang dag par 'das pa/ byang chub sems dpa'i rigs dang ldan pa thams cad kyis mngon par mos
120b7(phal chen): par bya ba/ sems can 'dul ba ji lta ba bzhin du tshim par bya ba'i phyir sangs rgyas kyi sku yang dag par rjes su khyab par gyur pa/ dge ba'i rtsa ba brjod pa thams cad rnam par dag pas sangs rgyas kyi yon tan
120b8(phal chen): tshad myed pa yang dag par sten pa/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i yul rgyun myi 'chad par 'byung ba'i ting nge 'dzin las 'byung ba/ 'gro ba thams cad ma lus pa'i lus kyi rjes su 'dul ba/ sku'i byin gyi brlabs
121a1(phal chen): las mtshams myed pa/ yid tshad myed pa yongs su mgu bar mdzad pa/ thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyi rigs rgyun mi gcod pa/ sangs rgyas kyi rnam par spyod pa mtha' dang dbus myed pa 'byung ba brnyes
121a2(phal chen): pa/ 'das pa dang ma byon pa dang / da ltar byung ba'i sangs rgyas thams cad kyi rigs su byung ba/ khams dang mos pa bgrang du myed pa thams cad sbyong bar mdzad pa/ byang chub sems dpa' thams cad ye shes
121a3(phal chen): mngon par bsgrub pa la 'jug par mdzad pa/ byang chub sems dpa' thams cad kyi dbang po rab tu dga' bar mdzad pa/ chos kyi sprin kyis nam mkha'i khams thams cad du g.yog par mdzad pa/ chos kyi
121a4(phal chen): dbyings thams cad ma lus par de bzhin gshegs pas 'dul ba'i byin gyis rlob pa/ sems can thams cad kyi rtog pa bsam pa ji lta ba bzhin du yongs su rgyas par mdzad pa/ myi gnas pa'i ye shes kyi
121a5(phal chen): rgyud kyis 'gro ba thams cad las 'phags pa/ ye shes kyi rnam pa thams cad brnyes pa/ sangs rgyas kyi byin gyis rlabs snang ba gzigs pa/ dge ba'i rtsa ba ji ltar bskyed pa bzhin du yang dag par
121a6(phal chen): gzigs pa/ sems bskyed pa rgya chen po skye bar mdzad pa/ 'gro ba thams cad du kun tu bzang po thub pa myed pa'i ye shes yang dag par rgyu las byung ba 'gro ba dang zhing thams cad du khyab pa/ chos kyi dbyings
121a7(phal chen): thams cad du myi ldog par gshegs pa/ sangs rgyas kyi sku'i rgyud brjod du myed pa yang dag par ston pa/ bsam pa ji lta ba bzhin du 'khrul pa myi mnga' bar byin gyis rlob pa/ 'gro ba thams cad kyi tshig gi rnam
121a8(phal chen): pas yon tan myi zad pa sangs rgyas rjes su dran pas/ chos kyi dbyings thams cad rgyas par mdzad pa/ 'jig rten gyi khams mtha' dang dbus myed pa khyab par mdzad pa/ byang chub kyi sems kyi ji ltar dam bcas
121b1(phal chen): pa'i sems can la rim gror mdzad pa/ ji ltar brnyes pa'i chos kyi sbyin pa mdzad pa/ sems can ji ltar 'dul ba bzhin du 'dul ba mdzad pa/ mos pa dang bsam pa ji lta ba bzhin du rnam par dag par mdzad
121b2(phal chen): pa/ gzugs kyi sku bsam gyis myi khyab par byin gyis rlob pa/ 'gro ba thams cad la gnas pa mi mnga' zhing mnyam pa nyid kyi rjes su bzhud pa/ spyod pa tha dad pa las byung ba/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i stobs
121b3(phal chen): bcu sgrib pa myed pa mngon par sangs rgyas pa/ thugs la chags pa myi mnga' bas rtag tu mnyam par gzhag cing ma 'dres pa/ ye shes thams cad la rnam par spyod pa/ don dang tshig dang yi ge tha dad pa yang dag par ston
121b4(phal chen): pa dang / ye shes rgya mtsho mtha' dang dbus myed pa la zhugs pa/ yon tan gyi mchog ye shes snying pos byung bas chos kyi dbyings thams cad du sangs rgyas kyi nyi ma shar ba/ 'gro ba thams cad du sngon gyi smon lam
121b5(phal chen): zad pa myi mnga' bar chos kyi dbyings kyi rang bzhin la gnas pa/ sangs rgyas kyi rnam par spyod pa ma nyams pa brnyes pa/ bdag gi dang yongs su gzung ba myed pas gnas par myi mnga' ba/ 'jig rten las 'das
121b6(phal chen): pa'i chos thams cad 'byung zhing 'jig rten gyi chos thams cad kyis ma gos pa/ 'gro ba thams cad kyis myi shes pa'i rgyal mtshan yang dag par bcad pa/ 'jig rten thams cad kyi myi shes pa chen po yongs su
121b7(phal chen): bsal ba'i gnas su gyur pa 'gro ba thams cad snang bar mngon par 'dod pa/ 'jig rten thams cad ye shes khyad par du 'phags pa la rab tu gzhog pa/ 'gro ba thams cad nye bar 'tsho ba'i bsod nams
121b8(phal chen): yongs su mi zad pa/ byang chub sems dpa' thams cad kyi shes pa thugs su chud pa/ dad par bya bar 'os pa/ yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas su gzhol ba'i byams pa chen po las byung ba thugs
122a1(phal chen): rje chen po yang dag par ston pas spyod pa/ sangs rgyas kyi sku brjod du myed pa'i chos dang / sangs rgyas kyi chos sna tshogs bsam gyis myi khyab pa'i gsung dang dbyangs kyi char 'babs pa/ sems can gyi
122a2(phal chen): bsam pa ji lta ba bzhin du yang dag par tshim par mdzad pa/ sngon gyi mtha' dang phyi ma'i mtha' dang da ltar byung ba'i mtha'i dmyigs pa'i byin gyis rlabs shin tu dag cing bsam gyis myi khyab pas sems can
122a3(phal chen): dag par mdzad pa/ byang chub sems dpa' thams cad lung bstan pa rgyun myi 'chad pa/ sangs rgyas kyi rigs su dbang bskur bas/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i rgyud du byung ba/ 'jig rten thams cad du 'khor lo myi ldog
122a4(phal chen): par 'khor ba/ 'jig rten thams cad kyi mngon par zhen pa thams cad las 'phags pa/ sangs rgyas kyi zhing dang chos kyi dbyings thams cad kyi mthas klas pa la myi gnas pa/ 'gro ba thams cad mnyam pa nyid du

122a6(phal chen): rang bzhin ye shes kyi zla ba/ de bzhin gshegs pa tshad myed pa'i rjes su bzhud pa/ sgyu ma lta bur 'jig rten sna tshogs byin gyis rlob pa/ myig yor lta bu'i ye shes kyis rnam par ston pa/ rmi lam lta bu
122a7(phal chen): rjes su dran pa/ sprul pa dang mnyam par byung ba/ sems kyi rang bzhin lta bur 'jig rten sna tshogs thams cad byin gyis rlob pa/ las kyi rnam par smyin pa'i tshul dang / bsam pa ji lta ba bzhin du sems can gyi skye
122a8(phal chen): mched rnam par phye ba yang dag par ston pa/ sems can gyi dbang po dang 'thun par sangs rgyas kyi sku byung ba/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i dmyigs pa la sems can grangs myed pa'i sems yang dag par gnas
122b1(phal chen): pa/ 'jig rten thams cad rten cing 'brel par 'byung ba/ rnam par bstan pa'i rang bzhin du chos kyi mtshan nyid gyis yang dag par spyod pa/ ye shes kyi rgyud mtshan nyid myed pa'i rang bzhin dang mtshan nyid cig du
122b2(phal chen): gyur pa/ 'jig rten thams cad kyi rang bzhin gyi mtshan nyid snang ba mngon par sgrub pa'i spyod pa yang dag par ston cing 'gro ba thams cad gdon par brtson pa/ sangs rgyas kyi spyod yul bla na myed pa yang dag par
122b3(phal chen): ston pa/ 'jig rten dang zhing thams cad yongs su skyob pas sangs rgyas kyi mtshan ma gzung bar 'jig rten du mngon par byung ba/ 'jig rten gyi nyon mongs pa'i mtshan ma thams cad rnam par bstsal ba/
122b4(phal chen): 'jig rten thams cad kyis rjes su dran pa dang / dmyigs par 'byor par gyur pa/ 'khrug pa myed par khong du chud par 'gyur ba'i theg pa chen pos zhal yongs su rgyas pas/ chos thams cad kyi don grub pa/
122b5(phal chen): 'gro ba thams cad kyi dge ba'i rtsa bas rnam par phye ba nyams pa myed pa'i phrin las rnam par smyin pas rnam par dag pa/ ye shes kyi 'byung gnas dus gsum mnyam pa nyid du thugs su chud pa/ 'jig rten thams
122b6(phal chen): cad kyi yongs su rtog pa yongs su mi rtog pas byung ba/ 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du 'od gzer gyi dra bas gsal bar gyur pa/ phyogs bcu 'byam klas pa thams cad du sangs rgyas kyi 'od kyis snang bar
122b7(phal chen): mdzad pas/ sangs rgyas thams cad kyi rjes su bzhud pa/ blta bas mi ngoms shing gtang mi bra ba/ yon tan chen po dang ye shes dang mngon par shes pa dang / byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa 'byung ba dang / dbang po
122b8(phal chen): mngon par mkhyen pa'i ye shes kyi spyod yul can/ ye shes kyi dkyil 'khor gyis sangs rgyas kyi mdzad pa rgyas par mdzad pa/ sangs rgyas kyi 'phrin las shin tu bsgrub pa/ nub cing 'das pa dang / ma 'ongs pa dang

123a2(phal chen): dpal thams cad kyis rab tu 'bar ba/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku kha dog mtha' yas pa sna tshogs su 'jig rten thams cad la mngon par ston pa/ sgrib pa'i chos thams cad du ma lhung ba/ chos thams
123a3(phal chen): cad kyi rang bzhin gyi don gyis dag pa yon tan gyi chos thams cad la mnga' bas mdzes pa'i dkyil 'khor can yon tan gyi 'od gzer mnga' ba'i nyi mar gyur pa/ bsod nams kyi zhing du shar ba/ gzi brjid thams

123a7(phal chen): phugs rab rib myed cing rnam par dag pa/ sangs rgyas kyi lo legs pa yang dag par ston pa/ 'khu ba'i sems can gyi khams las su rung bar mdzad pa/ 'dul ba sna tshogs du ma la 'jug pa/ dus bzhin

123b6(phal chen): ri bo rnam par dag pa/ sangs rgyas 'jam klas pa dang / byang chub sems dpa' gzhan dang gzhan du ston pa/ kha na ma tho ba myed pa'i sa la sems can rab tu 'god pa/ sangs rgyas kyi yon tan grangs myed par

123b8(phal chen): 'thob par mdzad pa/ 'jig rten thams cad kyi smon lam rjes su srung ba myi shigs pa/ 'gro ba thams cad la dge ba'i bshes gnyen ston pa/ snang ba dri ma myed cing mchog du dag par mdzad pa/

124b1(phal chen): yang dag par blta ba/ rnam pa de lta bur ye shes kyi mu stegs las 'bab pa/ rnam pa de lta bu'i yon tan rgya mtsho'i gangs chen mtsho thams cad la 'jug pa/ rnam pa de lta bu'i ye shes kyi nam mkha'i rjes

124b5(phal chen): gzer bye ba khrag khrig brgya stong grangs myed pa 'byung ba/ grangs myed pa rim par dag pa/ grangs myed par shin tu snang ba/ grangs myed par bltar yod pa/ grangs myed pa'i sems can gyi dga' ba bskyed

124b8(phal chen): rnam par 'phrul pa sna tshogs kyis 'phrul zhing 'byung ba/ kha dog bsam gyis mi khyab pa/ mdog bsam gyis myi khyab pa/ 'od bsam gyis myi khyab pa/ chos kyi dbyings mtha' dang dbus myed pa

125a2(phal chen): yongs su 'dzin pa/ 'jig rten thams cad las rnam par 'das shing 'jig rten las 'das pa'i dge ba'i rtsa bas yongs su byung ba/ rgyan bye ba khrag khrig brgya stong bsam gyis mi khyab pa yang dag par ston pa/
125a3(phal chen): bskal pa bye ba khrag khrig bsam gyis mi khyab par yon tan myi zad pa/ sangs rgyas kyi rnam par 'phrul pa zad myi shes pa las byung ba/ sangs rgyas skye ba brjod du myed pa yang dag par ston pa/ ye shes
125a4(phal chen): kyi sgo la rab tu g.yog pa/ don yangs pa shin tu ston pa sangs rgyas kyi sprul pa brjod du myed pa'i tshul yang dag par ston pa/ sangs rgyas kyi yul mtha' dang dbus myed pa chos kyi dbyings kyis klas pa/
125a5(phal chen): nam mkha'i khams kyi mthar thug pa/ 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du byin gyi rlabs kyis byung ba 'gro ba thams cad rnam par dag pa/ mnyam pa nyid kyi rjes su song ba/ thams cad mkhyen pa chags pa myed
125a6(phal chen): pa/ mtha' dang dbus myed pa'i sangs rgyas kyi spyod pa las byung ba/ de bzhin gshegs pa bsam gyis myi khyab pas bsten pa'i dpal yod pa/ rin po che'i 'od 'phro ba bye ba brgya stong bsam gyi mi khyab pa
125a7(phal chen): ltar 'byung ba mthong bar gyur to/ /bcom ldan 'das kyis kyang byin gyis rlabs kyi brgyan smon lam chen po las byung ba'i dge ba'i rtsa ba mtha' yas pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa mnyes par bya ba'i spyod pas
125a8(phal chen): rnam par dag pa dang / sngon gyi bag yod pa las yang dag par byung ba'i thams cad mkhyen pa'i sems chags pa med pa'i dge ba'i rtsa ba las byung ba dang / de bzhin gshegs pa 'jam klas pa 'gro ba thams cad kyi
125b1(phal chen): the tsom gcod pa/ de bzhin gshegs pa mthong ba la sems can tshad myed pa rab tu dgod pa dang / dge ba'i rtsa ba'i sgo dang sangs rgyas kyi cho 'phrul zil gyis non pa myed pa la rgya mtsho'i mthas gtugs pa'i
125b2(phal chen): sems can gzung bar bya ba dang / byang chub sems dpa'i bka' bzhin byed pa thams cad sangs rgyas kyi zhing kun nas 'dus pa dang / sangs rgyas kyis byin gyis rlabs dang / sangs rgyas kyi chos bsam
125b3(phal chen): gyis myi khyab pa yongs su brjod pa'i tshul gyis de bzhin gshegs pa'i 'khor du ji lta ji ltar sangs rgyas kyi zhing 'jam klas pa bye ba khrag khrig brgya stong brjod du myed pa grangs myed pa dag na/ sems
125b4(phal chen): ma dad par bya ba dang / dad pa rnams rnam par 'phel bar bya ba dang / sems rnam par 'phel ba rnams rnam par dag par bya ba dang / sems can rnam par dag pa rnams yongs su smin par bya ba dang /
125b5(phal chen): sems can yongs su smin pa rnams 'dul bar bya ba dang / chos zab mo khong du chud par bya ba dang / ye shes snang ba mtha' dang dbus myed pa khong du chud par bya ba dang / sems tshad myed pa'i rnams rgya che bar
125b6(phal chen): bya ba dang / thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du sems bskyed pa las phyir myi ldog par bya ba dang / chos nyid dang myi 'gal bar bya ba dang / yang dag pa'i mthas mi skrag par bya ba dang / de bzhin nyid rab tu rtogs par bya ba dang /
125b7(phal chen): pha rol tu phyin pa'i rnams kyang rab tu rdzogs par bya ba dang / 'jig rten las 'das pa'i dge ba'i rtsa ba rnam par sbyang bar bya ba dang / dmyigs pa thams cad la brtson pa'i sangs rgyas kyi rnam par 'phrul
125b8(phal chen): pa yang kun tu bzang po'i tshul du mos par bya ba dang / bdud kyi yul las rnam par ldog par bya ba dang / sangs rgyas kyi yul 'thob par bya ba dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i chos nyid shes par bya ba dang /
126a1(phal chen): ye shes bsam gyis myi khyab pa skye bar bya ba dang / theg pa chen po'i smon lam las phyir mi ldog par bya ba dang / sangs rgyas blta ba las mi 'phang bar bya ba dang / ye shes khong du chud par
126a2(phal chen): bya ba tshad myed pa rtogs par bya ba dang / sa mtshams med pa'i bsod nams kyi stobs yang dag par bsgrub par bya ba dang / shin tu dga' ba'i sems bskyed par bya ba dang / the tsom med pa'i sa la 'jug
126a3(phal chen): par bya ba dang / kha na ma tho ba med cing yongs su dag pa 'thob par bya ba dang / thams cad mkhyen pa nyid la brten pa so sor 'thob par bya ba dang / chos mthong ba las phyir mi ldog par bya ba dang / byang chub sems
126a4(phal chen): dpa' thams cad kyi tshogs kyi rjes su 'jug par bya ba dang / dus gsum kyi sangs rgyas thams cad kyi rigs grub par bya ba de lta de ltar bcom ldan 'das kyis thugs rje chen po kun tu khyab pa dang / thams
126a5(phal chen): cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes kyi phung po chen pos byin gyis rlabs kyi rgyan rnam pa mang po yang dag par bstan to/ /de ltar bcom ldan 'das kyis sems can thams cad 'dul ba'i dbang du sangs rgyas kyi
126a6(phal chen): bdag nyid che ba brjod pa'i phyir chags pa med pa'i ye shes gyi snying po rab tu snang bas/ sangs rgyas kyi dpal mtha' yas pa rab tu 'bar ba/ sangs rgyas kyi cho 'phrul bsam gyis mi khyab pas
126a7(phal chen): rnam par snang ba thams cad du zhugs pa'i de bzhin gshegs pa'i skus rnam par 'phrul pa mtha' dang dbus med pa'i cho 'phrul gyi mthu dang ldan pa/ dgongs pa yongs su rdzogs pa'i sngon gyi smon
126a8(phal chen): lam gyis yongs su grub pa'i ye shes kyi rnam par gnon pas de bzhin gshegs pa'i stobs phun sum tshogs pa/ chos kyi dbang phyug brnyes pas chos thams cad la mnga' ba dang ldan pa thams cad
126b1(phal chen): mkhyen pa nyid kyi sgo nas byung ba'i de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku rnam par dag pas shin tu sbyangs pa mnga' ba/ 'das pa dang / ma byon pa dang da ltar byung ba'i sangs rgyas thams cad dang mnyam pa nyid du gyur
126b2(phal chen): pa/ dge ba'i rtsa ba thams cad kyi snying po shin tu sbyangs pa/ 'gro ba thams cad kyi dpes dper myi 'gyur ba'i sku gzugs mnga' ba/ mtshan thams cad kyi lo ma shin tu 'phags pa'i sku can/ stobs bcu'i
126b3(phal chen): rgyal mtshan gyi stobs chen po dang ldan pa/ bskal pa mi zad pa thams cad du blta bas mi ngoms pa/ sngon gyi dge ba'i rtsa ba ston pa'i dbyangs kyi ye shes kyi nga ror gyur ba/ byang chub sems dpa'
126b4(phal chen): thams cad kyi dkyil 'khor mi zad pas 'gro ba thams cad la nyi ma'i dkyil 'khor du gyur pa/ yon tan thams cad kyi rgyal po chos thams cad kyi srid la mnga' ba'i phyir dus gsum snang bar
126b5(phal chen): byed pa'i gsung mnga' bas byin gyis rlabs kyi rgyan sngon gyi dge ba'i rtsa ba'i tshogs las yang dag par byung ba'i byin gyis brlabs so/ /de nas lha'i dbang po rab dga' ldan gyi tshul 'di lta bur de bzhin
126b6(phal chen): gshegs pa la mchod pa dang / rim gro dang / rgyan kun tu bshams pa byas te/ dga' ldan gyi ris kyi lha bye ba brgya stong grangs med pa dang lhan cig du/ zhe sa can rim gro dang bcas par bcom ldan
126b7(phal chen): 'das gang na ba der thal mo sbyar te/ phyag 'tshal nas bcom ldan 'das la 'di skad ces gsol to/ /bcom ldan 'das gshegs su gsol/ bde bar gshegs pa gshegs su gsol/
126b8(phal chen): de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas bde bar gshegs sam/ de nas bcom ldan 'das lha'i rgyal po rab dga' ldan gyis spyan drangs nas/ sangs rgyas kyi
127a1(phal chen): rgyan rnam pa 'di lta bu dang / sangs rgyas kyi bdag nyid che ba 'gro ba thams cad la mdzes pa/ byang chub sems dpa' thams cad mos pa/ dga' ldan gyi ris kyi lha'i bu thams cad mngon par dga'
127a2(phal chen): ba/ lha'i rgyal po rab dga' ldan gyis mi ngoms par rim gror bya zhing / tshad myed pa'i sems can sangs rgyas la dmyigs par brtson pa bskyed pa/ tshad med pa'i sems can sangs rgyas su dge ba'i rtsa ba
127a3(phal chen): bskyed pa mi zad pa'i bsod nams dang ldan par 'gyur ba/ dad pa dri ma med pa'i tshogs kyis bstsags pa de bzhin gshegs pa'i zhal blta ba dang / mchod pas skyo bar mi 'gyur ba/ lhag pa'i bsam

127a5(phal chen): ji ltar bcom ldan 'das 'dir gshegs pa de bzhin du 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad kyi gling bzhi dang / dga' ldan gyi gnas dag du gshegs par snang ngo / /bcom ldan 'das rin po che thams cad
127a6(phal chen): kyis brgyan pa'i khang par gshegs ma thag tu de'i tshe/ rin po che thams cad brgyan pa'i khang pa rin po che'i rgyan las shin tu 'das par gnas so/ /lha rdzas las 'das pa'i rin po che thams cad
127a7(phal chen): kyi dra bas kun nas g.yog par gnas so/ /lha rdzas las 'das pa'i rin po che thams cad kyi sprin gyi char mngon par 'bab par gnas so/ /lha rdzas las 'das pa'i rin po che thams cad kyi rgyan
127a8(phal chen): sprin gyis brgyan pa'i gnas so/ /lha rdzas las 'das pa'i rin po che thams cad kyi sprin rab tu gtong bar gnas so/ /lha rdzas las 'das pa'i tsan dan thams cad kyi sprin chen po rab tu gtong bar
127b1(phal chen): gnas so/ /lha rdzas las 'das pa'i dri thams cad kyi mchog dang / bdug pa 'thul ba'i sprin gyi char rab tu 'bab par gnas so/ /lha rdzas las 'das pa'i rin po che sna tshogs thams cad kyi sprin rnam

127b3(phal chen): ba brgya stong bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i sgra rab tu 'byin par gnas so/ /thams cad mkhyen pa'i chos kyi dbyangs su sgrag pa'i rol mo sgra dang / glu'i dbyangs kyang rab tu 'byed par gnas par gyur te/ ji ltar
127b4(phal chen): bcom ldan 'das gshegs pa de bzhin du 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad kyi gling bzhi pa dang / dga' ldan gyi gnas dag du yang rin po che thams cad kyis brgyan pa'i khang par gshegs par snang ngo / /
127b5(phal chen): de nas lha'i rgyal po rab dga' ldan gyis lha'i gnas thams cad du lha'i rgyal po rab dga' ldan gyis de bzhin gshegs pa la gsol ba gtab pa zhes sgra brjod do/ /de nas sangs rgyas kyi mthus lha'i
127b6(phal chen): rgyal po rab dga' ldan la bar chad du myi 'gyur ba dang / sngon gyi dge ba'i rtsa ba tshogs dang / tshad med pa'i dge ba'i rtsa bas brtan pa dang / mtha' yas par sems bskyed pa'i dad pa rnam par 'phel ba dang /

130a8(phal chen): blta na don yod par sems can gdul ba dang / rnam par dag pa'i chos kyis sangs rgyas kyi rnam par 'phrul pa yongs su ston pa dang / 'gro ba thams cad yongs su bskyab
130b1(phal chen): par byang chub sems dpa'i rtse gcig du smon lam gtab pas/ dkyil mo bkrung bcas te 'khod do/ /byang chub sems dpa' de dag thams cad kyang 'di lta ste/ chags pa myed par spyod pas
130b2(phal chen): sangs rgyas kyi zhing thams cad du 'gro ba dang / 'di lta ste/ gnas med pa'i lus dang / 'di lta ste/ tshad med pa'i lus kyis kun tu 'gro ba'i ye shes kyi byin gyis brlabs dang / 'di lta ste/ mtha'
130b3(phal chen): dbus myed pa'i sangs rgyas kyi rnam par 'phrul pa bsam gyis mi khyab pa la 'jug pa dang / 'di lta ste/ thams cad mkhyen pa'i sgo 'byam klas pa/ tshad med par gyur pa dang / 'di lta ste/
130b4(phal chen): chos la myi 'jigs par mkhas pa'i snang ba mtha' yas pa dang / 'di lta ste/ phyi ma'i mtha'i bskal par mi zad pa'i tha dad pa yang dag pa shes pa'i tshul bshad pa dang / 'di lta ste/ gzugs
130b5(phal chen): thams cad kyis snang bar byas pa'i ye shes kyi phung po rab tu rgyas pa dang / 'di lta ste/ chos kyi dbyings rgyas par gyur pa'i shes rab kyi myig rnam par dag pa'i spobs pa dang / 'di lta ste/ nam
130b6(phal chen): mkha'i dbyings kyis klas par ye shes kyi spyod yul yongs su gnas pa dang / mtshams myed cing mtha' yas pa'i sangs rgyas rnams kyi spyod pa dang / ldan pa rab tu thob par gyur pa dag go /
130b7(phal chen): ji ltar gling bzhi pa 'di'i dga' ldan gyi gnas su/ byang chub sems dpa' 'dus par gyur pa de bzhin du/ 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad kyi gling bzhi pa dang / dga' ldan gyi gnas
130b8(phal chen): dag tu yang / byang chub sems dpa' ming de skad bya ba dag /'jig rten gyi khams ming de skad ces bya ba dag nas/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i mtshan de skad ces bya ba dag gi zham
131a1(phal chen): ring na tshangs par spyod pa sha stag 'ongs par gyur to/ /de nas bcom ldan 'das kyi zhabs kyi pus mo'i lha nga gnyis nas 'od gzer bye ba khrag khrig brgya stong byung ste/ phyogs bcu
131a2(phal chen): thams cad snang bar byas nas/ 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad bstan to/ /de nas byang chub sems dpa' de dag gis/ 'jig rten gyi khams de dag gi gling bzhi pa thams cad dang / dga'
131a3(phal chen): ldan gyi gnas thams cad na de bzhin gshegs pa'i rnam par 'phrul pa yod pa mthong bar gyur to/ /byang chub sems dpa' de dag ji snyed kyis phyogs bcur chos kyi dbyings kyis klas pa'i 'jig
131a4(phal chen): rten gyi khams kyi mthar thug pa dag na/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i sangs rgyas rnam par rol pa mthong bar gyur pa de dag thams cad de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas
131a5(phal chen): rnam par snang mdzad kyis sngon/ byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa la dge ba'i rtsa ba'i grogs su gyur pa dag ste/ 'di ltar sangs rgyas kyi rnam par thar pa zab mos rnam par 'phrul pa la mos pa
131a6(phal chen): sha stag go/ /chos kyi dbyings kyi lus tha dad pa med pa'i rjes su song ba sha stag go/ /gnas med pa'i sangs rgyas kyi zhing du 'gro ba'i rjes su song bas rab tu zhugs pa sha stag go/ /sangs rgyas bsam
131a7(phal chen): gyis mi khyab pa blta ba la rjes su gzhol ba sha stag go/ /chags pa med pa'i sems skad gcig gis chos kyi dbyings khyab par byed pa sha stag go/ /bsam pa rin po che rdul dang bral ba dang
131a8(phal chen): ldan pa sha stag go/ /brjod du myed pa'i sangs rgyas mang po dang 'grogs pa dang ldan pa sha stag go/ /sangs rgyas kyi byin gyis rlabs grangs myed pa dang ldan pa sha stag go/ /yang dag par spyod pa'i
131b1(phal chen): mchog gi pha rol tu phyin pa sha stag go/ /bla na myed pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub kyi dran pa rnam par dag pa la gnas pa sha stag go/ /blo dang sems skad cig thams cad kyis cher 'phags pa
131b2(phal chen): rab tu thob pa sha stag go/ /chung ngur zhugs shing cher gyur pa'i spyod pa la dbang ba sha stag go/ /cher gyur pa la zhugs shing chung ngur 'jug pa'i rjes su chud nas ye shes kyis spyod pa'i pha rol tu phyin
131b3(phal chen): pa sha stag go/ /de lta bu'i gnas dang / sangs rgyas kyi sku'i rang bzhin rjes su rtogs pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa dang 'grogs shing thams cad mkhyen pa nyid thob pa/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams dang /
131b4(phal chen): rin po che sna tshogs ltar grub pa'i lus dang / de bzhin gshegs par 'gyur ba'i spyod yul thams cad du 'gro ba dang / ye shes chen po'i rgyud kyi sgo rnam par phye ba dang / ye shes kyi stobs
131b5(phal chen): rdo rje'i rgyal mtshan gyi mthu'i mchog thob pa dang / rdo rje gcod pa'i ting nge 'dzin gyi tshul rab tu thob pa dang / sems can bye ba khrag khrig brgya stong grangs med pa rnams yongs su smyin par gdul ba la
131b6(phal chen): rmongs pa myed pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi rnam par 'phrul pa thams cad du 'gro ba gdon mi za ba'i mchog thob pa dang / bgrang ba thams cad la mngon par chags pa dang / bgrang ba'i mngon par bsgrub pa
131b7(phal chen): thams cad shin tu bslabs pa dang / bgrang ba'i shes pa thams cad kyi mthar thug cing chos rnam par dgod pa la mkhas pa/ 'di dag dang gzhan yang yon tan bye ba khrag khrig brgya stong brjod du med pa
131b8(phal chen): dang / yon tan sngags pa rnam par dag pa myi zad pas byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi dus gsum kyi yon tan tshad med pa dang ldan pa sha stag go/ /de bzhin gshegs pa mngon sum du bya ba dang /
132a1(phal chen): sangs rgyas 'byam klas pa thams cad blta ba'i phyir kun nas 'dus par gyur to/ /de nas byang chub sems dpa' rdo rje rgyal mtshan gyis/ sangs rgyas kyi byin gyis rlabs kyis phyogs
132a2(phal chen): bcur rnam par bltas te/ de'i tshe tshigs su bcad pa 'di skad smras so/ /yang dag sangs rgyas skye ba myed/ /rgyal ba mya ngan myi 'da' ste/ /rgyu mthun pa yi smon lam gyis/ /des ni rnam par
132a3(phal chen): 'phrul pa snang / /'di dag chos ni bsam mi khyab/ /'di dag sems ni spyod yul myin/ /gang gis ye shes pha rol phyin/ /des ni sangs rgyas spyod yul mthong / /lus 'di yang dag sangs rgyas
132a4(phal chen): myin/ /sgra yang de bzhin gshegs pa myin/ /lus dang sgra las gzhan na yang / /sangs rgyas rnam par 'phrul myi mthong / /sngon gyi las rnams ma gtogs par/ /rang byung rnams kyi spyod
132a5(phal chen): yul gyi/ /mchog gi tshul rnams shes pa ni/ /blo zhan rnams kyis mi nus so/ /yang dag sangs rgyas rnam 'phrul 'di/ /gang dag nas kyang ma 'ongs ste/ /gang du 'gro bar myi 'gyur ro/ /'di dag
132a6(phal chen): rang byung sku yin no/ /tshad myed shin tu 'dren pa rnams/ /chos 'di rab tu bshad mdzad kyang / /chos la gnas pa gang yang myed/ /zhing rnams bye ba kun na snang / /mkhyen pas mtha' dang dbus myed de/ /
132a7(phal chen): chos kun thugs su chud cing rtogs/ /chos kyi dbyings la rab zhugs nas/ /rnam par 'phrul pa ston pa mdzad/ /chos rnams kun la chags pa myed/ /'gro la de ni bsgribs mi mnga'/ /
132a8(phal chen): tshad med pa yi yon tan gyis/ /zhing rnams kun na rab tu snang / /gang zhig ye shes 'di dag dang / /ye shes thams cad rtogs 'dod pas/ /bsam pa rnam par spyad byas ste/ /byang chub spyod pa spyad
132b1(phal chen): par bya/ /drang srong chen pos byin gyis rlabs/ /'di 'dra gang gis mthong gyur cing / /da ni the tsom myi byed na/ /dge bshes mchog la bsnyen pa yin/ /de nas byang chub sems dpa' dam pa'i rgyal mtshan
132b2(phal chen): gyis/ sangs rgyas kyi byin gyis rlabs kyis phyogs bcur rnam par bltas nas/ de'i tshe tshigs su bcad pa 'di dag smras so/ /shin tu zab ste brjod du myed/ /brjod du yod kyang 'da' bar dka'/ /
132b3(phal chen): tshig gi lam las shin tu 'das/ /nam mkha' la ni rgyal ba snang / /de bzhin gshegs pa'i byin rlabs kyis/ /myi'i seng ge mthong bar 'gyur/ /yang dag sangs rgyas rtog med kyang / /rgyal ba rnam par
132b4(phal chen): rtog par snang / /'jig rten mgon pos chos nyid dngos/ /zab mo 'di dag yang dag bsnan/ /gang zag mtshungs pa med pa yi/ /des ni sku 'di rab tu 'byung / /thams cad gzigs kyi spyod yul gyi/ /
132b5(phal chen): ye shes chen po 'di 'dra ste/ /'di la gang zhig rtogs 'dod pa/ /des ni rgyal ba mngon du byos/ /yid kyi dbang po rnam dag pas/ /de bzhin gshegs pa bsnyen bskur zhing / /'di yi tshul las 'da'
132b6(phal chen): byed de/ /nam yang skyo bar mi bya'o/ /myi zad pa yi bsod nams dang / /byang chub sems dpa' bstan pa rnams/ /the tsom rnam par bzlog byas te/ /de dag la ni skyo med bltos/ /rgyal sras gang gis
132b7(phal chen): chos dbyings kyi/ /shin tu bstan pa'i mthar phyin pa/ /des ni kun gzigs rnam 'phrul ba/ /'di dag shin tu 'da' bar bya/ /dad pa chos 'di'i rtsa ba zhes/ /chos kyi phung pos bshad mdzad kyis/ /
132b8(phal chen): dad pa shin tu cher bskyed la/ /byang chub spyod pa spyad par gyis/ /sangs rgyas sting stang gang byed cing / /de bzhin gshegs la drin gzo ba/ /yang dag sangs rgyas dpal ldan pas/ /de dag
133a1(phal chen): rgyang ma ring gnas so/ /bdag nyid che ba 'di lta bu/ /gang gis thos mthong mkhas pa rnams/ /spyod yul thob par cis 'gyur ba'i/ /smon lam su zhig sbyong mi byed/ /de nas byang chub
133a2(phal chen): sems dpa' dpa' ba'i rgyal mtshan gyis sangs rgyas kyi byin gyi rlabs kyis phyogs bcur rnam par bltas nas/ de'i tshe tshigs su bcad pa 'di dag smras so/ /ji ltar nyi ma'i 'od snang bas/ /myig
133a3(phal chen): gis gzugs rnams mthong gyur pa/ /de bzhin sangs rgyas byin rlabs kyis/ /dad pa'i sems ldan rgyal ba mthong / /ji ltar brtson 'grus stobs ldan pa/ /rgya mtsho la ni 'jug par byed/ /de
133a4(phal chen): bzhin ye shes stobs ldan pas/ /bsam du myed pa'i sangs rgyas mthong / /ji ltar sa bon rnam dag pa/ /zhing bzang la ni skyer 'gyur ba/ /de bzhin sems bzang rnam dag la/ /sangs rgyas chos ni skye bar
133a5(phal chen): 'gyur/ /ji ltar nor gyi phung po yis/ /dbul ba thams cad spong byed pa/ /de bzhin sangs rgyas chos rnams kyis/ /byang chub sems dpa' rnam dag 'byung / /ji ltar dug du gyur pa la/ /nad myed dug sman rgyal
133a6(phal chen): bar byed/ /de bzhin nyon mongs rnam pa la/ /rnam dag tshul ni spyod yul lo/ /sangs rgyas kyis ni gang bsngags pa'i/ /dge ba'i gshes la brten byas na/ /de yi mthus ni sangs rgyas kyi/ /chos nyid
133a7(phal chen): 'di dag thos par 'gyur/ /skal ba bye ba grangs med pas/ /sbyin pa mchog rnams sbyin byas kyang / /'di yi tshul la rab spyod pa'i/ /grangs dang char yang myi 'gro'o/ /sangs rgyas yon tan mtha' yas te/ /mtshan
133a8(phal chen): gyis shin tu rnam par bris/ /brjod pas yang dag sangs rgyas rnams/ /rgyal ba shes par myi nus so/ /rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas rkang gnyis mchog /gnas nas g.yo ba myi mnga' bar/ /sku ni kun tu rnam rgyu
133b1(phal chen): zhing / /chos kyi dbyings ni ston pa mdzad/ /ji ltar nam mkha' khams 'di ni/ /nam yang rang bzhin mi 'gyur te/ /de bzhin sangs rgyas chos nyid kyang / /ngo bo nyid las 'gyur ba myed/ /de nas byang chub sems
133b2(phal chen): dpa' skar ma'i rgyal mtshan gyis/ sangs rgyas kyi byin gyi rlabs kyis/ phyogs bcur rnam par bltas te/ de'i tshe tshigs su bcad pa 'di smras so/ /myi yi 'jig rten 'di kun dang / /lha yi gnas rnams
133b3(phal chen): thams cad dang / /'gro ba ma lus kun na yang / /myi yi gtso bo shin tu snang / /ji ltar sems dngos gcig pu las/ /rnam pa tha dad sems brjod pa/ /de bzhin sangs rgyas sku gcig las/ /sangs rgyas thams
133b4(phal chen): cad brjod pa yin/ /byang chub gnyis su med pa brjod/ /byang chub de yang mtshan nyid med/ /mtshan kyis mngon par rnam bris pa'i/ /sku rnams gnyis su snang bar gyur/ /mkha' dang chos kyi dbyings la zhugs/
133b5(phal chen): sgyu ma'i sa yang rab tu bstan/ /de phyir sangs rgyas de dag gi/ spyod yul blta ba zad pa myed/ /yang dag sangs rgyas chos kyi sku/ /mgon po thams cad dus gsum du/ /ji ltar 'dul ba'i 'gro ba la/ /
133b6(phal chen): gzugs kyi sku yang rab tu snang / /'di 'dra'i lus su bdag gyur ces/ /sangs rgyas rtog par myi mdzad de/ /ston la rnam rtog myi mnga' yang / /byin gyi rlabs ni ston pa mdzad/ /dbyer myed pa yi dbyings la
133b7(phal chen): yang / /chos kyi dbyings ni yang dag gnas/ /'jig rten khams ni tshad myed par/ /thub pas rnam par rtog pa bstan/ /sku ni sprul pa ma yin te/ /sprul pa myin pa'ang sku ma yin/ /sprul pa myed pa'i
133b8(phal chen): chos 'di yis/ /sprul pa rnams ni rab tu bstan/ /yang dag sangs rgyas tshad myed pa/ /chos kyi dbyings la shin tu brten/ /mtha' dang dbus med rab tu zab/ /tshig gi lam gyis bzla bar
134a1(phal chen): dka'/ /kun tu 'gro ba'i chos rnams la/ /de bzhin gshegs pa don nges mkhyen/ /zhing rnams kun la chags mi mnga'/ /chos kyi dbyings la rnam par spyod/ /de nas byang chub sems dpa' ye
134a2(phal chen): shes rgyal mtshan gyis sangs rgyas kyi byin gyi brlabs kyis phyogs bcur rnam par bltas te/ de'i tshe tshigs su bcad pa 'di dag smras so/ /kun mkhyen ye shes ma chags pa/ /de la zhugs par
134a3(phal chen): gang gyur pa/ /de yi sems ni tshad mi zin/ /byang chub kyi ni spyad pa spyod/ /de bzhin gshegs pa mang po rnams/ /yul dang yul du de dag snang / /chos rnams phyogs gcig gang la yang / /yang dag
134a4(phal chen): sangs rgyas gnas pa med/ /'jig rten sgron ma de dag gis/ /byin gyi rlabs ni gang bstan pa/ /bskal pa bsam kyis mi khyab par/ /'di yi mtha' ni rnyed par dka'/ /dus gsum rnams ni ji snyed pa'i/ /
134a5(phal chen): sems can rnams kyi mthar thug pa/ /bgrang ba'i mthar ni phyin par nus/ /'dren pa la ni mthar thug myed/ /de dag sku ni gcig tu snang / /sku gnyis de dag bsam mi khyab/ /'jig rten khams su snang
134a6(phal chen): gyur kyang / /sku la gnyis su gyur pa myed/ /ji ltar zla ba shar gyur pa/ /tshad med pa yi gzugs brnyan rnams/ /chu yi snod du snang gyur kyang / /zla ba gnyis su gyur pa myed/ /de bzhin chags myed mkhyen
134a7(phal chen): ldan rnams/ /chags med rnam par 'tshang rgya ba/ /zhing rnams kun la rab tu snang / /sangs rgyas la ni gnyis kyang med/ /'di la gcig kyang yod ma yin/ /sku ni gnyis sam gsum du myed/ /ji ltar
134a8(phal chen): sems can bsam pa bzhin/ /tshad myed par ni rab tu snang / /sku ni 'das pa ma yin te/ /ma 'ongs par ni sku ma yin/ /skyes dang byang chub mya ngan 'das/ /skad gcig gis ni rab tu snang / /ji ltar sgyu mar gyur pa'i
134b1(phal chen): gzugs/ /skyes pa ma yin 'ongs pa myin/ /de ltar de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku/ /skye ba myed par shin tu bstan/ /de nas byang chub sems dpa' rin po che'i rgyal mtshan gyis/ sangs rgyas kyi byin gyi
134b2(phal chen): rlabs kyis phyogs bcur rnam par bltas te/ de'i tshe tshigs su bcad pa 'di dag smras so/ /yang dag sangs rgyas tshad myed pas/ /ched du sku yang rnam par bstan/ /ji ltar 'dul ba'i sems can rnams/
134b3(phal chen): de bzhin 'dren pas rab tu mthong / /sku la phyogs ni myed par brjod/ /sangs rgyas yul ni ma lus khyab/ /bar snang nam mkha' ji lta bar/ /de bzhin sangs rgyas bsam mi khyab/ /der ni sems la 'pho
134b4(phal chen): ba myed/ /sems la skye ba 'ang yod ma yin/ /sangs rgyas rnams kyi spyod yul ni/ /skye ba myed la rab tu gnas/ /ji ltar rab rib ldan pa'i myig /nang na myed cing phyi na 'ang myed/ /de bzhin 'jig rten sangs rgyas
134b5(phal chen): dag / nang na myi bzhugs phyi na 'ang myin/ /'jig rten kun kyi don kyi phyir/ /rkang gnyis kyi ni mchog byed de/ /'jig rten du mar byung ba yang / /'jig rten dag tu skye bos mthong / /sangs rgyas rnams la zhing myi
134b6(phal chen): gnas/ /rgyal ba dag la nyin mtshan med/ /skad gcig ma yin zla ba myin/ /rgyal ba la ni lo mi gnas/ /'jig rten dag na 'di skad brjod/ /nyi ma che ge mo zhig du/ /rang byung byang chub rgyal bas thob/
134b7(phal chen): sangs rgyas nyi ma rjes myi 'brang / /de la bskal pa yod ma yin/ /dus kyang ma lus med pa ste/ /dus gsum yang dag rdzogs sangs rgyas/ /mgon po rnams ni mnga' bar 'gyur/ /ji ltar nyi ma'i dkyil
134b8(phal chen): 'khor ni/ /nams kyang mtshan dang myi gnas ste/ /de bzhin sangs rgyas chos nyid do/ /bskal pa gcig dang dus gsum du/ /'dren par bzhugs pa ma yin te/ /dus gsum zhes kyang rab tu brjod/ /
135a1(phal chen): sangs rgyas rnams kyi chos nyid ltos/ /de nas byang chub sems dpa' rdul dang bral ba'i rgyal mtshan gyis/ sangs rgyas kyi byin gyi rlabs kyis phyogs bcur rnam par bltas te/ de'i tshe tshigs
135a2(phal chen): su bcad pa 'di dag smras so/ /yang dag sangs rgyas sku cig ste/ /'dren pa thams cad don gcig kyang / /tshad myed gzhan dang gzhan dag du/ /phyogs bcu kun na rab tu snang / /gang gis ma lus thams
135a3(phal chen): cad kyi/ /chos kyi dbyings rnams kun khyab pas/ /sems can gtso bo thub pa yin/ /spyod yul rnams ni ci 'dra ltos/ /sangs rgyas rnams kyi chos nyid ni/ /nang gi skus kyang snang ba myin/ /de bzhin
135a4(phal chen): gshegs pa'i byin gyis rlabs/ /phyi rol skus kyang myi snang ngo / /dus rnams kun tu las rnams gyis/ /ji ltar las rnams bstsags pa bzhin/ /de bzhin so sor phye ba'i skus/ /rigs su byung bar
135a5(phal chen): rab tu bstan/ /rgyal ba'i chos nyid ma gtogs par/ /sangs rgyas sku ni ci 'dra ba/ /grangs su bgrang bar myi nus te/ /bsam pas lta yang shes myi nus/ /ji ltar bdag cag sems kyi las/ /bsam
135a6(phal chen): gyis myi khyab myi 'byung ba/ /de bzhin sangs rgyas bsam myi khyab/ /sems kyi 'phrin las myi mnga'o/ /ji ltar zhing rnams bsam yas pa/ /sa la rnam par dag par mdzes/ /de bzhin sangs rgyas
135a7(phal chen): bsam mi khyab/ /'gro ba dag na mdzes par snang / /ji ltar las rnams 'jug pa ni/ /rkyen kyis rab tu 'byung 'gyur ba/ /de bzhin rgyu rnams 'thun pa las/ /sangs rgyas shin tu mthong bar 'gyur/ /yid
135a8(phal chen): bzhin nor bu'i rgyal po ni/ /ji ltar yid bsam rdzogs byed pa/ /de bzhin sangs rgyas chos nyid kyang / /rtag tu smon lam rdzogs par bsgrub/ /mtha' dang dbus med 'jig rten 'dir/ /'jig rten mgon po
135b1(phal chen): 'dren par 'gyur/ /de yi smon lam de dag gis/ /phyogs bcu 'di dag rgyal bas gang / /de nas byang chub sems dpa' dri ma myed pa'i rgyal mtshan gyis/ sangs rgyas kyi byin gyi brlabs kyis/ phyogs bcur

135b3(phal chen): rnams rab tu brjod/ /des ste sems can mnyam sangs rgyas/ /sems can la la bsam byas na/ /rgyal ba de dag thams cad mthong / /sangs rgyas la ni gshegs pa myed/ /sangs rgyas la ni dmigs
135b4(phal chen): byas nas/ /sems kyis sangs rgyas dmyigs pas na/ /sems bskyed pa dang rgyal mnyam par/ /de bzhin de dag rgyal ba mthong / /dkar po chos kyis nyer brtan cing / /gang gis grags pa rnam sbyangs pa/ /de dag
135b5(phal chen): thams cad sems bskyed la/ /shes rab ldan pa rab tu bzhugs/ /dmyigs pa dag dang byin gyis brlabs/ /myi yi gtso bo ston pa mdzad/ /de'i phyir dmyigs pa kun tu yang / /sangs rgyas rgyal ba gshegs
135b6(phal chen): par brjod/ /'jig rten khams rnams 'di dag ni/ /sangs rgyas sku rnams bdag gi myed/ /sems la bdag gi med pa bstan/ /byang chub rtogs la bdag gi med/ /mi yi seng ge'i chos nyid dang / /dpa' ba'i stobs
135b7(phal chen): la rab tu gnas/ /lus dang mtshan nyid mi 'dra ste/ /snang ba'i sems dang mnyam pa'i sku/ /ji ltar 'jig rten de bzhin sku/ /ji bzhin skur yang rgyal ba ste/ /sku yi rang bzhin shes pa ni/ /sangs rgyas chags
135b8(phal chen): pa med ces bya/ /sangs rgyas kun tu gzigs pa ste/ /chos rnams thams cad rab tu gzigs/ /sangs rgyas chos dang byang chub rnams/ /gang la'ang dmyigs pa med pa yin/ /sangs rgyas la ni gshegs
136a1(phal chen): pa myed/ /sangs rgyas gang na'ang mi bzhugs ste/ /yang dag sangs rgyas log pa myed/ /de bzhin gshegs pa len mi mnga'/ /de nas byang chub sems dpa' dpal gyi rgyal mtshan gyis sangs rgyas
136a2(phal chen): kyi byin gyis brlabs kyis phyogs bcur rnam par bltas te/ de'i tshe tshigs su bcad pa 'di dag smras so/ /sangs rgyas thams cad kun tu khyab/ /zhing gcig la ni mi gnas te/ /thams cad du ni sangs
136a3(phal chen): rgyas gshegs/ /zhing rnams kun tu rab tu snang / /sangs rgyas sku ni thams cad du/ /byin gyis brlabs dag rab tu 'byung / /'tshang rgya chos kyi 'khor lo dang / /bsam pa bzhin du mya ngan 'da'/ /sangs rgyas la

136a5(phal chen): du/ /gang dag chos rnams gcig tsam yang / /de bzhin nyid la mi 'jug go/ /'di ni 'jig rten 'di rgyal zhes/ /'jig rten dag na rnam rtog yod/ /gang gis ngo bo nyid shes na/ /'jig rten myed de rgyal ba med/ /

136b6(phal chen): sangs rgyas brjod 'gyur ba'i/ /chos 'di gang gis thos gyur pa/ /des ni myi bde kun kyis kyang / /spyad pa rnams ni blang bar bya/ /ji tsam chos kyi dbyings rnams dang / /dus gsum gyi ni mgon po yi/ /

137a5(phal chen): zhal bstan pa mthong ste/ de dag kyang 'di lta ste/ mtshan rdo rje'i rgyal mtshan zhes bya ba sha stag go/ phyogs gcig nas ji lta ba ltar phyogs bcu nas kyang de bzhin te/ de na sangs rgyas bcom ldan

137a8(phal chen): 'di'i sngon gyi smon lam dang / sngon gyi byin gyis brlabs dang / khyod kyi ye shes rnam par dag pa dang / byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi dge ba'i rtsa bas brtan pa'i phyir/ 'di lta ste/ byang chub sems

137b8(phal chen): dag par gzung bar bya ba'i phyir byin gyis brlabs pa mdzad kyis/ kye rigs kyi bu khyod kyis de bzhin gshegs pa'i mthu dang / sangs rgyas kyi byin gyis brlabs dang /

147a4(phal chen): myed yid ldan pa/ /sangs rgyas yon tan rtag tu sbyor zhing tshol/ /gang zhig mtshungs med skyes bu 'dul drung du/ /bsam pa dri ma med par rnam sbyangs shing / /chos mkhas 'gro ba bskyab pa'i sems

152a6(phal chen): chos dkar po snang bar 'gyur pas/ nye bar brtan cing yongs su bsngo ba'i mchog skyes bu dam pas spyad pa dang ldan pa dang / yongs su dag pa'i yid kyis yang dag par rtog pa dang / sems
152a7(phal chen): dang 'dra ba'i chos thams cad la zhugs pa dang / sgyu ma dang 'dra ba'i las yongs su shes pa dang / myig yor lta bu'i las kyi rnam par smyin pa la mos pa dang / sprul pa lta bu'i mngon par 'du
152a8(phal chen): byed pa la gnas pa dang / sgra rnyan lta bu'i las la rten pa dang / grib ma lta bu'i byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa'i rjes su song ba dang / chags pa med pa'i chos kyi myig rab tu skyes pa dang /
152b1(phal chen): bya ba med pa'i 'byam klas pa'i rjes su song ba dang / zhi ba'i rigs rab tu thob pa dang / gnyis su myed pa dang ldan pa'i 'dus byas dang 'dus ma byas kyi chos thams cad la rab tu zhugs pa dang / chos ma
152b2(phal chen): nor ba'i mtshan ma thob par bya ba dang / byang chub sems dpa'i spyad pa thams cad kyi rjes su song ba dang / mtshan ma thams cad la zhen pa med pa dang / thun mong gi las la mkhas pa rjes su song ba dang
152b3(phal chen): chos dkar po thams cad rgyun ma chad pa dang / chags pa thams cad kyis mngon par ma zhen pa dang / chags pa med par 'gro ba la rten pa dang ldan pa yin te/ de ltar byang chub sems dpa'
152b4(phal chen): sems dpa' chen po shin tu bsam pa'i blo dang ldan pa/ dge ba'i rtsa ba la rmongs pa med pa/ chos thams cad dang 'gal ba myed pa'i chos can rgyu dang las dang bya ba dang / 'gal ba med pa yang dag par
152b5(phal chen): mthong ba yongs su bsngo ba la mkhas pa/ ngo bo nyid kyi chos kyi tshul dang las rnam par smyin pa mngon par bsgrub pa'i/ pha rol tu phyin pa chos thams cad la rnam par lta zhing rnam par dpyod pa'i
152b6(phal chen): ye shes dang ldan pa/ yongs su bsngo ba'i ye shes chen po mngon par shes pa la shin tu rig pa'i dge ba'i rtsa ba dang ldan pa/ mngon par 'du bya ba med par spyod pa'i sems dge ba'i rtsa ba dang ldan pa de/
152b7(phal chen): dge ba'i rtsa ba de dag 'di ltar ci nas kyang 'gro ba thams cad yongs su dgrol ba dang / sangs rgyas kyi rigs bdud kyi las dang bral ba/ las kyi rnam par yongs su byang ba'i bdag nyid can thams cad
152b8(phal chen): mkhyen pa nyid du mos shing rjes su song ba'i sems dang ldan par 'gyur bar yongs su bsngo'o/ /bsngo ba de yang tshad med pa'i ye shes khong du chud par bya ba'i phyir yang dag par mthong bar byed de/ dge
153a1(phal chen): ba'i rtsa ba de dag 'jig rten gyi yul dang bral ba nyon mongs pa thams cad dang rnam par bral bar yongs su bsngo'o/ /sems can thams cad shin tu rnam par byang bar bya ba'i phyir yang yongs su bsngo ste/
153a2(phal chen): ye shes rnam par dag pa'i mthar thug par zab pa'i tshul gyis dge ba'i rtsa ba de dag ci nas kyang 'khor ba'i chos kyis mi bskyod cing sangs rgyas kyi dge ba'i rtsa ba mngon par 'byung bar sems bskyed pa dang
153a3(phal chen): ldan par yongs su bsngo'o/ /dge ba'i rtsa ba de dag yongs su bsngo ba'i tshe yang bdud kyi las thams cad las rnam par bzlog ste/ chos mnyam pa nyid kyi rgya yongs su bsngo ba'i ye shes kyi rjes su song
153a4(phal chen): ba las rgyas 'debs par byed do/ /dge ba'i rtsa ba de dag thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyi longs spyod kyi phyir yang chos thams cad 'jig rten las 'das par khong du chud pa'i phyir yongs su bsngo'o/ /de ltar
153a5(phal chen): byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po dge ba'i rtsa ba de dag yongs su bsngo ba ni thams cad mkhyen pa'i theg pa'i dkyil 'khor yongs su grub pas 'gyod pa med pa'i dge ba'i rtsa ba dang ldan pa yin te/ kye
153a6(phal chen): rgyal ba'i sras dag / 'di ni byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi yongs su bsngo ba mi phyed pa dang ldan pa zhes bya ba ste gnyis pa'o/ /yongs su bsngo ba de dang ldan pa'i byang chub sems dpa' ni dge ba'i rtsa ba
153a7(phal chen): thams cad yongs su bsngo zhing / sangs rgyas grangs med pa mngon sum du bya ba thob par 'gyur ro/ /chos brjod du med pa yongs su dag pa yang yongs su rdzogs par byed de/ sems can thams cad mnyam
153a8(phal chen): pa nyid kyang khong du chud par byed do/ /chos thams cad la 'jug pa rmongs pa med pa la yang rab tu 'jug go/ sangs rgyas thams cad kyi byin gyis rlabs bdud kyi las thams cad rab tu 'joms pa yang
153b1(phal chen): yongs su bsgrub bo/ /mngon par skyes pa'i byang chub kyi sems kyang yongs su rdzogs par 'grub par 'gyur ro/ /chags pa myed pa la rab tu 'jug pa'i phyir gzhan gyi dring mi 'jog pa la yang dag par
153b2(phal chen): 'grub po/ /chos thams cad kyi don mthong ba yang rab tu 'thob bo/ /sangs rgyas kyi zhing thams cad rjes su song ba'i 'du shes kyi gnas kyang rab tu rtogs par byed do/ /'gro ba thams cad yongs su snang
153b3(phal chen): bar bya ba'i yongs su dag pa'ang yongs su bsgrub bo/ /de nas byang chub sems dpa' rdo rje rgyal mtshan gyis/ sangs rgyas kyi byin gyis rlabs kyis phyogs bcur rnam par bltas te/ de'i tshe tshigs su
153b4(phal chen): bcad pa 'di dag smras so/ /de dag yid kyis dbye ba med bsgyur cing / /ji snyed las rnams yang dag brtson byed kun/ /ci nas rgyal ba mngon par mnyes 'gyur ba/ /de ltar 'jig rten mkhas la yongs su
153b5(phal chen): bsngo bar byed/ /sangs rgyas bsam du med pa bsnyen bkur cing / /sbyin dul sdom pa mchog gi tshul khrims rnams/ /ci nas 'gro kun rnam par dag 'gyur ba/ /de ltar 'jig rten phan phyir yongs su bsngo/ /
153b6(phal chen): ji snyed 'di na spos kyi gzhal med khang / /me tog rnam pa na bza'i rnam pa dang / /lhab lhub rnam pa gdugs kyi rnam pa dag /des ni ye shes mkhas la bsnyen bkur byed/ /de ltar skyes bu seng ge drang
153b7(phal chen): srong rnams/ /bskal pa bsam yas bsnyen cing bkur byas kyang / /rgyal ba skyes bu 'dul ba mchod byas pas/ /nam yang ngoms par tshor bar mi 'gyur ro/ /de dag rgyal ba kun la mos byed cing / /
153b8(phal chen): phyogs rnams kun kyi 'jig rten sgron ma rnams/ /mi yi seng ge mtshungs myed ji snyed pa/ /'jig rten phyogs bcu dag na bzhugs par mthong / /bskal pa bsam gyis mi khyab rnam mang du/ /
154a1(phal chen): mi ngoms yid kyis sbyin pa gtong byed cing / /dge ba de la rjes su sems byed pas/ /bskal pa brgyar yang ngoms par mi tshor ro/ /'gro ba'i 'du shes rnam rtog rab shes kyang / /de la de ni
154a2(phal chen): mi rtog rnam myi rtog / de dag 'gro ba'i dbang po ma lus shes/ /de dag phan phyir rtag tu 'jug par byed/ /de dag dga' zhing mnyam par gzhag pa sems/ /dad pa 'di bstsal srid zhu ldan pa rnams/ /
154a3(phal chen): bsam yas bskal par 'jig rten 'gro phan phyir/ /yongs su dgrol ba'i sems kyis spro bar byed/ /de dag bde gshegs mya ngan 'das pa las/ /sna tshogs rnam pa tha dad yid 'ong ba'i/ /mchod
154a4(phal chen): rten bsam gyis myi khyab rtsig byed cing / /mchod pa byed kyang nam yang tshim pa myed/ /mtshungs med de dag sku gzugs rnam dag pa/ /rab tu 'od 'bar gser gyi snying po can/ /rgyal ba'i sku
154a5(phal chen): gzugs ri rab mnyam pa dag / bye ba brgya phrag mtha' yas rab tu byed/ /zil non dam pa rnyed pa de dag ni/ /bsod nams yangs pa'i stobs de grub pa na/ /de dag yongs bsngo shes pa rab rtogs shing / /
154a6(phal chen): dngos dang dngos med thams cad rab tu bsgom/ /'di 'dra'i ye shes tshul la yongs bsngos pas/ /de phyir 'khor bas zad par mi 'gyur te/ /chos nyid ye shes mchog dang dam pa dag /de la chos rnams
154a7(phal chen): skye ba gang yang myed/ /des ni 'jig rten mkhyen pa rnam dag ltar/ /sems kyang rab tu rnam par dag par 'gyur/ /des ni mi zad mthar phyin tshul rtogs pa/ /'dus byas bsod nams zad par 'gyur
154a8(phal chen): ba myed/ /gang rnams byang chub sems dang ldan 'gyur cing / /'jig rten kun la gnas pa med pa dag /'gro ba kun la chags pa med pa yin/ /phyogs rnams kun tu 'ang mtha' yas rab tu
154b1(phal chen): 'gro/ /gang gis mi yi dbang po kun 'byung ba/ /de 'dra yongs su bsngo ba byed par 'gyur/ /'gro ba thams cad sems dang mnyam rtogs kyang / /'gro ba kun tu sems ni dmyigs pa myed/ /de dag dngos po
154b2(phal chen): thams cad ma lus par/ /chos rnams dngos med ji bzhin 'jug pa med/ /ci nas 'jig rten lam du nyams med par/ /rnam dag myig can yongs su bsngo ba byed/ /des ni srid rnams yongs su dag par
154b3(phal chen): bsngo/ /dngos su srid pa rtog par mi byed de/ /dngos dang dngos med tshul ni shes byed cing / /'od gsal dang bas sems kyang tshim par byed/ /sangs rgyas zhing gcig gnas par mi byed de/ /zhing rnams ma
154b4(phal chen): lus kun la'ang gnas mi 'cha'/ /'dus byas chos kyis snyems par mi byed de/ /de dag rang bzhin la 'ang myi gnas so/ /ci nas rgyal ba kun kyi kun mkhyen pa/ /ci nas bla med sangs rgyas rgyan thob
154b5(phal chen): cing / /ci nas rgyal ba thams cad mnyes 'gyur ba/ /de ltar de dag las ni yongs su bsngo/ /ye shes dam pa'i rnam pa tshul shes pa/ /de dag rkang gnyis dam pa dran byed cing / /de 'dra'i chos rnams
154b6(phal chen): gnas med rab shes pas/ /de 'dra'i bsod nams gnas pa med par 'gyur/ /de dag 'gro ba kun kyi skyabs yin te/ /las kyi mtha' rnams thams cad rnam par sbyangs/ /'gro ba kun la phan dang
154b7(phal chen): bde sems kyis/ /'jig rten yongs su spang ba gang yang med/ /chos dang bar du mya ngan 'da' ba dag /gang phyir gzhan myin 'grangs pa'i sa la srung / /gang gis rgyal 'gyur sangs rgyas gyur pa'i
154b8(phal chen): rnams/ /de ltar dge ba de dag yongs su bsngo/ /'jig rten 'gro ba'i rgyud la rlom sems med/ /'dus byas rnams la'ang de dag chags pa med/ /tshig gi lam la de dag gnas pa myed/ /
155a1(phal chen): tshig med lam la'ang nams kyang myi gnas so/ /chos rnams thams cad ma lus bsdu mdzad de/ /mi yi dam pa sangs rgyas ji snyed pas/ /'gro rgyud thams cad rnam par phye bas mkhyen/ /
155a2(phal chen): thugs kyis rnam par dbye dang rtog mi mnga'/ /rgyan cig las ni rgyan rnams kun 'byin kyang / /rnam par rtog pa'i chos su myi byed de/ /de dag thams cad dngos med spyod myed par/ /'jig rten rtog
155a3(phal chen): pa med par rab tu shes/ /mi phyed pa dang ldan pa zhes bya ba ste yongs su bsngo ba gnyis pa'o// //sangs rgyas rmad ga cad ces bya ba shin tu rgyas pa chen po'i mdo/ bam po
155a4(phal chen): bcu gnyis pa/ /kye rgyal ba'i sras dag /byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rnams kyi yongs su bsngo ba sangs rgyas thams cad la yang dag par bskyed pa zhes bya ba
155a5(phal chen): gsum pa gang zhe na/ kye rgyal ba'i sras dag /'di la byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po 'das pa'i sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyis yongs su bsngo ba la yang rjes su slob bo/ /ma byon
155a6(phal chen): pa'i sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyis yongs su bsngo ba la'ang rjes su slob bo/ /da ltar byung ba'i sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyis yongs su bsngo ba la'ang rjes su slob po/ /de byang
155a7(phal chen): chub sems dpa'i spyad pa spyod pa'i tshe/ mi 'thun pa ma yin zhing yid du 'ong ba'am/ mi 'thun pa ma yin zhing yid du 'ong bar reg pa'am/ mi 'thun pa ma yin zhing yid du 'ong ba'i chos sam/ mi 'thun pa ma
155a8(phal chen): yin zhing kha na ma tho ba myed pa rnam par dag pa/ dge ba yangs pa/ 'od gsal ba/ gang gis yid dga' ba skye zhing bde bar 'gyur ba/ dang ba skye ba/ dga' ba skye ba/ rab tu dga' bar gnas pa/ spro ba
155b1(phal chen): rab tu 'byung ba yid mi bde ba rnam par bzlog pa/ sems bde bar 'gyur ba'am/ nyams dga' bar 'gyur ba/ bsam pa 'jam par 'gyur ba'am/ dbang po sim par gyur ba'i gzugs gang ji
155b2(phal chen): snyed yod pa de dag thams cad mthong bar gyur te/ de bde ba'i gzugs de dag mthong ba'i tshe/ 'di ltar yongs su bsngo ste/ de dag gi bde ba yongs su bsngo ba 'dis sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das
155b3(phal chen): de dag sangs rgyas kyi rnam par spyod pa'i bde ba bsam gyis mi khyab pa dang / phyi phyir zhing yang ldan par gyur cig /sangs rgyas kyi ting nge 'dzin gyi bde ba mtshungs pa myed pas yang dag par gzung
155b4(phal chen): bar gyur cig / sangs rgyas kyi thugs rje chen po'i bde ba mtha' yas pa phyir zhing yang shin tu brtan par gyur cig /sangs rgyas kyi rnam par thar pa'i bde ba tshad med pa dang yang dag par ldan
155b5(phal chen): par gyur cig / sangs rgyas kyi cho 'phrul tshad myed pas shin tu gzung bar gyur cig /sangs rgyas kyi khyu mchog gi mthu phyung ba'i bde ba rnyed par dka' bas shin tu khyab par gyur cig /
155b6(phal chen): sangs rgyas kyi stobs kyi bde ba tshad myed pas shin tu bde bar gyur cig /tshor ba thams cad zhi zhing skye ba med pa'i bde bas 'gyur ba med par gyur cig /chags pa med par gnas pa rtag tu
155b7(phal chen): mnyam par gzhag pa'i de bzhin gshegs pa'i bde ba gnyis su med cing yang dag par spyod pas 'khrug pa myed pa bde bar gyur cig ces/ de ltar byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen
155b8(phal chen): pos dge ba'i rtsa ba de dag de bzhin gshegs pa rnams la yongs su bsngos nas/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams la yongs su bsngo ba byed de/ 'di ltar bsam pa yongs su ma rdzogs pa rnams kyi
156a1(phal chen): bsam pa yongs su rdzogs par 'gyur ba'i phyir yongs su bsngo'o/ /lhag pa'i bsam pa yongs su ma dag pa rnams yongs su dag par bya ba dang / pha rol tu phyin pa yongs su ma rdzogs
156a2(phal chen): pa thams cad yongs su rdzogs par bya ba dang / byang chub kyi sems rdo rje lta bu shin tu brtan par bya ba dang / thams cad mkhyen pa'i go ca phyir mi ldog pa rgyun mi 'chad par bya ba dang / byang chub tu
156a3(phal chen): gzhol ba'i dge ba'i rtsa ba rnams yongs su bsrung ba dang / 'gro ba thams cad dang mnyam pa'i byang chub kyi sems bskyed pa'i smon lam yongs su rdzogs par bya ba dang / byang chub sems dpa' thams cad kyi rnam
156a4(phal chen): par spyod pa thob par bya ba dang / byang chub sems dpa' dbang po thams cad kyi mngon par shes pa shin tu rno bar bya ba dang / byang chub sems dpa' thams cad kyi dge ba'i rtsa ba thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du thug
156a5(phal chen): par 'gyur bar bya ba'i phyir yongs su bsngo ste/ de ltar dge ba'i rtsa ba de dag thams cad byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi don du yongs su bsngo'o/ /de yang dge ba'i rtsa ba chung ngu na se gol tog pa rtsam du
156a6(phal chen): sangs rgyas zhi ba'i sgra thos sam/ chos nyan tam/ 'phags pa'i dge 'dun bsnyen bkur byed dam/ gang ci yang rung ste/ dge ba'i rtsa ba de dag sems can thams cad la bar chad med par yongs
156a7(phal chen): su bsngo'o/ /sangs rgyas rjes su dran pa yongs su rdzogs par yongs su bsngo'o/ /chos rjes su dran pa rab tu sbyor bar yongs su bsngo'o/ /'phags pa'i dge 'dun rim gror bya bar yongs su
156a8(phal chen): bsngo'o/ /sangs rgyas mthong ba dang mi 'bral bar yongs su bsngo'o/ /sems rnam par dag par yongs su bsngo'o/ /sangs rgyas kyi chos khong du chud par yongs su bsngo'o/ /tshad myed
156b1(phal chen): pa'i yon tan la rab tu 'jug pa'i phyir yongs su bsngo'o/ /mngon par shes pa dang dge ba'i rtsa ba rnam par dag pa'i phyir yongs su bsngo'o/ /chos kyi the tsom rnam par bstsal ba'i phyir yongs su bsngo'o/ /
156b2(phal chen): ji ltar nyan thos dang / rang sangs rgyas rnam par dag pa bstan pa la spyod pa'i sems can rnams la yongs su bsngo ba de bzhin du/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po de dge ba'i rtsa ba de dag
156b3(phal chen): sems can thams cad la'ang yongs su bsngo ste/ 'di ltar sems can dmyal ba'i lam rnam par bzlog par bya ba'i phyir yongs su bsngo'o/ /byol song gi skye gnas rgyun gcod pa'i phyir yongs su bsngo'o/ /
156b4(phal chen): gshin rje'i 'jig rten rtsa ba nas chad pa'i phyir yongs su bsngo'o/ /ngan song gi rgyud thams cad ma lus par rgyun gcod pa'i phyir yongs su bsngo'o/ /sems can de dag thams cad kyang bla na myed pa'i byang chub
156b5(phal chen): du mos shing phyir mi ldog pa'i phyir yongs su bsngo'o/ /lhag pa'i bsam pas thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du sems bskyed pa rab tu thob par bya ba'i phyir yongs su bsngo'o/ /sangs rgyas kyi chos
156b6(phal chen): thams cad mi spang ba'i phyir yongs su bsngo'o/ /thams cad mkhyen pa'i sa shin tu bde ba thob par bya ba'i phyir yongs su bsngo'o/ /sems can thams cad shin tu rnam par dag par bya ba'i phyir
156b7(phal chen): yongs su bsngo'o/ /sems can thams cad ye shes mtha' yas pa khong du chud par bya ba'i phyir yongs su bsngo'o/ /byang chub sems dpa' ni dge ba'i rtsa ba gang yang rung ste/ byang chub du dmyigs
156b8(phal chen): pa dang ma bral ba'i sems dang / thams cad mkhyen par dmyigs pa la brtson pa'i yid la byed pa dang / bdag gdul ba dang pha rol gdul ba la gzhol ba'i lhag pa'i bsam pa dang / bdag
157a1(phal chen): dang gzhan yongs su smyin par sbyor ba'i thabs mkhas pa dang / byang chub pa'i tshul dang ye shes kyi rjes su 'brang bas yongs su smyin par byed pa'i rnam par thar pa dang / sems bskyed pa gnas pa
157a2(phal chen): med pa dang / 'grogs pa'i mnyam par gzhag pa dang / sngon snying rje chen po bskyed pas khyim na gnas pa dang / byams pa'i sems dang ldan pas rang gi chung ma'i rjes su 'brang ba dang / sbyor ba nyams pa myed
157a3(phal chen): pa dang / byang chub sems dpa'i lam shin tu rnam par dag pas brtson pa dang / yang dag par brtson pa dang / bsgrub pa dang / yang dag par bsgrub pa dang / skyed pa dang yang dag par bskyed pa dang / dmyigs pa chen
157a4(phal chen): pos yang dag par sdud pa dang / grub par byed pa dang / rgya cher byed pa dang / yongs su rdzogs par byed pa dang / khyim na gnas pa dang / bu dang 'grogs shing gnas pa na 'di ltar yongs su bsngo ste/ byang chub sems
157a5(phal chen): dpa' khyim na gnas pa'i tshe gang ci yang rung ste/ gos dang zas dang mal stan dang / nad kyi rkyen sman dang / yo byad dang 'gro ba dang 'ong ba dang / spyod pa dang / ldan pa dang ston pa dang / skye mched 'byung ba'i las dang /
157a6(phal chen): spyod lam la gnas pa dang / spyod lam brtul ba dang / lus dang ngag gi las spyod pa dang / dbang po drug bsdams pa dang / rang gi lus phyi ba dang / mnye ba dang / khrus byed pa dang / zos pa dang / 'thungs pa dang /
157a7(phal chen): 'chos pa dang / myangs pa dang / brkyang ba dang / bskum pa dang / lta ba dang / kun tu lta ba dang / log pa dang sad pa dang / rang gi lus brtan par bya ba dang / de dag thams cad byang chub sems dpa' thams cad
157a8(phal chen): mkhyen pa'i sems dang ldan pa/ thams cad mkhyen par dmyigs pa la brtson pa/ sems can thams cad la phan pa dang / bde bar sems dpa'/ byang chub du smon lam tshad med pa btab pa
157b1(phal chen): sems tshad myed pa dang ldan pa/ dge ba'i rtsa ba rgya chen po yongs su sdud pa/ 'gro ba thams cad bskyab par brtson pa/ dge ba'i rtsa ba la rtag tu brtson pa/ rlom pa dang bag myed pa rnam par bzlog pa/
157b2(phal chen): thams cad mkhyen pa'i chos nyid la rab tu brten pa/ rnam par shes pa dang sems bskyed pa dang / yid la byed pa gzhan med pa/ sangs rgyas thams cad kyi byang chub la mngon par gnas pa nyon mongs pa'i
157b3(phal chen): phyogs thams cad las phyir phyogs pa/ byang chub sems dpa' thams cad kyi bslab pa la slob pa'i sems dang ldan pa/ thams cad mkhyen pa'i lam nyams pa myed pa/ ye shes kyi sa la rten pa/
157b4(phal chen): ston pa'i sa dang ldan pa/ dge ba'i rtsa bas shes rab che ba/ bung ba bzhin du dge ba'i rtsa ba'i tshogs chen po bstsags pa/ 'gro ba thams cad rgyud shin tu 'phags pa/ 'du byed la mngon par zhen pa myed
157b5(phal chen): pa/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi gdam ngag 'thun par 'dzin pas/ thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du ma bsngos pa gang yang med de/ de ltar byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po khyim na
157b6(phal chen): gnas pa'i tshe/ dge ba'i rtsa ba de dag yang dag pa bsdud pa sgrub pa yongs su bsngo ste de ltar de chung ngu na khyi'i lam gyi rgyud du gtogs pa dang / de ma yin pa'i byol song gi rigs su gtogs pa la zas sna

210b1(phal chen): mched la yang dag par btang ba'i sems dang / dus gsum gyi byang chub sems dpa' dang / mnyam par byas pa'i sbyin pa dang / gtong ba'i sems dang / zhe sdang ba myed pa'i myig gis dad pa myi zlog pa'i
210b2(phal chen): dbang dang / slong ba rnams la phan 'dogs pa'i sems dang / sangs rgyas kyi spyan la gzhol bas byang chub sems dpa'i theg pa chen po dang / byams pa dang / snying rje yongs su bsgoms pa dang
210b3(phal chen): dbang po drug shin tu bsdams pas slong ba rnams la myig sbyin pa de bzhin du de yang myig yongs su gtong zhing chos de lta bu la zhugs pa'i sems kyis slong ba dang / 'dod pa dag la sbyin pa byed cing mchod
210b4(phal chen): sbyin gyi don la 'jug pa dang / chos kyi mthu shin tu bskyed pa dang / 'jig rten thams cad kyi dga' bar blta ba dang / bag myed pa'i srid pa rnam par bzlog par byed pa dang / 'jig rten gyi
210b5(phal chen): dga' ba dang / 'dod pa sna tshogs mthong bas rang gi dga' ba khong du chud par byed pa dang / byang chub sems dpa'i dga' ba myong bar byed pa dang / ci bslangs pa'i dngos pos kha myi stong
210b6(phal chen): par byed pa dang / myi gnyis pa'i sbyin pa rjes su srung ba dang / rlom sems myed pas shin tu sbyin pa yongs su gtong ba dang / slong ba rnams kyis dngos po ci bslangs pa sbyin par byed pa'i
210b7(phal chen): tshe/ dge ba'i rtsa ba de dag 'di ltar yongs su bsngo ste/ dge ba'i rtsa ba 'dis sems can thams cad 'gro ba thams cad kyi myig du gyur te/ myig gi dam par gyur cig /sems can
210b8(phal chen): thams cad ye shes kyi mdzod shin tu yangs pas nyams pa myed pa'i myig du gyur cig / sems can thams cad snang ba myi 'phrogs pa dang ldan zhing sha'i myig rnam par dag pa yongs su
211a1(phal chen): grub par gyur cig / sems can thams cad shi 'pho dang / skye ba shes shing lha'i myig rnam par dag par gyur cig /sems can thams cad de bzhin gshegs pa'i ye shes kyi
211a2(phal chen): rjes su 'dong zhing chos kyi myig rab tu thob par gyur cig / sems can thams cad btong ba thams cad rnam par ston pas shes rab kyi myig thob par gyur cig /sems can thams cad chos
211a3(phal chen): thams cad mngon par 'tshang rgya ba'i phyir/ sangs rgyas kyis spyan dang ldan par gyur cig /sems can thams cad chags pa myed pa'i myig gi mthar thug ste/ kun tu lta ba'i myig dang
211a4(phal chen): ldan par gyur cig / sems can thams cad sems can gyi khams yongs su shes shing / rab rib myed pa'i myig dang ldan par gyur cig /sems can thams cad stobs bcu mnga' ba'i
211a5(phal chen): de bzhin gshegs par phyin pa sgrib pa myed pa'i myig dang ldan par gyur cig ces/ de ltar byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po myig yongs su gtong ba na/ thams cad mkhyen pa'i tshad kyi
211a6(phal chen): myig gi chos sems can thams cad yongs su bsngo ba la nye bar 'god do/ / //sangs rgyas rmad ga cad ces bya ba shin tu rgyas pa chen po'i mdo/ bam po bcu drug pa/ 'di ltar
211a7(phal chen): yang byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po ji ltar rgyal po khyad par du 'gro ba dang / byang chub sems dpa' mdud pa myed pa spyi gtsug yongs su btang ba bzhin du slong ba nye bar 'ongs
211a8(phal chen): pa la byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa blang ba'i sems dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i rigs dang ldan par byung bas/ sangs rgyas kyi rigs su byung ba'i sbyin pa'i sems dang /
211b1(phal chen): byang chub sems dpa' thams cad rjes su dran pa'i spyod pa la brtson pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi byang chub tu mthun par skyes pa dang / dbang po dang / ye shes dang / yon tan gyis shin tu brtson pa dang
211b2(phal chen): khams gsum ma dag cing snying po myed pa la snying por rab tu rtogs pa dang / sangs rgyas dang byang chub sems dpa' blta ba rab tu thob pas/ rang gi lus la chags pa myed pa'i sems dang /
211b3(phal chen): gnas med pa'i sangs rgyas kyi chos thams cad rjes su dran par gnas pa dang / dul ba dang zhi ba'i sems dang / dbang po'i rgyu ba shin tu zhi ba dang / 'gro ba mya ngan thams cad nas sems can gdon
211b4(phal chen): par sems dpa'i ye shes 'byung ba'i shes rab dang / bsod nams kyi 'byung gnas dang / rgyud ched du brjod pa rgya mtsho gtong ba'i sems yangs par byas pa dang / don la rnam par nges
211b5(phal chen): pa'i chos dang / mgon po thams cad kyi lam du 'jug pa dang / chos kyi dbang phyug la ye shes kyis dpyod pa dang / rang gi lus snying po myed pa las snying po blang ba'i blos yongs su gtong
211b6(phal chen): ba'i tshe/ rna ba dang / sna yongs su btang bas yang dag par bzung ba'i dge ba'i rtsa ba de 'di ltar yongs su bsngo ste/ dge ba'i rtsa ba 'dis sems can thams cad chos kyi sgra rnam par rig
211b7(phal chen): par bya ba la chags pa myed pa'i rna ba dang ldan par gyur cig / sems can thams cad kyis sgra thams cad skad ji lta ba bzhin du shes par bya ba'i phyir sgrib pa myed pa'i rna ba dang ldan par gyur cig /
211b8(phal chen): sems can thams cad sangs rgyas kyi snyan dang ldan pas thogs pa myed pa'i rna ba dang ldan par gyur cig /sems can thams cad rna ba'i skye mched shin tu bsgoms pas rna ba rnam par dag
212a1(phal chen): par gyur cig / sems can thams cad rnam par shes pa zhi ba skye ba'i phyir bsgrib pa myed pa'i rna ba dang ldan par gyur cig /sems can thams cad sangs rgyas thams cad

212a3(phal chen): dang ldan par gyur cig / sems can thams cad phyir rgol ba 'jig par byed pa shes pa la myi phyed pa'i rna ba dang ldan par gyur cig /sems can thams cad rna ba shin tu dag pa la dbang
212a4(phal chen): bsgyur ba'i sa kun tu 'jug pa'i rna ba dang ldan par gyur cig / sems can thams cad sangs rgyas kyi snyan rab tu thob par bya ba thob pas lha'i rna ba rab tu thob par gyur cig ces/

212a6(phal chen): su bsngos nas/ sna rnam par dag par yongs su bsngo ste/ sems can thams cad legs par mthong ba'i sna dang / dpe byad bzang po'i sna dang / mtshan bzang po'i sna dang /
212a7(phal chen): shin tu yid du 'ong ba'i sna dang / rnam par dag pa'i sna dang / rim gyis gzhol ba'i sna dang / mdzes pa 'phags pa'i sna dang / dgra thams cad rab tu 'dul ba'i sna dang / blta
212a8(phal chen): na sdug pa'i sna dang / de bzhin gshegs pa sangs rgyas kyi shangs rab tu 'thob pa'i phyir yongs su bsngo'o/ /sems can thams cad ngo la myi sdug pa med pa dang chos thams
212b1(phal chen): cad la chags pa myed pa'i ngo dang / lta na sdug pa'i ngo dang / myi mthun pa myed pa'i ngo dang / shin tu rnam par dag pa'i ngo dang / kha na ma tho ba myed pa'i ngo dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i zhal gyi

212b4(phal chen): cad la rab tu 'jug par 'gyur ba dang / ci nas kyang sems can thams cad kyi sangs rgyas kyi chos thams cad shin tu 'dus par 'gyur ba dang / ci nas kyang sems can thams cad
212b5(phal chen): kyis sangs rgyas kyi chos thams cad shin tu shes par 'gyur ba dang / ci nas kyang sems can thams cad sangs rgyas kyi chos thams cad la shin tu 'jug par 'gyur ba dang / ci nas

212b7(phal chen): ba dang / ci nas kyang sems can thams cad shin tu zil gyis myi non pa'i yongs su dag pa thob par 'gyur ba dang / ci nas kyang sems can thams cad kyis sangs rgyas kyi chos thams

213a2(phal chen): dpa' sems dpa' chen po skyed pa zil gyis myi non pa'i sa la gnas te/ u dum ba ra ltar shin tu dkon par sems pa'i sems rnam par dag pa dang / gtong ba myi zad cing 'byam klas
213a3(phal chen): pa / dad cing klung sprugs te gtang ba'i sems dang / yongs su gtong ba'i blo mtha' yas pa dang / dul ba dang / yongs su dul ba'i yid kyis gtong ba'i dbang po dang / gtong ba thams cad

213a5(phal chen): gtong ba dang / mchog tu gtong ba'i sems kyis rang gi lus dang / yan lag dang / gdong gis kyang phan 'dogs pa dang / myi smad par gtong ba'i sems kyis rnam pa de lta bu'i chos la
213a6(phal chen): rab tu gnas te ji ltar rgyal po me tog so dang / glang po'i rgyal po mche ba drug pas so ji ltar byin pa de bzhin du rang gi lus dang / kha nas so yongs su gtong ba'i tshe/ dge ba'i rtsa ba de dag
213a7(phal chen): 'di ltar yongs su bsngo ste/ sems can thams cad 'gro ba kun gyis mchod rten du mchod par 'os par gyur te/ mche ba dkar zhing rno ba dang ldan par gyur cig /sems can thams

262b1(phal chen): te yongs su bsngo'o/ /sems can thams cad rgyan du mas rim gro bya ba'i phyir btang ba'i sems la gnas te yongs su bsngo'o/ /sems can thog ma nas med par gtong ba'i sems la gnas te yongs su

262b3(phal chen): su bsngo'o/ /sems can thams cad la nyi ma ltar snyoms pa'i 'od gzer gyi gtang ba'i sems la gnas te yongs su bsngo'o/ /sems can thams cad la sangs rgyas kyi ye shes bsgrub pa'i phyir btang
